# COGNITIVE RADAR: Hexa-Modal Profiling & Alignment Engine

## Product Requirements Document (AI-Executable)

**Version:** 9.0.0
**Target Hardware:** NVIDIA RTX 5090 (Blackwell Architecture) - Single Device
**Architecture:** CUDA 13.1 Green Context Partitioning, Tile-Based DSP, Zero-PCIe Latency
**Core Logic:** Unified Theory of Learning (UTL) minimizing Total Loss ($J$) via Phase-Modulated Learning Dynamics ($L = f((ΔS × ΔC) ⋅ w_e ⋅ cos φ)$)
**Technology Stack:** Rust (core) + Node.js (optional WebSocket bridge)

---

## 1. System Identity & Objective

**Cognitive Radar** is a local-first cognitive alignment engine. It ingests **Semantic**, **Tone**, **Emotion**, **Style**, **Action**, and **Chronemic** data streams. It uses a **Weighted Ensemble** approach to measure the **proximity of the user's individual stream vectors** to pre-computed **North Star Reference Vectors** within each of the 5 independent embedding spaces (Semantic, Tone, Emotion, Style, Action). These North Stars are **fixed reference points derived from actual recordings** of individuals verified to match the 49 Hogshead Archetypes and VAK modalities. They serve as the immutable "rulers" for identity measurement. The system navigates a user from Entropy (Confusion) to Coherence (Understanding) using the **Cognitive Mirror Protocol**.

### 1.1 Primary Constraints

| Constraint ID | Description | Enforcement |
|:--------------|:------------|:------------|
| CONST-001 | System MUST identify user's Primary and Secondary Hogshead Archetypes AND VAK Modality using 6-stream triangulation | Mandatory classification after T > 60s OR upon Fast-Track Exit |
| CONST-002 | System operates in Safe Harbor Mode (Gamma=0.1) until T > 60s **OR** Identity Confidence > 97% (Fast-Track Exit). | **Dynamic Exit:** Safe Harbor ends immediately upon Identity Verification. |
| CONST-003 | Identity Verification MUST utilize **Hexa-Modal Fusion**. The system computes a **Weighted Composite Confidence Score** by summing the weighted, normalized similarity scores of all 6 streams (Voice, Semantic, Emotion, Style, Action, Chronemic). | Verification is ONLY successful if **Weighted Composite Confidence Score > 0.97**. Single-vector cosine similarity MUST NOT be used as the sole verification metric. |
| CONST-004 | All inference and signal processing MUST complete within 50ms (Enabled by Green Context isolation) | Enforced via timeout |
| CONST-005 | System MUST process 6 parallel streams (Semantic, Tone, Emotion, Style, Action, Chronemic) | Parallel stream processing with independent embedding spaces |
| CONST-006 | Safety Stop triggers when Valence < 0.3 AND Arousal > 0.7 | Immediate escalation protocol |
| CONST-007 | Audio MUST be normalized to -3dB and VAD-processed before identity verification | Mandatory preprocessing for 0.97 Composite Score |
| CONST-008 | Strategy pruning MUST occur post-session only, never during real-time loop | Prevents database locking and premature pruning |
| CONST-009 | System MUST load **North Star Reference Sets** (arrays containing one reference vector per embedding space) for all 49 Archetypes and VAK Modalities at startup. These act as the immutable "rulers" for identity measurement within each of the 5 independent embedding spaces. | Panic on missing **North Star reference** data |
| CONST-010 | **Native FP8 Inference.** The inference engine uses CUDA 13.1 Native FP8 Tensor Cores. Vocabulary steering (Priming) occurs via System Prompt Injection for architectural simplicity. | Rust Compiler (Architecture limitation) |

### 1.2 Core Capabilities

| Capability ID | Name | Description |
|:--------------|:-----|:------------|
| CAP-001 | Universal | Works for Debt, Sales, Therapy, Support via TOML Profile swap |
| CAP-002 | Safe | Mathematically incapable of violating defined compliance vectors (enforced by Rust type system) |
| CAP-003 | Smart | Remembers context via Linear Attention O(n) |
| CAP-004 | Fast | **< 200ms response latency** via Unified Binary Architecture |
| CAP-005 | Adaptive | Real-time archetype profiling with 60s discovery window |
| CAP-006 | Hexa-Modal Sensing | Simultaneous inference of all embedding models via **cuBLAS Grouped GEMM** on Green Context B, fusing 5 streams into a single kernel launch. |
| CAP-007 | VAK Detection | Specific profiling of Visual, Auditory, and Kinesthetic language patterns via keyword analysis and chronemic pacing |
| CAP-008 | Trust Voice DSP | Real-time output audio post-processing using **CUDA Tile IR** kernels directly in GPU memory (Context A). |
| CAP-009 | Neuroacoustic Modulation | Implements Leapable Frequency Modulation (LFM): Subliminal γ-harmonic glides (17-21 Hz) mixed at -18dB during critical closing moments to stimulate parasympathetic compliance. |
| CAP-010 | Voice Phase Coherence (VPCE) | Maintains real-time phase-locking ($\Phi > 0.85$) between synthetic voice and user speech using CUDA Tile IR phase-locked loops and micro-timing adjustments ($\pm 50ms$) to create unconscious acoustic synchrony. |
| CAP-011 | Prosodic Anticipation Graphs (PAG) | Self-learning GNN that predicts emotional trajectory 5 seconds ahead using tonal drift, breathing rhythm, and lexical entropy to enable proactive emotional management (e.g., pre-emptive empathy for rising anger). |

### 1.3 Architecture Summary

| Component | Technology | Benefit |
|:----------|:-----------|:--------|
| Core Runtime | Unified Rust Binary | Sub-microsecond IPC via Tokio channels |
| HTTP/WebSocket API | Axum | Type-safe routing, tower middleware |
| ML Inference | Candle | Native GPU inference, zero FFI overhead |
| State Machine | Rust enums/structs | Compile-time state machine validation |
| Configuration | TOML + serde | Strongly typed, fail-fast deserialization |
| Strategy Storage | RuVector GraphDatabase | `@ruvector/graph-node` for Hypergraph/Cypher storage of Intent/Strategy Nodes. Uses `createNode`, `createEdge`, and `query()` APIs. Distance metric: Cosine. |
| Identity Storage | LanceDB | Native Rust append-only storage for Voice X-Vectors (512-dim WavLM) and Ghost Replay execution holograms. |
| Reasoning Storage | AgentDB ReasoningBank | `ReasoningBank` for high-reward strategy pattern storage, `CausalMemory` for impact factors via `causal_add_edge`/`causal_query`, and `Reflexion` for near-miss episode storage. Node.js Bridge/WASM integration. |

## 2. Terminology Standardization

All domain-specific naming conventions use universal terms.

| Term ID | Universal Term | Definition | Examples |
|:--------|:---------------|:-----------|:---------|
| TERM-001 | Counterpart | The human participant | customer, patient, lead, user |
| TERM-002 | Operator | The AI managing the interaction | agent, assistant, bot |
| TERM-003 | Topic | Subject matter being aligned on | payment, appointment, issue |
| TERM-004 | Resolution | Generic successful outcome | payment collected, appointment set |
| TERM-005 | Protocol | Constraint category | HIPAA, Legal, Brand Safety |
| TERM-006 | Turbulence | High entropy, low coherence state | confusion, disagreement |
| TERM-007 | Momentum | Low entropy, high coherence state | flow, agreement |
| TERM-008 | Alignment Score | Universal success metric | 0.0 to 1.0 scalar |
| TERM-009 | Shadow Slot | Background async process for post-hoc analysis | User satisfaction analysis |
| TERM-010 | Archetype | One of 49 Hogshead personality profiles | Power-Prestige, Trust-Innovation |
| TERM-011 | CognitiveState | Unified struct from parallel hexa-modal analysis | Contains IntentID, Archetypes, VAK, Scalars |
| TERM-012 | North Star Reference Set | A pre-computed collection of 5 distinct reference vectors (one for each embedding space) derived from verified profile recordings. Each Archetype has a specific array of vectors (e.g., Semantic Vector A, Tone Vector B, etc.) that defines it. Used as the reference point to measure the user's distance and calculate Identity. | 49 Hogshead Archetype Reference Sets (each containing 5 vectors: Semantic 768-dim, Tone 512-dim, Emotion 1024-dim, Style scalar, Action 42-dim) |
| TERM-013 | Safe Harbor | Discovery phase with Gamma = 0.1 | First 60 seconds |
| TERM-014 | **Identity Lock** | Verified user state achieved when the **Weighted Composite Confidence Score** (the sum of 6 weighted stream similarities: Voice 60% + Semantic 10% + Emotion 10% + Style 10% + Action 5% + Chronemic 5%) exceeds 0.97. Triggers immediate profile hydration. | >0.97 Composite Score |
| TERM-015 | Tone Signal | Bio-signal derived from WavLM (pitch/timbre) used for identity verification and stress detection | X-Vector fingerprint, stress indicators |
| TERM-016 | **User Position Vectors** | The set of 5 individual vectors representing the user's behavior in each specific embedding space (Semantic, Tone, Emotion, Style, Action). **The user does NOT have a centroid**, as all embedding spaces differ in dimension and model. This refers to the specific 5-vector combination used for profiling. | User's Semantic Vector (768-dim), User's Tone Vector (512-dim), User's Emotion Vector (1024-dim), User's Style Score (scalar), User's Action Vector (42-dim) |
| TERM-017 | w_e | Emotional Weight calculated from Valence and Arousal scalars | Physics equation modulator |
| TERM-018 | Style Signal | Formality and complexity score derived from RoBERTa embeddings | Scalar 0.0 (informal) to 1.0 (formal) |
| TERM-019 | Action Signal | Dialog Act classification (Command/Question/Statement) derived from BERT embeddings | 42-class logit vector |
| TERM-020 | Chronemic Signal | Time-based behavioral data (Pace, Latency, Jitter) calculated by the Audio Preprocessor | 4-dimensional vector: [latency_ms, wpm, jitter_ms, overlap_ratio] |
| TERM-021 | VAK Modality | Visual, Auditory, or Kinesthetic preference detected via Semantic keywords and Chronemic pacing | Visual: "see", "look"; Auditory: "hear", "sounds"; Kinesthetic: "feel", "grasp" |
| TERM-022 | **North Star Reference Vector** | The specific vector within a Reference Set that applies to a single embedding space. E.g., The "Power Archetype Semantic Reference Vector" is the ruler for the Semantic space only. Each archetype has one reference vector per embedding space. | Power Archetype Semantic Reference Vector, Power Archetype Tone Reference Vector, Trust Archetype Emotion Reference Vector |
| TERM-023 | Teleology | The goal-seeking logic layer that maps semantic intents to business outcomes. Enables the system to pursue specific business objectives (Sales, Support, Collection) while adapting to user psychology. | "Consultative Sales Flow", "Technical Support Flow", "Debt Collection Flow" |
| TERM-025 | Milestone | A mandatory or optional checkpoint that must be semantically satisfied to progress toward the goal. Milestones are matched via semantic similarity (embedding comparison) against user utterances. | "Identity Verified", "Budget Confirmed", "Pain Points Identified", "Commitment Secured" |
| TERM-026 | Goal Vector | A dynamic scalar (0.0 to 1.0) representing distance to the final objective. 0.0 = session start, 1.0 = goal complete. Calculated as (completed_mandatory_milestones / total_mandatory_milestones). | Sales progress toward closing, Support progress toward resolution |
| TERM-027 | Constraint Node | A "Hard Gate" logic check that prevents progression until satisfied. Unlike optional milestones, Constraint Nodes MUST be completed before advancing. | "Must read legal disclaimer before closing", "Must verify identity before account access" |
| TERM-028 | **Cognitive Resonance (CRM)** | The calculated synchronization state between the Operator and Counterpart across Prosody, Semantics, and Rhythm. Defined by R(t) = (P × S × C) / σ. | R(t) > 0.82 indicates maximum receptivity ("The Close Window"). |
| TERM-029 | **Resonance Trigger** | The event fired when R(t) exceeds the configured threshold (0.82), forcing the system to switch strategy from "Discovery/Building" to "Closing". | "Close Now" signal sent to Strategy Brain. |
| TERM-030 | **Temporal Archetype Drift (TAD)** | The continuous tracking of a user's psychological movement between archetypes over time. Specifically monitors movement from "Defensive" archetypes (Mystique/Alert) toward "Receptive" archetypes (Trust/Passion). | Moving from "Skeptical" to "Trusting" over 10 turns. |
| TERM-031 | **Drift Velocity** | The rate of change in the user's distance to Receptive North Stars. A positive velocity indicates the user is warming up; negative indicates cooling off. Calculated via weighted sum of distance deltas. | +0.45 (Rapid warming), -0.1 (Slight cooling) |
| TERM-032 | **Leapable Frequency Modulation (LFM)** | A neuroacoustic modulation technique that introduces γ-harmonic glides (17-21 Hz sine sweep over 350ms) underneath the main vocal stream at -18dB. Triggered during settlement offers and closing attempts to induce parasympathetic calm and reduce resistance. |
| TERM-033 | **Voice Phase Coherence (VPCE)** | A DSP engine that aligns the phase angle of the AI's TTS output with the user's speech envelope to create unconscious rapport. |
| TERM-034 | **Phase Coherence Coefficient ($\Phi$)** | A metric (0.0 to 1.0) measuring the temporal alignment of F0 contours. Calculated as $|⟨e^{i\theta_{AI}} \times e^{-i\theta_{recipient}}⟩|$. |
| TERM-035 | **Prosodic Anticipation Graphs (PAG)** | A GNN-based predictive engine that forecasts the user's emotional state at $t+5s$ based on 500ms temporal windows. | Output: "Anger Rising (85%)" |
| TERM-036 | **Tonal Drift** | The first ($d/dt$) and second ($d^2/dt^2$) derivatives of the F0 contour, measuring the direction and acceleration of pitch changes. | Rising fast = Anxiety/Anger |
| TERM-037 | **Inter-Breath Interval (IBI)** | The time duration between detected inhalation events in the speech envelope. Shortening IBI correlates with increasing arousal/anger. | 400ms (High Arousal) vs 2500ms (Calm) |
| TERM-038 | **Lexical Entropy** | A measure of information density and word predictability. High entropy in user speech correlates with uncertainty or disengagement. | High: Stuttering, filler words, complex sentence structures |
| TERM-039 | **PAG State** | The predicted future emotional state: `AngerRising`, `Disengaging`, `Receptive`, or `PeakReceptive`. | Triggers proactive strategy overrides |

|:--------------|:-----|:------------|

| **SCOPE-003** | **Visual Embedding Space** | 3D UMAP/t-SNE visualization of User trajectories relative to fixed North Star Profile Coordinates. |

### 2.2 Non-Scope

The following capabilities are explicitly excluded from this system:

| Exclusion ID | Category | Description |
|:-------------|:---------|:------------|
| NONSCOPE-001 | Multi-Tenancy | System supports single active session only. No concurrent user sessions. |
| NONSCOPE-002 | Cloud Authentication | No external authentication mechanisms (OAuth, SAML, SSO). Local system access only. |
| NONSCOPE-003 | Long-Term Storage | No S3, GCS, Azure Blob, or other cloud storage integration. Local disk only. |
| NONSCOPE-004 | Horizontal Scaling | No load balancing, clustering, or multi-node deployment. Single node architecture only. |
| NONSCOPE-005 | User Management | No user accounts, roles, or permissions system. Single operator assumed. |
| NONSCOPE-006 | API Gateway | No public API exposure. Internal channel communication only. |

## 3. Neural Architecture Specifications

### 3.1 Model Registry & Dimensions

**REQ-MODELS-001: Model Specifications & Paths**

The system MUST load the following 5 models and implement the Chronemic Logic stream. All vector operations MUST strictly adhere to the defined Output Dimensions.

| Stream | Input | Model Name | Path | Output Dim | Purpose |
|:-------|:------|:-----------|:-----|:-----------|:--------|
| **A (Semantic)** | Text | Nomic Embed Text v1 | `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/nomic-embed-text-v1` | 768 | Topic/Intent Vector for StrategyGraph matching |
| **B (Tone/ID)** | Audio | WavLM Base Plus SV | `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/wavlm-base-plus-sv` | 512 | Identity (X-Vector) & Tonal Quality |
| **C (Emotion)** | Audio | Wav2Vec2 Emotion | `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/wav2vec2-emotion` | 1024 | Arousal/Valence scalars + Baseline Vector for LanceDB |
| **D (Style)** | Text | RoBERTa Formality | `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/roberta-formality` | 1 (Scalar) | Formality Score (0.0-1.0) |
| **E (Action)** | Text | BERT Dialog Act | `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/bert-dialog-act` | 42 | Dialog Act Logits (Command/Question/Statement/etc) |
| **F (Chronemic)** | Metadata | Logic-Based | N/A | 4 | [latency_ms, wpm, jitter_ms, overlap_ratio] |
| **G (PAG)** | Streams A, B, F | RuVector GNN (Logic) | N/A | 4 (Probabilities) | Future Emotional State Prediction (Anger, Disengaging, Receptive, Peak) |
| **Brain** | Text | Qwen 3 14B FP8 | `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/qwen3-14b-fp8-instruct.safetensors` | N/A | Response Generation (Dual-Mode: Instruct/Thinking) |

**REQ-MODELS-002: Compile-Time Dimension Constants**

```rust
/// CRITICAL: These constants define buffer sizes for the Rust compiler.
/// Do NOT modify without updating all dependent code.
pub mod dimensions {
    pub const SEMANTIC_DIM: usize = 768;    // Nomic Embed Text v1
    pub const IDENTITY_DIM: usize = 512;    // WavLM Base Plus SV
    pub const EMOTION_DIM: usize = 1024;    // Wav2Vec2 Emotion
    pub const STYLE_DIM: usize = 1;         // RoBERTa Formality (scalar)
    pub const ACTION_DIM: usize = 42;       // BERT Dialog Act (42-class logits)
    pub const CHRONEMIC_DIM: usize = 4;     // [latency_ms, wpm, jitter_ms, overlap_ratio]
}
```

**REQ-MODELS-003: Model Loading Specification**

```rust
use candle_core::{Device, DType};
use std::path::Path;
use crate::dimensions::{SEMANTIC_DIM, EMOTION_DIM, IDENTITY_DIM, ACTION_DIM};

pub struct ModelPaths {
    pub nomic: &'static str,
    pub wavlm: &'static str,
    pub gender_classifier: &'static str,
    pub wav2vec: &'static str,
    pub roberta: &'static str,
    pub bert: &'static str,
    pub qwen: &'static str,
}

pub const MODEL_PATHS: ModelPaths = ModelPaths {
    nomic: "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/nomic-embed-text-v1",
    wavlm: "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/wavlm-base-plus-sv",
    gender_classifier: "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/gender-classifier-linear",
    wav2vec: "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/wav2vec2-emotion",
    roberta: "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/roberta-formality",
    bert: "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/bert-dialog-act",
    qwen: "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/qwen3-14b-fp8-instruct.safetensors",
};

pub struct ModelRegistry {
    pub semantic_model: NomicEmbedder,          // Stream A: Output [f32; 768]
    pub identity_model: WavLMSpeakerVerify,     // Stream B: Output [f32; 512]
    pub emotion_model: Wav2Vec2Emotion,         // Stream C: Output EmotionOutput
    pub style_model: RoBERTaFormality,          // Stream D: Output f32 (scalar 0.0-1.0)
    pub action_model: BERTDialogAct,            // Stream E: Output [f32; 42] (logits)
    pub brain_model: QwenLLM,                   // Text generation (FP8 Dual-Mode: Instruct/Thinking)
    /// Gender classifier for detecting user gender from voice samples
    /// Used to select appropriate gender-specific reference vectors (tone_male/tone_female, emotion_male/emotion_female)
    pub gender_classifier: GenderClassifier,
    /// Priming Controller for vocabulary steering via System Prompt Injection
    pub priming_controller: PrimingController,
    /// CUDA 13.1 Green Context handles for GPU partitioning
    pub green_contexts: GreenContexts,
}

/// Lightweight gender classification head running on top of WavLM embeddings
///
/// The GenderClassifier uses the same X-Vector (512-dim) extracted by WavLM
/// to classify the speaker's gender. This enables runtime selection of
/// gender-specific North Star reference vectors for Tone and Emotion streams.
///
/// **Architecture:**
/// - Input: 512-dim X-Vector from WavLM
/// - Hidden: Single linear layer (512 -> 64) with ReLU
/// - Output: Linear layer (64 -> 2) with softmax for Male/Female classification
///
/// **Training Data:**
/// - VoxCeleb2 gender labels
/// - Accuracy: >98% on held-out test set
pub struct GenderClassifier {
    /// Linear layer weights (512 x 64)
    hidden_weights: [[f32; 64]; 512],
    /// Hidden bias (64)
    hidden_bias: [f32; 64],
    /// Output layer weights (64 x 2)
    output_weights: [[f32; 2]; 64],
    /// Output bias (2)
    output_bias: [f32; 2],
}

impl GenderClassifier {
    /// Predict gender from WavLM X-Vector embedding
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    /// * `x_vector` - 512-dimensional speaker embedding from WavLM
    ///
    /// # Returns
    /// * `Gender::Male` or `Gender::Female` based on classification
    pub fn predict(&self, x_vector: &[f32; 512]) -> Gender {
        // Forward pass through hidden layer
        let mut hidden = [0.0f32; 64];
        for i in 0..64 {
            let mut sum = self.hidden_bias[i];
            for j in 0..512 {
                sum += x_vector[j] * self.hidden_weights[j][i];
            }
            // ReLU activation
            hidden[i] = sum.max(0.0);
        }

        // Forward pass through output layer
        let mut output = [0.0f32; 2];
        for i in 0..2 {
            let mut sum = self.output_bias[i];
            for j in 0..64 {
                sum += hidden[j] * self.output_weights[j][i];
            }
            output[i] = sum;
        }

        // Softmax and argmax
        let exp_0 = output[0].exp();
        let exp_1 = output[1].exp();
        let prob_male = exp_0 / (exp_0 + exp_1);

        if prob_male > 0.5 {
            Gender::Male
        } else {
            Gender::Female
        }
    }

    /// Get confidence score for the predicted gender
    ///
    /// # Returns
    /// * Confidence score (0.5 to 1.0) for the predicted gender
    pub fn predict_with_confidence(&self, x_vector: &[f32; 512]) -> (Gender, f32) {
        // Forward pass (same as predict)
        let mut hidden = [0.0f32; 64];
        for i in 0..64 {
            let mut sum = self.hidden_bias[i];
            for j in 0..512 {
                sum += x_vector[j] * self.hidden_weights[j][i];
            }
            hidden[i] = sum.max(0.0);
        }

        let mut output = [0.0f32; 2];
        for i in 0..2 {
            let mut sum = self.output_bias[i];
            for j in 0..64 {
                sum += hidden[j] * self.output_weights[j][i];
            }
            output[i] = sum;
        }

        let exp_0 = output[0].exp();
        let exp_1 = output[1].exp();
        let prob_male = exp_0 / (exp_0 + exp_1);

        if prob_male > 0.5 {
            (Gender::Male, prob_male)
        } else {
            (Gender::Female, 1.0 - prob_male)
        }
    }

    /// Load GenderClassifier weights from file
    pub fn load(path: &std::path::Path) -> Result<Self, ModelError> {
        // Load weights from binary file
        todo!("Load gender classifier weights from {}", path.display())
    }
}

/// Gender classification for audio stream processing
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
pub enum Gender {
    Male,
    Female,
}

/// CUDA 13.1 Green Context Handles for RTX 5090 Blackwell Architecture
/// Provides spatial partitioning of the GPU with guaranteed QoS per partition.
pub struct GreenContexts {
    /// Context A (10% SMs): Audio/DSP Reflex Loop - Dedicated to WavLM, Audio Preprocessing, Trust Voice DSP
    /// This partition has highest priority and never waits for other contexts.
    pub context_a_reflex: CudaContext,
    /// Context B (30% SMs): Semantic Loop - Dedicated to Grouped GEMM for Nomic, RoBERTa, BERT, Wav2Vec2
    /// Runs cuBLAS Grouped GEMM to fuse 5 stream inferences into single kernel launch.
    pub context_b_semantic: CudaContext,
    /// Context C (60% SMs): Deep Thought Loop - Dedicated to Qwen 3 14B FP8 inference and Prescience MCTS
    /// Leverages FP8 Tensor Cores for 2x throughput with medical-grade simulation depth.
    pub context_c_deep: CudaContext,
}

/// Output from Wav2Vec2 Emotion model
///
/// CRITICAL DUAL-PURPOSE:
/// - pooled_embedding (1024-dim): Stored in LanceDB for long-term emotional baseline tracking
/// - Scalars (arousal, valence): Used by Physics Engine to calculate w_e (Emotional Weight)
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct EmotionOutput {
    /// Pooled hidden states for history storage in LanceDB (1024-dim)
    pub pooled_embedding: [f32; EMOTION_DIM],
    /// Arousal scalar (0.0 to 1.0)
    pub arousal: f32,
    /// Dominance scalar (0.0 to 1.0)
    pub dominance: f32,
    /// Valence scalar (0.0 to 1.0)
    pub valence: f32,
}

/// Output from RoBERTa Formality model
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct StyleOutput {
    /// Formality score (0.0 = informal/innovation, 1.0 = formal/prestige)
    pub formality: f32,
}

/// Output from BERT Dialog Act model
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ActionOutput {
    /// 42-class logit vector for dialog act classification
    pub logits: [f32; ACTION_DIM],
}

/// Chronemic signal calculated by Audio Preprocessor (not a model)
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ChronemicOutput {
    /// Response latency in milliseconds
    pub latency_ms: f32,
    /// Words per minute speaking rate
    pub wpm: f32,
    /// Timing jitter (variance) in milliseconds
    pub jitter_ms: f32,
    /// Overlap ratio (interruption frequency)
    pub overlap_ratio: f32,
    /// Standard deviation of syllable timing (high variance = emotional instability)
    /// Used for PAG input
    pub speech_rate_variance: f32,
}

impl ModelRegistry {
    pub fn load(device: &Device) -> Result<Self, ModelError> {
        // Validate all model paths exist before loading
        let required_paths = [
            MODEL_PATHS.nomic,
            MODEL_PATHS.wavlm,
            MODEL_PATHS.gender_classifier,
            MODEL_PATHS.wav2vec,
            MODEL_PATHS.roberta,
            MODEL_PATHS.bert,
            MODEL_PATHS.qwen,
        ];

        for path in required_paths {
            if !Path::new(path).exists() {
                panic!("CRITICAL: Required model not found at path: {}", path);
            }
        }

        Ok(Self {
            semantic_model: NomicEmbedder::load(MODEL_PATHS.nomic, device)?,
            identity_model: WavLMSpeakerVerify::load(MODEL_PATHS.wavlm, device)?,
            gender_classifier: GenderClassifier::load(Path::new(MODEL_PATHS.gender_classifier))?,
            emotion_model: Wav2Vec2Emotion::load(MODEL_PATHS.wav2vec, device)?,
            style_model: RoBERTaFormality::load(MODEL_PATHS.roberta, device)?,
            action_model: BERTDialogAct::load(MODEL_PATHS.bert, device)?,
            brain_model: QwenLLM::load(MODEL_PATHS.qwen, device, DType::FP8)?,
        })
    }
}
```

**REQ-MODELS-004: Nomic Embedding Prefixes**

The Nomic Embed Text v1 model requires specific prefixes to function correctly. The system MUST prepend the following prefixes before embedding:

| Context | Prefix | Example |
|:--------|:-------|:--------|
| User Transcript (Query) | `search_query: ` | `search_query: I need help with my payment` |
| Strategy/Intent Node (Storage) | `search_document: ` | `search_document: Payment assistance strategy` |

```rust
/// CRITICAL: Nomic embedding prefix constants
pub mod nomic_prefixes {
    pub const QUERY_PREFIX: &str = "search_query: ";
    pub const DOCUMENT_PREFIX: &str = "search_document: ";
}

impl NomicEmbedder {
    /// Embed user transcript with query prefix
    ///
    /// CRITICAL: Always use this method for user input
    pub fn embed_query(&self, transcript: &str) -> Result<[f32; 768], EmbedError> {
        let prefixed = format!("{}{}", nomic_prefixes::QUERY_PREFIX, transcript);
        self.embed_raw(&prefixed)
    }

    /// Embed strategy/intent for storage with document prefix
    ///
    /// CRITICAL: Always use this method when storing to RuVector
    pub fn embed_document(&self, content: &str) -> Result<[f32; 768], EmbedError> {
        let prefixed = format!("{}{}", nomic_prefixes::DOCUMENT_PREFIX, content);
        self.embed_raw(&prefixed)
    }

    /// Raw embedding without prefix - internal use only
    fn embed_raw(&self, text: &str) -> Result<[f32; 768], EmbedError> {
        // Model inference implementation
        todo!()
    }
}

/// Qwen 3 14B FP8 Inference Mode
///
/// Qwen 3 supports dual-mode inference:
/// - Instruct Mode: Standard instruction following without internal reasoning tokens.
///   Used during real-time loop for <50ms response compliance.
/// - Thinking Mode: Chain-of-Thought reasoning with internal thought tokens.
///   Used during offline Oneiric Engine simulations for deep reasoning.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub enum InferenceMode {
    /// Non-Thinking Mode: Strict instruction following, no CoT tokens.
    /// Use for real-time loop to minimize latency.
    Instruct,
    /// Thinking Mode: Chain-of-Thought reasoning enabled.
    /// Use for offline Oneiric Engine dreaming simulations.
    Thinking,
}

/// QwenLLM generation methods
///
/// CRITICAL: Candle/GGUF does not support logit_bias (CONST-010).
/// Vocabulary steering is implemented via Prompt Injection.
///
/// Qwen 3 14B FP8 supports dual-mode inference:
/// - InferenceMode::Instruct - Real-time loop (low latency, no CoT)
/// - InferenceMode::Thinking - Oneiric Engine (deep reasoning with CoT)
impl QwenLLM {
    /// Generate response with priming support via Prompt Injection
    ///
    /// CONST-010 COMPLIANCE: Candle with quantised GGUF models does not support
    /// logit manipulation. Priming is achieved by injecting guidance into the
    /// system prompt rather than biasing token logits.
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    /// * `system_context` - Base system prompt with cognitive state
    /// * `user_input` - User's transcript
    /// * `priming_injection` - Priming guidance string to inject (may be empty)
    /// * `max_tokens` - Maximum tokens to generate
    /// * `mode` - Inference mode (Instruct for real-time, Thinking for offline)
    ///
    /// # Returns
    /// Generated response with text and metadata
    pub async fn generate_with_priming(
        &self,
        system_context: &str,
        user_input: &str,
        priming_injection: &str,
        max_tokens: usize,
        mode: InferenceMode,
    ) -> Result<GenerationResult, InferenceError> {
        // Inject priming guidance into system prompt if provided
        let enhanced_system = if priming_injection.is_empty() {
            system_context.to_string()
        } else {
            format!("{}\n\n{}", system_context, priming_injection)
        };

        self.generate(&enhanced_system, user_input, max_tokens, mode).await
    }

    /// Standard generation with mode selection (internal use)
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    /// * `system_context` - System prompt with cognitive state
    /// * `user_input` - User's transcript
    /// * `max_tokens` - Maximum tokens to generate
    /// * `mode` - Inference mode:
    ///   - InferenceMode::Instruct: No internal reasoning tokens (fast)
    ///   - InferenceMode::Thinking: CoT reasoning tokens enabled (deep)
    pub async fn generate(
        &self,
        system_context: &str,
        user_input: &str,
        max_tokens: usize,
        mode: InferenceMode,
    ) -> Result<GenerationResult, InferenceError> {
        // Candle FP8 inference implementation
        // Mode selection determines whether to enable thinking tokens
        todo!()
    }
}
```

## 4. Data Storage Specifications

The system uses three distinct storage engines, each with a specialized role. This Parallel Stream Architecture ensures vectors of different dimensions are NEVER concatenated or mathematically combined—they are searched in their respective databases independently and fused only at the `CognitiveState` struct level.

**CRITICAL ARCHITECTURE RULE**: Vectors from different models (768-dim Nomic, 512-dim WavLM, 1024-dim Wav2Vec2) exist in incompatible vector spaces. The system MUST NOT:
- Concatenate vectors of different dimensions
- Perform mathematical operations between vectors from different models
- Store vectors of different dimensions in the same database table

### 4.1 RuVector: The Strategy Brain

**REQ-DATA-001: RuVector GraphDatabase Implementation**

The `StrategyBrain` MUST utilize the `GraphDatabase` class from `@ruvector/graph-node`. It MUST NOT use the base `VectorDB` class, as the system relies on Cypher relationships (`REQUIRES`, `LEADS_TO`, `ADVANCES`, `RESOLVES`).

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Content** | Semantic Vectors (768-dim) mapped to Intents and Strategies |
| **Purpose** | "What worked?" (Winning Strategies) - Graph-based strategy navigation for reaching target goals |
| **Constraint** | Does NOT store Identity vectors or Emotion vectors |
| **Required Class** | `GraphDatabase` from `@ruvector/graph-node` (NOT `VectorDB` from `@ruvector/core`) |
| **Distance Metric** | `distanceMetric: 'Cosine'` MUST be set in `GraphDatabase` constructor |
| **Query Language** | Cypher (via `db.query()`) |
| **Node Creation** | Use `db.createNode({})` for GoalNodes, MilestoneNodes, Strategy nodes |
| **Edge Creation** | Use `db.createEdge({})` for REQUIRES, LEADS_TO, ADVANCES, RESOLVES relationships |
| **Vector Storage** | Use `db.storeVector()` for semantic embeddings |
| **Vector Search** | Use `db.vectorSearch()` with HNSW indexing |

**REQ-DATA-002: Strategy Graph Schema**

The Strategy Graph uses a goal-oriented structure that maps business objectives to conversational strategies. This enables the system to pursue specific goals (Sales, Support, Collection) while adapting to user psychology.

| Node Type | Description | Fields |
|:----------|:------------|:-------|
| `GoalNode` | The ultimate objective of the session. Defines the business outcome being pursued. | `id: String`, `name: String`, `type: GoalType` (SALES, SUPPORT, COLLECTION), `description: String` |
| `MilestoneNode` | A mandatory or optional checkpoint in the goal progression. Matched via semantic similarity. | `id: String`, `description: String`, `completion_condition: [f32; 768]` (semantic embedding), `is_mandatory: bool`, `order_index: u32` |
| `Strategy` | A conversation approach optimized for a specific archetype and VAK modality. | `id: String`, `embedding: [f32; 768]`, `description: String`, `target_archetype: ArchetypeId`, `vak_modality: VakType`, `created_at: Timestamp` |
| `Outcome` | Result of strategy application, used for reinforcement learning. | `id: String`, `type: OutcomeType` (WIN, FAIL), `coherence_gain: f32`, `timestamp: Timestamp` |

| Edge Type | From | To | Weight/Fields |
|:----------|:-----|:---|:--------------|
| `LEADS_TO` | Strategy | Outcome | `coherence_gain: f32` - The coherence improvement when this strategy leads to this outcome |
| `ADVANCES` | Strategy | MilestoneNode | `success_probability: f32` - Probability (0.0-1.0) that this strategy advances the milestone |
| `REQUIRES` | GoalNode | MilestoneNode | `order_index: u32` - The sequence order of this milestone within the goal |
| `RESOLVES` | Strategy | GoalNode | `success_rate: f32` - Historical success rate of this strategy achieving the goal |

**REQ-DATA-002f: PAG Temporal Graph Schema**

The PAG utilizes RuVector to store temporal nodes representing 500ms windows of conversation.

| Node Type | Description | Fields |
|:----------|:------------|:-------|
| `PAGNode` | Represents a 500ms temporal window | `id: String`, `tonal_drift: f32`, `ibi: f32`, `lexical_entropy: f32`, `rate_variance: f32`, `timestamp: i64` |

| Edge Type | From | To | Weight |
|:----------|:-----|:---|:-------|
| `NEXT_WINDOW` | PAGNode(t) | PAGNode(t+1) | 1.0 (Sequential) |
| `SKIP_3S` | PAGNode(t) | PAGNode(t+6) | Correlation strength |
| `SKIP_5S` | PAGNode(t) | PAGNode(t+10) | Correlation strength |

**GoalType Enumeration:**

```rust
/// The type of business objective being pursued
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub enum GoalType {
    /// Consultative sales - building rapport and closing deals
    Sales,
    /// Technical support - diagnosing and resolving issues
    Support,
    /// Debt collection - negotiating payment arrangements
    Collection,
}
```

**MilestoneNode Field Definitions:**

| Field | Type | Description |
|:------|:-----|:------------|
| `id` | `String` | Unique identifier (e.g., "m1", "m2") |
| `description` | `String` | Human-readable description of the milestone (e.g., "Identify Pain Points") |
| `completion_condition` | `[f32; 768]` | Nomic semantic embedding of the milestone description. Used to match user utterances via cosine similarity. |
| `is_mandatory` | `bool` | If true, this milestone MUST be completed before goal can be achieved. If false, it's optional but improves success rate. |
| `order_index` | `u32` | Suggested sequence order. Lower numbers should be attempted first. |

**REQ-DATA-002d: Teleological Graph Queries**

```rust
impl StrategyBrain {
    /// Predict future emotional state using PAG GNN propagation

        tonal_drift: f32,
        ibi: f32,
        lexical_entropy: f32,
        rate_variance: f32,
    ) -> Result<PagPrediction, RuVectorError> {

        // 3. Return probabilities for t+5s state
        todo!("Implement GNN forward pass")

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct PagPrediction {
    pub anger_rising_prob: f32,
    pub disengaging_prob: f32,
    pub receptive_prob: f32,
    pub peak_receptive_prob: f32,
    pub predicted_state: PagState,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub enum PagState {
    AngerRising,
    Disengaging,
    Receptive,
    PeakReceptive,
    Neutral,
}

impl StrategyBrain {
    /// Load the active goal and its milestones from RuVector
    ///
    /// Called at session start to initialize the Teleological Engine state.
    pub async fn load_goal_graph(
        &self,
        goal_type: GoalType,
    ) -> Result<GoalGraph, RuVectorError> {
        // Query for the GoalNode
        let goal: GoalRecord = self.db.query(&format!(
            "MATCH (g:GoalNode {{type: '{}'}})
             RETURN g.id AS id, g.name AS name, g.type AS goal_type, g.description AS description",
            goal_type
        )).await?.into_iter().next()
            .ok_or(RuVectorError::GoalNotFound(goal_type))?;

        // Query for all MilestoneNodes linked to this goal, ordered by sequence
        let milestones: Vec<MilestoneRecord> = self.db.query(&format!(
            "MATCH (g:GoalNode {{id: '{}'}})-[r:REQUIRES]->(m:MilestoneNode)
             RETURN m.id AS id, m.description AS description, m.is_mandatory AS is_mandatory, r.order_index AS order_index
             ORDER BY r.order_index ASC",
            goal.id
        )).await?;

        // Load embeddings for each milestone
        let mut milestone_nodes = Vec::new();
        for m in milestones {
            let embedding = self.get_vector(&m.id).await?;
            milestone_nodes.push(MilestoneNode {
                id: m.id,
                description: m.description,
                completion_condition: embedding,
                is_mandatory: m.is_mandatory,
                order_index: m.order_index,
            });
        }

        Ok(GoalGraph {
            goal_id: goal.id,
            goal_name: goal.name,
            goal_type,
            milestones: milestone_nodes,
        })
    }

    /// Check if user utterance semantically matches a milestone
    ///
    /// Returns the milestone ID and similarity score if match exceeds threshold.
    pub async fn check_milestone_completion(
        &self,
        user_embedding: &[f32; 768],
        milestone: &MilestoneNode,
        completion_threshold: f32,
    ) -> Option<(String, f32)> {
        let similarity = cosine_similarity_768(user_embedding, &milestone.completion_condition);

        if similarity >= completion_threshold {
            Some((milestone.id.clone(), similarity))
        } else {
            None
        }
    }

    /// Find strategies that advance a specific milestone
    ///
    /// Returns strategies sorted by success probability for this milestone.
    pub async fn find_strategies_for_milestone(
        &self,
        milestone_id: &str,
        target_archetype: ArchetypeId,
        vak_modality: VakType,
    ) -> Result<Vec<StrategyResult>, RuVectorError> {
        let strategies: Vec<StrategyRecord> = self.db.query(&format!(
            "MATCH (s:Strategy)-[r:ADVANCES]->(m:MilestoneNode {{id: '{}'}})
             WHERE s.target_archetype = '{}' AND s.vak_modality = '{}'
             RETURN s.id AS id, s.description AS description, r.success_probability AS success_prob
             ORDER BY r.success_probability DESC
             LIMIT 5",
            milestone_id, target_archetype, vak_modality
        )).await?;

        let mut results = Vec::new();
        for s in strategies {
            let embedding = self.get_vector(&s.id).await?;
            results.push(StrategyResult {
                strategy_id: s.id,
                description: s.description,
                coherence_gain: s.success_prob,
                embedding,
                target_archetype,
                vak_modality,
            });
        }

        Ok(results)
    }
}

/// The loaded goal graph with all milestones
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct GoalGraph {
    pub goal_id: String,
    pub goal_name: String,
    pub goal_type: GoalType,
    pub milestones: Vec<MilestoneNode>,
}

/// A milestone node with its completion condition embedding
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct MilestoneNode {
    pub id: String,
    pub description: String,
    pub completion_condition: [f32; 768],
    pub is_mandatory: bool,
    pub order_index: u32,
}

/// RuVector GraphDatabase createNode() request structure
///
/// This struct maps directly to the RuVector `@ruvector/graph-node` createNode API.
/// Reference: RuVector GraphDatabase API `db.createNode({ id, embedding, labels, properties })`
///
/// CRITICAL: The `labels` field is an array of strings that maps to Cypher node labels.
/// Example: labels: ["GoalNode"] enables queries like `MATCH (n:GoalNode) RETURN n`
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct CreateNodeRequest {
    /// Unique identifier for this node
    pub id: String,
    /// Embedding vector for semantic search (768-dim for Nomic compatibility)
    pub embedding: Vec<f32>,
    /// Cypher node labels (e.g., ["GoalNode"], ["MilestoneNode"])
    /// CRITICAL: RuVector requires labels array for Cypher type matching
    pub labels: Vec<String>,
    /// Key-value properties stored on the node
    pub properties: HashMap<String, String>,
}

/// RuVector GraphDatabase createEdge() request structure
///
/// This struct maps directly to the RuVector `@ruvector/graph-node` createEdge API.
/// Reference: RuVector GraphDatabase API `db.createEdge({ from, to, description, embedding, confidence, metadata })`
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct CreateEdgeRequest {
    /// Source node ID
    pub from: String,
    /// Target node ID
    pub to: String,
    /// Edge type/description (e.g., "REQUIRES", "LEADS_TO", "ADVANCES")
    pub description: String,
    /// Optional embedding for edge semantic search
    pub embedding: Option<Vec<f32>>,
    /// Confidence score (0.0-1.0)
    pub confidence: Option<f32>,
    /// Additional metadata
    pub metadata: Option<HashMap<String, String>>,
}
```

**REQ-DATA-002e: Teleology Bootloader (Configuration Ingestion)**

At system startup, the `StrategyBrain` MUST read the `[teleology]` section from `config/cognitive_physics.toml` and ensure the corresponding `GoalNode` and `MilestoneNode` entities exist in RuVector. This synchronization ensures the Graph Database always matches the business rules defined in TOML configuration.

**Implementation Mandate (RuVector GraphDatabase APIs):**
1. Use `db.createNode({})` for GoalNodes and MilestoneNodes (NOT raw Cypher strings for creation)
2. Use `db.createEdge({})` for REQUIRES relationships (NOT raw Cypher strings for edge creation)
3. Use `db.query()` ONLY for retrieval operations and complex traversals
4. Ensure `distanceMetric` is set to `'Cosine'` in `GraphDatabase` constructor

| Step | Action | RuVector API Call |
|:-----|:-------|:------------------|
| 1 | Parse TOML | N/A (Rust serde deserialization) |
| 2 | Embed Goal | `nomic.embed_document(&goal.description)` |
| 3 | Create GoalNode | `db.createNode({ type: 'GoalNode', id, name, description, goal_type })` |
| 4 | Store Goal Vector | `db.storeVector(goal_id, goal_embedding)` |
| 5 | Embed Milestones | `nomic.embed_document(&milestone.description)` for each |
| 6 | Create MilestoneNodes | `db.createNode({ type: 'MilestoneNode', id, description, is_mandatory, order_index })` |
| 7 | Store Milestone Vectors | `db.storeVector(milestone_id, milestone_embedding)` |
| 8 | Link Goal → Milestones | `db.createEdge({ from: goal_id, to: milestone_id, type: 'REQUIRES', order_index })` |

```rust
/// Teleology configuration section from cognitive_physics.toml
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize)]
pub struct TeleologyConfig {
    /// The type of goal being pursued (Sales, Support, Collection)
    pub active_goal_mode: GoalType,
    /// The active goal definition
    pub active_goal: GoalDefinition,
}

/// Goal definition from TOML configuration
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize)]
pub struct GoalDefinition {
    /// Unique identifier for this goal
    pub id: String,
    /// Human-readable goal name
    pub name: String,
    /// Full description (used for embedding generation)
    pub description: String,
    /// Ordered list of milestones for this goal
    pub milestones: Vec<MilestoneDefinition>,
}

/// Milestone definition from TOML configuration
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize)]
pub struct MilestoneDefinition {
    /// Unique identifier for this milestone
    pub id: String,
    /// Description of what constitutes completion (used for embedding generation)
    pub description: String,
    /// Whether this milestone must be completed for goal success
    pub mandatory: bool,
    /// Suggested sequence order (lower = earlier)
    pub order_index: u32,
}

impl StrategyBrain {
    /// Sync TOML Teleology Config into RuVector Graph
    ///
    /// Called at system startup. Uses RuVector GraphDatabase APIs for node/edge creation.
    ///
    /// CRITICAL: This function MUST be called before any session processing begins.
    /// It ensures the RuVector graph contains all GoalNodes and MilestoneNodes
    /// defined in the configuration file.
    ///
    /// IMPLEMENTATION MANDATE:
    /// - Use `db.createNode({})` for node creation (NOT raw Cypher MERGE)
    /// - Use `db.createEdge({})` for edge creation (NOT raw Cypher CREATE)
    /// - Use `db.storeVector()` for embedding storage
    /// - Use `db.query()` ONLY for retrieval operations
    ///
    /// Parameters:
    /// - `config`: The parsed TeleologyConfig from cognitive_physics.toml
    /// - `nomic`: Reference to the Nomic embedding model for semantic vectorization
    ///
    /// Returns: Ok(()) on success, RuVectorError if database operations fail
    pub async fn ingest_teleology_config(
        &self,
        config: &TeleologyConfig,
        nomic: &NomicEmbedder,
    ) -> Result<(), RuVectorError> {
        // 1. Generate embedding for the Goal description
        let goal_embedding = nomic.embed_document(&config.active_goal.description)?;

        // 2. Create GoalNode using RuVector GraphDatabase createNode API
        // RuVector requires 'labels' array for Cypher node type matching (e.g., MATCH (n:GoalNode))
        // This is an upsert operation - creates or updates the node
        self.db.create_node(CreateNodeRequest {
            id: config.active_goal.id.clone(),
            embedding: goal_embedding.clone(),
            labels: vec!["GoalNode".to_string()],
            properties: hashmap! {
                "name".to_string() => config.active_goal.name.clone(),
                "description".to_string() => config.active_goal.description.clone(),
                "goal_type".to_string() => config.active_goal_mode.to_string(),
            },
        }).await?;

        // 3. Store the goal's semantic embedding vector
        self.db.store_vector(&config.active_goal.id, &goal_embedding).await?;

        // 4. Create MilestoneNodes for each milestone in the goal
        for milestone in &config.active_goal.milestones {
            // Generate embedding for the milestone description
            // This is the "completion_condition" used for semantic matching
            let milestone_embedding = nomic.embed_document(&milestone.description)?;

            // Create MilestoneNode using RuVector GraphDatabase createNode API
            // RuVector requires 'labels' array for Cypher node type matching (e.g., MATCH (m:MilestoneNode))
            self.db.create_node(CreateNodeRequest {
                id: milestone.id.clone(),
                embedding: milestone_embedding.clone(),
                labels: vec!["MilestoneNode".to_string()],
                properties: hashmap! {
                    "description".to_string() => milestone.description.clone(),
                    "is_mandatory".to_string() => milestone.mandatory.to_string(),
                    "order_index".to_string() => milestone.order_index.to_string(),
                },
            }).await?;

            // Store the milestone's semantic embedding vector
            self.db.store_vector(&milestone.id, &milestone_embedding).await?;

            // 5. Create REQUIRES edge using RuVector GraphDatabase createEdge API
            // Reference: RuVector API `db.createEdge({ from, to, description, embedding, confidence, metadata })`
            self.db.create_edge(CreateEdgeRequest {
                from: config.active_goal.id.clone(),
                to: milestone.id.clone(),
                description: "REQUIRES".to_string(),
                embedding: None, // No semantic embedding needed for structural edges
                confidence: Some(1.0), // Structural edges have full confidence
                metadata: Some(hashmap! {
                    "order_index".to_string() => milestone.order_index.to_string(),
                }),
            }).await?;
        }

        Ok(())
    }

    /// Perform vector search in RuVector
    ///
    /// Generic vector search with optional metadata filter.
    /// Used for both strategy retrieval and semantic matching.
    pub async fn vector_search(
        &self,
        embedding: &[f32; 768],
        limit: usize,
        filter: Option<&str>,
    ) -> Result<Vec<StrategyResult>, RuVectorError> {
        let results = self.db.vector_search(embedding, limit, filter).await?;

        let mut strategies = Vec::new();
        for record in results {
            let strategy_embedding = self.get_vector(&record.id).await?;
            strategies.push(StrategyResult {
                strategy_id: record.id,
                description: record.description,
                coherence_gain: record.similarity_score,
                embedding: strategy_embedding,
                target_archetype: record.target_archetype.unwrap_or_default(),
                vak_modality: record.vak_modality.unwrap_or_default(),
            });
        }

        Ok(strategies)
    }
}
```

**Strategy Node Field Definitions:**

| Field | Type | Description |
|:------|:-----|:------------|
| `target_archetype` | `ArchetypeId` | The archetype this strategy is optimized for (e.g., "Power", "Trust", "Influence") |
| `vak_modality` | `VakType` | The VAK modality this strategy targets (Visual, Auditory, Kinesthetic) |

**REQ-DATA-002a: Strategy Filtering by Profile**

When querying strategies from RuVector, the system MUST filter by the user's detected archetype and VAK modality. A strategy optimized for a "Power" archetype (Direct/Fast communication style) will fail for a "Trust" archetype (Warm/Slow communication style).

**REQ-DATA-002b: Strategy Injection (Frontend)**

The system MUST support manual strategy injection via the Frontend "Strategy Architect". This injects a conversational Strategy to guide the user toward a goal; it does NOT modify the fixed North Star coordinates used for identity measurement.

| Step | Action | Details |
|:-----|:-------|:--------|
| **Input** | Natural Language | Operator types a strategy description (e.g., "Use humor to diffuse tension") |
| **Process** | Embedding Generation | Generate 768-dim vector via Nomic embedding model |
| **Action** | Graph Node Creation | Create `Strategy` node, link to nearest `IntentNode` with `origin: HUMAN_INJECTED` |

**REQ-DATA-002c: Fractal Ontology (Self-Healing Graph)**

If the system detects high internal coherence but low intent mapping (the user makes sense but is off-script), it MUST create a Temporary Bridge Node in RuVector.

| Condition | Threshold | Action |
|:----------|:----------|:-------|
| Semantic Similarity | < Intent Match Threshold | Trigger bridge creation |
| Coherence | > Coherence Threshold | User input is valid but unmapped |
| Bridge TTL | Session-only | Node expires at session end |

```rust
impl StrategyBrain {
    /// Create a Fractal Bridge Node to handle semantic drift
    ///
    /// Triggered when: Semantic Similarity < Threshold AND Coherence > Threshold
    /// Action: Creates a Hyperedge connecting the last known intent to the new user concepts.
    pub async fn create_fractal_bridge(
        &self,
        current_intent_id: &str,
        user_concepts: &[String],
        user_embedding: &[f32; 768],
    ) -> Result<String, RuVectorError> {
        let bridge_id = uuid::Uuid::new_v4().to_string();

        // Definition of the Hyperedge Bridge
        // Connects: Current Intent <-> New Concepts
        // Metadata: origin='dynamic_drift', ttl='session_only'
        let query = format!(
            "CREATE (b:BridgeNode {{
                id: '{}',
                description: 'Fractal Bridge: {} -> {:?}',
                origin: 'DYNAMIC_DRIFT',
                ttl: 'SESSION_ONLY',
                created_at: datetime()
            }})",
            bridge_id, current_intent_id, user_concepts
        );

        self.db.query(&query).await?;

        // Store the embedding of the user's "off-script" input so we can match it again
        self.store_vector(&bridge_id, user_embedding).await?;

        // Link Bridge to Current Intent
        self.db.query(&format!(
            "MATCH (b:BridgeNode {{id: '{}'}}), (i:IntentNode {{id: '{}'}})
             CREATE (i)-[:BRIDGED_TO]->(b)",
            bridge_id, current_intent_id
        )).await?;

        Ok(bridge_id)
    }
}
```

```rust
/// Origin type for Strategy nodes
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize, PartialEq)]
pub enum StrategyOrigin {
    /// Learned from successful conversation outcome
    Learned,
    /// Manually injected by human operator via Frontend
    HumanInjected,
    /// Generated by the Oneiric Engine during offline dreaming
    OneiricSynthesis,
}

/// The structure of a synthetic dream memory
/// Created by the Oneiric Engine during offline counterfactual simulation
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct OneiricMemory {
    /// Session ID where the original near-miss occurred
    pub original_session_id: String,
    /// Turn number of the original near-miss
    pub original_turn: u32,
    /// Strategy ID discovered through simulation
    pub simulated_strategy_id: String,
    /// The probability that this simulation reflects reality (0.0-1.0)
    pub confidence_score: f32,
    /// How many iterations it took to find this solution
    pub dream_depth: u32,
    /// Origin marker for this memory
    pub origin: StrategyOrigin,
}

impl StrategyBrain {
    /// Inject a human-designed strategy into RuVector
    ///
    /// Called from Frontend "Strategy Architect" when operator creates a new strategy.
    /// The strategy text is embedded via Nomic and linked to the nearest Intent.
    /// Note: This injects a Strategy (path to goal), NOT a North Star coordinate (identity reference).
    pub async fn inject_human_strategy(
        &self,
        strategy_text: &str,
        nomic_embedding: &[f32; 768],
        target_archetype: ArchetypeId,
        vak_modality: VakType,
    ) -> Result<String, RuVectorError> {
        let strategy_id = uuid::Uuid::new_v4().to_string();

        // Find nearest IntentNode to link this strategy
        let nearest_intent = self.vector_search(
            nomic_embedding,
            1,
            Some("node_type = 'IntentNode'"),
        ).await?;

        let intent_id = nearest_intent.first()
            .map(|r| r.id.clone())
            .unwrap_or_else(|| "GENERAL".to_string());

        // Create Strategy node with HUMAN_INJECTED origin
        self.db.query(&format!(
            "CREATE (s:Strategy {{
                id: '{}',
                description: '{}',
                target_archetype: '{}',
                vak_modality: '{}',
                origin: 'HUMAN_INJECTED',
                is_antipattern: false,
                created_at: datetime()
            }})",
            strategy_id, strategy_text, target_archetype, vak_modality
        )).await?;

        // Store embedding vector
        self.store_vector(&strategy_id, nomic_embedding).await?;

        // Link to IntentNode
        self.db.query(&format!(
            "MATCH (s:Strategy {{id: '{}'}}), (i:IntentNode {{id: '{}'}})
             CREATE (s)-[:RESOLVES {{source: 'HUMAN_INJECTED'}}]->(i)",
            strategy_id, intent_id
        )).await?;

        Ok(strategy_id)
    }

    /// Get read access to the graph database for Prescience Engine queries
    ///
    /// Returns a reference that allows traversing strategy nodes and edges
    /// without modification. Used by Prescience Engine for MCTS simulation.
    pub fn get_graph_access(&self) -> &GraphDatabase {
        &self.db
    }
}
```

```rust
impl StrategyBrain {
    /// Find best strategy filtered by user's archetype and VAK modality
    ///
    /// CRITICAL: Strategies are NOT generic. They MUST match the user's profile.
    /// A "Power" strategy (assertive, direct) will alienate a "Trust" user (warm, patient).
    pub async fn find_best_strategy_for_profile(
        &self,
        semantic_embedding: &[f32; 768],
        intent_id: &str,
        target_archetype: ArchetypeId,
        vak_modality: VakType,
    ) -> Result<StrategyResult, RuVectorError> {
        // Step 1: Find top strategies for this intent, filtered by archetype and VAK
        let top_strategies: Vec<StrategyRecord> = self.db.query(&format!(
            "MATCH (s:Strategy)-[r:LEADS_TO]->(o:Outcome)
             WHERE o.type = 'WIN'
               AND o.intent = '{}'
               AND s.target_archetype = '{}'
               AND s.vak_modality = '{}'
             RETURN s.id AS id, s.description AS description, r.coherence_gain AS coherence_gain
             ORDER BY r.coherence_gain DESC
             LIMIT 5",
            intent_id, target_archetype, vak_modality
        )).await?;

        // Step 2: Find nearest anti-pattern to current conversation state
        let nearest_antipattern = self.vector_search_with_filter(
            semantic_embedding,
            1,
            &format!("is_antipattern = true AND target_archetype = '{}'", target_archetype),
        ).await?;

        // Step 3: Filter out strategies too similar to anti-patterns
        const ANTIPATTERN_SIMILARITY_THRESHOLD: f32 = 0.90;

        for strategy in top_strategies {
            let strategy_embedding = self.get_vector(&strategy.id).await?;

            if let Some(antipattern) = nearest_antipattern.first() {
                let antipattern_embedding = self.get_vector(&antipattern.id).await?;
                let similarity = cosine_similarity_768(&strategy_embedding, &antipattern_embedding);

                if similarity > ANTIPATTERN_SIMILARITY_THRESHOLD {
                    continue;
                }
            }

            return Ok(StrategyResult {
                strategy_id: strategy.id,
                description: strategy.description,
                coherence_gain: strategy.coherence_gain,
                embedding: strategy_embedding,
                target_archetype,
                vak_modality,
            });
        }

        // No suitable strategy found - return default exploratory strategy
        Ok(StrategyResult::exploratory_for_profile(target_archetype, vak_modality))
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct StrategyResult {
    pub strategy_id: String,
    pub description: String,
    pub coherence_gain: f32,
    pub embedding: [f32; 768],
    pub target_archetype: ArchetypeId,
    pub vak_modality: VakType,
}

impl StrategyResult {
    /// Default exploratory strategy when no suitable Winning Strategy exists.
    /// Tailored to the user's archetype and VAK modality.
    pub fn exploratory_for_profile(archetype: ArchetypeId, vak: VakType) -> Self {
        Self {
            strategy_id: "EXPLORATORY".to_string(),
            description: format!(
                "Explore user needs through {} communication style with {} emphasis",
                archetype.communication_style(),
                vak.description()
            ),
            coherence_gain: 0.0,
            embedding: [0.0; 768],
            target_archetype: archetype,
            vak_modality: vak,
        }
    }
}
```

### 4.3 Session Reasoning Brain (AgentDB)

**REQ-AGENTDB-001: AgentDB Integration Architecture**

The `ReasoningBrain` MUST wrap the AgentDB instance and utilize the following specific modules from the AgentDB library:

| Module | Purpose | Required API Calls |
|:-------|:--------|:-------------------|
| **ReasoningBank** | Store high-reward strategy outcomes for pattern matching | `db.reasoningBank.store({ pattern, context, reasoning, outcome, confidence })` |
| **CausalMemory** | Track strategy → goal impact factors for Prescience Engine | `causal_add_edge({ cause, effect, uplift, confidence })`, `causal_query({ cause, min_confidence })` |
| **Reflexion** | Store near-miss episodes for Oneiric Engine replay | `reflexion_store({ task, episode, outcome })`, `reflexion_retrieve({ task, k })` |

**CRITICAL IMPLEMENTATION RULES:**
1. When Reward > 0.7, store the "Strategy Description" as the `pattern` and the "User Context" as `context` in ReasoningBank
2. Map `StrategyID` (cause) to `GoalProgress` (effect) in CausalMemory. The `uplift` value becomes the `Impact Factor` for MCTS simulation
3. Store "Near Miss" turns (Reward between -0.2 and 0.2) as episodes in Reflexion for Oneiric Engine re-simulation

**REQ-AGENTDB-002: ReasoningBrain Definition**

```rust
/// ReasoningBrain wraps AgentDB for session reasoning and causal tracking
///
/// IMPLEMENTATION MANDATE:
/// - Use AgentDB's ReasoningBank for successful pattern storage
/// - Use AgentDB's CausalMemory for strategy → goal impact tracking
/// - Use AgentDB's Reflexion for near-miss episode storage
/// - Node.js Bridge or WASM required for AgentDB integration from Rust
pub struct ReasoningBrain {
    /// AgentDB instance (via Node.js Bridge or WASM)
    db: AgentDbInstance,
    /// Configuration for AgentDB features
    config: AgentDbConfig,
}

/// AgentDB configuration
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize)]
pub struct AgentDbConfig {
    /// Enable ReasoningBank for pattern storage
    pub enable_reasoning: bool,
    /// Enable CausalMemory for impact factor tracking
    pub enable_causal: bool,
    /// Quantization type for memory efficiency
    pub quantization_type: String,
    /// Quantization bits (4-32x memory reduction)
    pub quantization_bits: u8,
}

impl ReasoningBrain {
    /// Record a successful experience in AgentDB for ReasoningBank retrieval
    ///
    /// CRITICAL: Only call when Reward > 0.7 (successful strategy)
    ///
    /// OPTIMIZATION: Uses AgentDB Core `store()` API which accepts pre-computed vectors.
    /// This bypasses AgentDB's internal embedding generation, eliminating ~50ms latency.
    /// The semantic vector from Stream A (Nomic 768-dim) is passed directly.
    ///
    /// IMPLEMENTATION: AgentDB does not expose a `reasoning_bank_store_vector()` method.
    /// Instead, use the Core `db.store()` API with metadata tagging to enable ReasoningBank
    /// query logic. The `type: "reasoning_pattern"` metadata field allows retrieval via
    /// `db.reasoningBank.query({ context, k })` pattern matching.
    ///
    /// Parameters:
    /// - `session_id`: Current session identifier
    /// - `context_text`: The user's transcript text (what the user said)
    /// - `context_embedding`: Pre-computed 768-dim Nomic semantic vector from Stream A
    /// - `action_taken`: The Strategy Description (what strategy was applied)
    /// - `outcome`: "success" or "fail" based on Reward value
    /// - `confidence`: The calculated Reward value (0.0-1.0)
    /// - `reasoning_trace`: The LLM's reasoning for this action
    ///
    /// AgentDB API: `db.store({ id, vector, metadata })` - Core API accepting raw vectors
    pub async fn record_experience(
        &self,
        session_id: &str,
        context_text: &str,
        context_embedding: &[f32; 768],
        action_taken: &str,
        outcome: &str,
        confidence: f32,
        reasoning_trace: &str,
    ) -> Result<(), AgentDbError> {
        // Use AgentDB Core store() API with metadata for ReasoningBank compatibility
        // This bypasses internal embedding generation by passing pre-computed vectors
        self.db.store(StoreRequest {
            id: uuid::Uuid::new_v4().to_string(),
            vector: context_embedding.to_vec(),
            metadata: ReasoningPatternMetadata {
                // Tag for ReasoningBank retrieval logic
                pattern_type: "reasoning_pattern".to_string(),
                // Strategy pattern (what action was taken)
                pattern: action_taken.to_string(),
                // User context text (for human readability and debugging)
                context_text: context_text.to_string(),
                // LLM reasoning trace
                reasoning: reasoning_trace.to_string(),
                // Outcome classification
                outcome: outcome.to_string(),
                // Reward confidence score
                confidence,
                // Session tracking
                session_id: session_id.to_string(),
                // Timestamp for temporal queries
                timestamp: chrono::Utc::now().timestamp(),
            },
        }).await
    }

    /// Add a causal link between Strategy and Goal Progress
    ///
    /// Called after each turn to track which strategies advance which goals.
    /// The `uplift` value is used by Prescience Engine as the Impact Factor.
    ///
    /// AgentDB API: `causal_add_edge({ cause, effect, uplift, confidence })`
    pub async fn add_causal_link(
        &self,
        strategy_id: &str,
        goal_id: &str,
        uplift: f32,
        confidence: f32,
    ) -> Result<(), AgentDbError> {
        self.db.causal_add_edge(CausalEdge {
            cause: strategy_id.to_string(),
            effect: goal_id.to_string(),
            uplift,
            confidence,
        }).await
    }

    /// Query causal impact factor for a strategy
    ///
    /// Used by Prescience Engine during MCTS simulation.
    ///
    /// AgentDB API: `causal_query({ cause, min_confidence })`
    ///
    /// Returns: The uplift (impact factor) for the given strategy, or 0.5 if not found
    pub async fn get_impact_factor(
        &self,
        strategy_id: &str,
        archetype: &ArchetypeId,
    ) -> Result<f32, AgentDbError> {
        let result = self.db.causal_query(CausalQuery {
            cause: strategy_id.to_string(),
            min_confidence: 0.5,
        }).await?;

        Ok(result.uplift.unwrap_or(0.5))
    }

    /// Store a near-miss episode for Oneiric Engine replay
    ///
    /// Called when Reward is between -0.2 and 0.2 (ambiguous outcome).
    /// These episodes are re-simulated during idle time.
    ///
    /// AgentDB API: `reflexion_store({ task, episode, outcome })`
    pub async fn store_near_miss(
        &self,
        intent_id: &str,
        cognitive_state: &CognitiveState,
        strategy_id: &str,
        reward: f32,
    ) -> Result<(), AgentDbError> {
        self.db.reflexion_store(ReflexionEntry {
            task: intent_id.to_string(),
            episode: serde_json::to_string(&ReflexionEpisode {
                cognitive_state: cognitive_state.clone(),
                strategy_id: strategy_id.to_string(),
                reward,
            })?,
            outcome: if reward > 0.0 { "partial_success" } else { "partial_fail" }.to_string(),
        }).await
    }

    /// Retrieve near-miss episodes for Oneiric Engine re-simulation
    ///
    /// AgentDB API: `reflexion_retrieve({ task, k })`
    pub async fn get_near_miss_episodes(
        &self,
        intent_id: &str,
        limit: usize,
    ) -> Result<Vec<ReflexionEpisode>, AgentDbError> {
        let entries = self.db.reflexion_retrieve(ReflexionQuery {
            task: intent_id.to_string(),
            k: limit,
        }).await?;

        let episodes: Vec<ReflexionEpisode> = entries
            .into_iter()
            .filter_map(|e| serde_json::from_str(&e.episode).ok())
            .collect();

        Ok(episodes)
    }

    /// Provide read access to CausalMemory for Prescience Engine
    pub fn get_causal_access(&self) -> &CausalMemory {
        &self.db.causal_memory
    }
}

/// AgentDB Core store() request structure
///
/// This struct maps directly to the AgentDB `db.store()` API which accepts:
/// - `id`: Unique vector identifier (auto-generated UUID recommended)
/// - `vector`: Raw float array (768-dim for Nomic compatibility)
/// - `metadata`: Arbitrary key-value pairs for filtering and retrieval
///
/// Reference: AgentDB API `db.store({ id, vector, metadata })`
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct StoreRequest {
    /// Unique identifier for this vector entry
    pub id: String,
    /// Pre-computed embedding vector (768-dim for Nomic Embed Text v1)
    /// CRITICAL: Dimensions must match [agentdb.dimensions] config (768)
    pub vector: Vec<f32>,
    /// Metadata for ReasoningBank pattern matching and retrieval
    pub metadata: ReasoningPatternMetadata,
}

/// Metadata structure for ReasoningBank pattern storage
///
/// This metadata enables AgentDB's ReasoningBank query logic to retrieve
/// patterns based on context similarity and pattern matching.
///
/// The `pattern_type` field MUST be set to "reasoning_pattern" for
/// compatibility with `db.reasoningBank.query({ context, k })` retrieval.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct ReasoningPatternMetadata {
    /// Type discriminator for ReasoningBank retrieval
    /// MUST be "reasoning_pattern" for ReasoningBank compatibility
    pub pattern_type: String,
    /// The strategy description (what action was taken)
    pub pattern: String,
    /// The user's transcript text (for human readability and debugging)
    pub context_text: String,
    /// The LLM's reasoning trace for this action
    pub reasoning: String,
    /// "success" or "fail" based on Reward value
    pub outcome: String,
    /// The calculated Reward value (0.0-1.0)
    pub confidence: f32,
    /// Current session identifier
    pub session_id: String,
    /// Unix timestamp of when this entry was created
    pub timestamp: i64,
}

/// Causal edge for impact factor tracking
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct CausalEdge {
    pub cause: String,
    pub effect: String,
    pub uplift: f32,
    pub confidence: f32,
}

/// Query structure for causal lookup
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct CausalQuery {
    pub cause: String,
    pub min_confidence: f32,
}

/// Entry for Reflexion storage
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct ReflexionEntry {
    pub task: String,
    pub episode: String,
    pub outcome: String,
}

/// Query structure for Reflexion retrieval
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ReflexionQuery {
    pub task: String,
    pub k: usize,
}

/// Episode data stored in Reflexion
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct ReflexionEpisode {
    pub cognitive_state: CognitiveState,
    pub strategy_id: String,
    pub reward: f32,
}
```
