**REQ-DATA-003: Strategy Pruning Logic (Post-Session Only)**

**CRITICAL TIMING CONSTRAINT**: Strategy pruning MUST only occur AFTER session ends. The system MUST NOT prune during an active session.

| Timing | Action | Reason |
|:-------|:-------|:-------|
| **During Session** | MARK for review only | Prevents database locking in <200ms loop |
| **Post-Session** | DELETE inferior strategies | Safe timing for database operations |

**Pruning Rule**: For every (IntentID + ArchetypeID + VakModality) combination, keep only the Top 1 strategy by CoherenceGain.

**Failure Deduplication Rule**: When storing a failed strategy as an AntiPattern:
- If an existing AntiPattern has similarity > 0.99, increment its `failure_count` instead of creating a new record
- This prevents database bloat from repeated similar failures

```rust
impl StrategyBrain {
    /// Prune inferior strategies at session end
    ///
    /// CRITICAL TIMING: This method MUST only be called AFTER session closes.
    /// Calling during active session causes:
    /// - Database locking issues in <200ms real-time loop
    /// - Premature pruning of strategies that need more samples
    ///
    /// Trigger: End of Session (session_end event)
    /// Rule: For every IntentID + ArchetypeID + VakModality combination,
    ///       keep only the Top 1 strategy by CoherenceGain
    /// Failure Handling:
    ///   - If strategy failed, store as AntiPattern
    ///   - If AntiPattern already exists (Similarity > 0.99), increment counter (Deduplication)
    pub async fn prune_strategies_post_session(&self) -> Result<PruneReport, RuVectorError> {
        let mut deleted_count = 0;
        let mut kept_count = 0;

        // Get all intents using Cypher query
        let intents: Vec<IntentRecord> = self.db.query(
            "MATCH (i:IntentNode) RETURN i.id AS id, i.name AS name"
        ).await?;

        for intent in intents {
            // Get all winning strategies for this intent, grouped by archetype and VAK
            let strategies: Vec<StrategyRecord> = self.db.query(&format!(
                "MATCH (s:Strategy)-[r:LEADS_TO]->(o:Outcome)
                 WHERE o.type = 'WIN' AND o.intent = '{}'
                 RETURN s.id AS id, s.target_archetype AS archetype,
                        s.vak_modality AS vak, r.coherence_gain AS coherence_gain
                 ORDER BY s.target_archetype, s.vak_modality, r.coherence_gain DESC",
                intent.id
            )).await?;

            // Group by archetype + VAK and keep top 1 per group
            let mut seen_groups: HashSet<(ArchetypeId, VakType)> = HashSet::new();

            for strategy in strategies {
                let group_key = (strategy.archetype, strategy.vak);

                if seen_groups.contains(&group_key) {
                    // Delete this inferior strategy
                    self.db.query(&format!(
                        "MATCH (s:Strategy {{id: '{}'}})
                         DETACH DELETE s",
                        strategy.id
                    )).await?;
                    deleted_count += 1;
                } else {
                    // Keep this strategy (best for its archetype + VAK group)
                    seen_groups.insert(group_key);
                    kept_count += 1;
                }
            }
        }

        Ok(PruneReport {
            deleted_count,
            kept_count,
            timestamp: chrono::Utc::now(),
        })
    }

    /// Mark strategy for potential pruning during session (NO DELETION)
    ///
    /// During active session, only MARK strategies - never delete.
    /// Deletion happens in prune_strategies_post_session()
    pub async fn mark_for_review(
        &self,
        strategy_id: &str,
        reason: &str,
    ) -> Result<(), RuVectorError> {
        self.db.query(&format!(
            "MATCH (s:Strategy {{id: '{}'}})
             SET s.marked_for_review = true, s.review_reason = '{}'",
            strategy_id, reason
        )).await?;
        Ok(())
    }

    /// Store failure with deduplication
    pub async fn store_fail(
        &self,
        strategy_embedding: &[f32; 768],
        intent_id: &str,
        target_archetype: ArchetypeId,
        vak_modality: VakType,
        description: &str,
    ) -> Result<(), RuVectorError> {
        // Check for duplicate failure (similarity > 0.99) using vector search
        let similar = self.vector_search(
            strategy_embedding,
            1,
            Some(&format!(
                "metadata.is_antipattern = true AND metadata.target_archetype = '{}'",
                target_archetype
            )),
        ).await?;

        if let Some(existing) = similar.first() {
            if existing.similarity > 0.99 {
                // Increment failure count using Cypher (Deduplication)
                self.db.query(&format!(
                    "MATCH (s:Strategy {{id: '{}'}})
                     SET s.failure_count = s.failure_count + 1",
                    existing.id
                )).await?;
                return Ok(());
            }
        }

        // Create new failure node as AntiPattern using Cypher
        let strategy_id = uuid::Uuid::new_v4().to_string();
        let outcome_id = uuid::Uuid::new_v4().to_string();

        // Create Strategy node with antipattern flag
        self.db.query(&format!(
            "CREATE (s:Strategy {{
                id: '{}',
                description: '{}',
                target_archetype: '{}',
                vak_modality: '{}',
                failure_count: 1,
                is_antipattern: true,
                created_at: datetime()
            }})",
            strategy_id, description, target_archetype, vak_modality
        )).await?;

        // Store embedding vector separately (RuVector vector storage)
        self.store_vector(&strategy_id, strategy_embedding).await?;

        // Create Outcome node
        self.db.query(&format!(
            "CREATE (o:Outcome {{
                id: '{}',
                type: 'FAIL',
                intent: '{}',
                timestamp: datetime()
            }})",
            outcome_id, intent_id
        )).await?;

        // Create LEADS_TO edge
        self.db.query(&format!(
            "MATCH (s:Strategy {{id: '{}'}}), (o:Outcome {{id: '{}'}})
             CREATE (s)-[:LEADS_TO {{coherence_gain: 0.0}}]->(o)",
            strategy_id, outcome_id
        )).await?;

        Ok(())
    }
}
```

**REQ-DATA-007: Strategy Retrieval Logic (Path to Target Intent)**

When querying RuVector for a **Winning Strategy** (that advances the user toward the target business goal/intent), the system MUST avoid known failure patterns and filter by the user's profile. Strategies are conversational paths; they are distinct from North Star Coordinates which serve as fixed identity measurement references.

**REQ-DATA-007a: Dual-Write Strategy Storage (RuVector + LanceDB)**

When storing a winning strategy, the system performs a DUAL-WRITE operation:
1. **Logic (The Map)**: Store the strategy graph structure in RuVector
2. **Hologram (The Holodeck)**: Store the execution recording in LanceDB

```rust
impl StrategyBrain {
    /// Store winning strategy (Logic -> RuVector) AND Hologram (Execution -> LanceDB)
    ///
    /// DUAL-WRITE: This method writes to BOTH databases atomically.
    /// - RuVector: Stores the strategic logic (graph node + edges)
    /// - LanceDB: Stores the execution recording (how it was delivered)
    pub async fn store_win(
        &self,
        cognitive_state: &CognitiveState,
        description: &str,
        reward: f32,
    ) -> Result<(), StorageError> {
        let strategy_id = uuid::Uuid::new_v4().to_string();
        let outcome_id = uuid::Uuid::new_v4().to_string();

        // 1. Store Logic in RuVector (The Map)
        self.db.query(&format!(
            "CREATE (s:Strategy {{
                id: '{}',
                description: '{}',
                target_archetype: '{}',
                vak_modality: '{}',
                is_antipattern: false,
                created_at: datetime()
            }})",
            strategy_id, description, cognitive_state.primary_archetype, cognitive_state.vak_modality
        )).await?;

        // Store embedding vector
        self.store_vector(&strategy_id, &cognitive_state.semantic_embedding).await?;

        // Create Outcome node
        self.db.query(&format!(
            "CREATE (o:Outcome {{
                id: '{}',
                type: 'WIN',
                intent: '{}',
                timestamp: datetime()
            }})",
            outcome_id, cognitive_state.intent_id
        )).await?;

        // Create LEADS_TO edge with coherence_gain
        self.db.query(&format!(
            "MATCH (s:Strategy {{id: '{}'}}), (o:Outcome {{id: '{}'}})
             CREATE (s)-[:LEADS_TO {{coherence_gain: {}}}]->(o)",
            strategy_id, outcome_id, reward
        )).await?;

        // Link to IntentNode if exists
        self.db.query(&format!(
            "MATCH (s:Strategy {{id: '{}'}}), (i:IntentNode {{id: '{}'}})
             MERGE (s)-[:RESOLVES]->(i)",
            strategy_id, cognitive_state.intent_id
        )).await?;

        // 2. Store Hologram in LanceDB (The Holodeck)
        let hologram = HolographicExecution {
            strategy_id: strategy_id.clone(),
            transcript: description.to_string(),
            tone_vector: cognitive_state.x_vector,
            emotion_vector: cognitive_state.emotion_embedding,
            valence: cognitive_state.valence,
            arousal: cognitive_state.arousal,
            wpm: cognitive_state.chronemics[0],
            latency_ms: cognitive_state.chronemics[1],
            style_score: cognitive_state.style_score,
            reward_score: reward,
            timestamp: chrono::Utc::now().timestamp(),
        };

        self.lancedb_connection.table("strategy_executions").add(&[hologram]).await?;

        Ok(())
    }
}
```

### 4.2 LanceDB: The Identity & Profile Brain

**REQ-DATA-004: LanceDB Purpose & Content**

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Content - Identity** | WavLM X-Vectors (512-dim) for Voice Fingerprinting |
| **Content - Emotion History** | Wav2Vec2 Pooled Embeddings (1024-dim) for emotional baseline tracking |
| **Content - Profile History** | Hexa-modal profile snapshots for tracking psychological drift over time |
| **Content - Execution Holograms** | Full-sense recordings of successful turns for Ghost Replay |
| **Profile Storage Purpose** | Long-term tracking of user's 6-dimensional coordinate across sessions |
| **Constraint** | Strictly append-only for profile history; optimized vector search for identity |
| **Constraint** | Does NOT store semantic strategy vectors (those go to RuVector) |
| **Library** | `lancedb` (Native Rust) |

**REQ-DATA-004b: Holographic Strategy Storage (Ghost Replay)**

| Table Name | `strategy_executions` |
|:---|:---|
| **Purpose** | Stores "Full-Sense" recordings of successful turns for future replay |
| **Content** | Hexa-modal snapshot of *how* a strategy was executed |

```rust
/// A "Full-Sense" recording of a successful strategy execution.
/// Used to instruct the AI on Tone, Pace, and Emotion for future execution.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct HolographicExecution {
    /// Link to the StrategyNode in RuVector
    pub strategy_id: String,
    /// The exact text used
    pub transcript: String,
    /// Stream B: Tone Vector (512-dim)
    pub tone_vector: [f32; 512],
    /// Stream C: Emotion Vector (1024-dim)
    pub emotion_vector: [f32; 1024],
    /// Stream C: Scalar targets
    pub valence: f32,
    pub arousal: f32,
    /// Stream F: Chronemics
    pub wpm: f32,
    pub latency_ms: f32,
    /// Stream D: Style
    pub style_score: f32,
    /// Metadata
    pub reward_score: f32,
    pub timestamp: i64,
}
```

**REQ-DATA-004a: Emotional Data Separation**

The Wav2Vec2 model produces TWO distinct outputs that MUST be routed differently:

| Output Type | Destination | Purpose |
|:------------|:------------|:--------|
| **Pooled Embedding (1024-dim)** | LanceDB | Long-term emotional baseline tracking |
| **Scalars (Arousal, Valence)** | Physics Engine | Calculate w_e weight for physics equation |

The Physics Engine requires scalar values (f32), NOT vectors. Using the 1024-dim embedding in physics calculations will cause mathematical errors.

**REQ-DATA-005: Identity Verification Schema**

| Field | Type | Description |
|:------|:-----|:------------|
| `user_id` | UUID | Unique identifier |
| `voice_embedding` | Vector[512] | WavLM identity embedding |
| `profile_history` | ProfileSnapshot[] | Hexa-modal User Position Arrays per turn (stores the 5 separate vectors + chronemics independently, append-only) |
| `created_at` | Timestamp | First seen |
| `last_seen` | Timestamp | Most recent interaction |
| `session_count` | u32 | Number of sessions |

**Profile Snapshot Structure:**

```rust
/// A snapshot of the user's 5-vector position across independent embedding spaces at a point in time.
/// Used for tracking psychological drift (e.g., user shifts from "Power" to "Trust" as rapport builds).
/// **NOTE**: The user does NOT have a single centroid. Each embedding space is independent and
/// uses different dimensions/models. This struct stores the user's position vector in each space.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct ProfileSnapshot {
    /// Stream A: Semantic position vector (768-dim Nomic embedding space)
    pub semantic_vector: [f32; 768],
    /// Stream B: Tone position vector (512-dim WavLM embedding space)
    pub tone_vector: [f32; 512],
    /// Stream C: Emotion position vector (1024-dim Wav2Vec2 embedding space)
    pub emotion_vector: [f32; 1024],
    /// Stream D: Style position (formality score 0.0-1.0)
    pub style_score: f32,
    /// Stream E: Action position vector (dialog act probabilities)
    pub action_logits: [f32; 42],
    /// Stream F: Chronemic position (wpm, latency, jitter, interruption_count)
    pub chronemics: [f32; 4],
    /// Detected archetype at this snapshot
    pub archetype: ArchetypeId,
    /// Detected VAK modality at this snapshot
    pub vak_modality: VakType,
    /// Detected gender for this snapshot (used for gender-specific reference vector selection)
    pub gender: Gender,
    /// Turn number when snapshot was taken
    pub turn_number: u32,
    /// Timestamp when snapshot was taken
    pub timestamp: chrono::DateTime<chrono::Utc>,
}
```

**REQ-DATA-006: Identity Verification Logic (Hexa-Modal Fusion)**

```rust
use lancedb::{Connection, Table};
use uuid::Uuid;
use crate::dimensions::{IDENTITY_DIM, SEMANTIC_DIM, EMOTION_DIM, STYLE_DIM, ACTION_DIM, CHRONEMIC_DIM};

/// CRITICAL: Weighted Composite Confidence Score Threshold
///
/// This is a SCALAR value (0.0 to 1.0) representing the weighted sum of all modality similarities.
/// It is NOT a raw cosine similarity threshold of a single vector.
///
/// Formula: Σ (ModalitySimilarity_i × ModalityWeight_i) > 0.97
///
/// WEIGHTING STRATEGY (Defined in config/cognitive_physics.toml):
/// - Voice (WavLM):     60% weight - Primary Biometric (Cosine Similarity)
/// - Semantic (Nomic):  10% weight - Topic Consistency (Cosine Similarity)
/// - Emotion (Wav2Vec2): 10% weight - Emotional Baseline (Cosine Similarity)
/// - Style (RoBERTa):   10% weight - Formality Baseline (Scalar Similarity)
/// - Action (BERT):      5% weight - Dialog Patterns (Cosine Similarity)
/// - Chronemics:         5% weight - Speaking Pace (Euclidean Similarity → inverted)
///
/// HEXA-MODAL FUSION RATIONALE:
/// - Voice-only verification can fail in noisy environments
/// - Combining 6 modalities provides robust identification
/// - Allows Fast-Track exit from Safe Harbor on first turn if user is recognized
/// - Weighted ensemble ensures primary biometric (Voice) dominates while
///   behavioral signals provide supporting evidence
pub const COMPOSITE_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD: f32 = 0.97;

#[derive(Debug)]
pub enum IdentityResult {
    /// Verified match where Weighted Composite Confidence Score > 0.97
    /// Returns User ID and their LAST KNOWN profile (for immediate hydration)
    Verified {
        user_id: String,
        /// This is the Weighted Composite Confidence Score, NOT a single cosine similarity
        similarity: f32,
        historical_profile: Option<ProfileSnapshot>,
    },
    /// No match found or Weighted Composite Confidence Score < 0.97
    NewUser {
        user_id: String,
    },
}

pub struct IdentityBrain {
    connection: Connection,
    table: Table,
}

impl IdentityBrain {
    pub const DB_PATH: &'static str = "./data/identity/voice_identities.lance";
    pub const TABLE_NAME: &'static str = "identities";

    /// Verify identity using Hexa-Modal Fusion
    ///
    /// CALCULATION METHOD: Linear Combination of Normalized Similarities
    ///
    /// This method performs composite identity verification by fusing signals
    /// from all 6 analysis streams. This enables Fast-Track identification
    /// where a returning user can be verified on the first turn, triggering
    /// immediate Safe Harbor exit and profile hydration.
    ///
    /// WEIGHTING STRATEGY (Must match config/cognitive_physics.toml):
    /// - Voice (WavLM):     60% (Primary Biometric - Cosine Similarity)
    /// - Semantic (Nomic):  10% (Topic Consistency - Cosine Similarity)
    /// - Emotion (Wav2Vec2): 10% (Emotional Baseline - Cosine Similarity)
    /// - Style (RoBERTa):   10% (Formality Baseline - Scalar Similarity)
    /// - Action (BERT):      5% (Dialog Patterns - Cosine Similarity)
    /// - Chronemics:         5% (Speaking Pace - Euclidean Similarity)
    ///
    /// INPUTS: All 6 stream vectors from CognitiveAnalyzer
    /// OUTPUT: IdentityResult with Weighted Composite Score and optional historical profile
    pub async fn verify_multimodal_identity(
        &self,
        wavlm_vector: &[f32; IDENTITY_DIM],
        semantic_vector: &[f32; SEMANTIC_DIM],
        emotion_vector: &[f32; EMOTION_DIM],
        style_score: f32,
        action_vector: &[f32; ACTION_DIM],
        chronemics: &[f32; CHRONEMIC_DIM],
    ) -> Result<IdentityResult, LanceDbError> {
        // 1. Fast Filter: Find top 5 candidates by Voice (WavLM)
        // Voice remains the primary biometric for candidate selection
        let candidates = self.table
            .search(wavlm_vector)
            .limit(5)
            .execute()
            .await?;

        let mut best_match: Option<(String, f32, Option<ProfileSnapshot>)> = None;
        let mut highest_composite_score = 0.0;

        for candidate in candidates {
            let stored_user_id = candidate.get::<String>("user_id")?;

            // Retrieve profile history to build user's average position in each embedding space
            let history: Vec<ProfileSnapshot> = candidate.get("profile_history")?;

            // Calculate user's average position in each embedding space from historical snapshots
            let user_pos = self.calculate_history_average_position(&history);

            // 2. Calculate Normalized Sub-Scores for each modality (0.0 to 1.0)
            let voice_sim = candidate.score; // WavLM Cosine Similarity
            let sem_sim = cosine_similarity_768(semantic_vector, &user_pos.semantic_vector);
            let emo_sim = cosine_similarity_1024(emotion_vector, &user_pos.emotion_vector);
            let action_sim = cosine_similarity_42(action_vector, &user_pos.action_logits);

            // Scalar/Euclidean distances inverted to Similarity (1.0 - Distance)
            let style_sim = 1.0 - (style_score - user_pos.style_score).abs().clamp(0.0, 1.0);
            let chron_sim = 1.0 - euclidean_distance_4(chronemics, &user_pos.chronemics).min(1.0);

            // 3. Calculate Weighted Composite Confidence Score
            // Formula: Σ (ModalitySimilarity_i × ModalityWeight_i)
            // Weights from config/cognitive_physics.toml - MUST sum to 1.0
            let composite_score = (voice_sim * 0.60)   // Voice: Primary biometric
                + (sem_sim * 0.10)                      // Semantic: Topic consistency
                + (emo_sim * 0.10)                      // Emotion: Emotional baseline
                + (style_sim * 0.10)                    // Style: Formality baseline
                + (action_sim * 0.05)                   // Action: Dialog patterns
                + (chron_sim * 0.05);                   // Chronemic: Speaking pace

            if composite_score > highest_composite_score {
                highest_composite_score = composite_score;
                // Capture the last known profile for hydration on successful match
                best_match = Some((stored_user_id, composite_score, history.last().cloned()));
            }
        }

        // 4. Threshold Check: Verify if Weighted Composite Confidence Score exceeds 0.97
        if let Some((user_id, score, history)) = best_match {
            if score > COMPOSITE_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD {
                self.update_last_seen(&user_id).await?;
                return Ok(IdentityResult::Verified {
                    user_id,
                    similarity: score,
                    historical_profile: history,
                });
            }
        }

        // No match or below threshold - create new user identity
        let new_user_id = self.create_new_identity(wavlm_vector).await?;
        Ok(IdentityResult::NewUser { user_id: new_user_id })
    }

    /// Calculates the user's average standing position in each of the 5 independent embedding spaces.
    ///
    /// Averages all historical profile snapshots to determine where the user
    /// typically positions in each of the 5 independent embedding spaces.
    /// **NOTE**: This function returns an array of average vectors, never a unified centroid.
    /// Each embedding space is independent with different dimensions and models.
    fn calculate_history_average_position(&self, history: &[ProfileSnapshot]) -> ProfileSnapshot {
        if history.is_empty() {
            return ProfileSnapshot::default();
        }

        let n = history.len() as f32;

        // Initialize accumulators
        let mut semantic_sum = [0.0f32; SEMANTIC_DIM];
        let mut tone_sum = [0.0f32; IDENTITY_DIM];
        let mut emotion_sum = [0.0f32; EMOTION_DIM];
        let mut style_sum = 0.0f32;
        let mut action_sum = [0.0f32; ACTION_DIM];
        let mut chronemic_sum = [0.0f32; CHRONEMIC_DIM];

        // Accumulate all snapshots
        for snapshot in history {
            for i in 0..SEMANTIC_DIM {
                semantic_sum[i] += snapshot.semantic_vector[i];
            }
            for i in 0..IDENTITY_DIM {
                tone_sum[i] += snapshot.tone_vector[i];
            }
            for i in 0..EMOTION_DIM {
                emotion_sum[i] += snapshot.emotion_vector[i];
            }
            style_sum += snapshot.style_score;
            for i in 0..ACTION_DIM {
                action_sum[i] += snapshot.action_logits[i];
            }
            for i in 0..CHRONEMIC_DIM {
                chronemic_sum[i] += snapshot.chronemics[i];
            }
        }

        // Calculate averages
        for i in 0..SEMANTIC_DIM {
            semantic_sum[i] /= n;
        }
        for i in 0..IDENTITY_DIM {
            tone_sum[i] /= n;
        }
        for i in 0..EMOTION_DIM {
            emotion_sum[i] /= n;
        }
        for i in 0..ACTION_DIM {
            action_sum[i] /= n;
        }
        for i in 0..CHRONEMIC_DIM {
            chronemic_sum[i] /= n;
        }

        ProfileSnapshot {
            semantic_vector: semantic_sum,
            tone_vector: tone_sum,
            emotion_vector: emotion_sum,
            style_score: style_sum / n,
            action_logits: action_sum,
            chronemics: chronemic_sum,
            archetype: history.last().map(|s| s.archetype).unwrap_or(ArchetypeId(0)),
            vak_modality: history.last().map(|s| s.vak_modality).unwrap_or(VakType::Visual),
            gender: history.last().map(|s| s.gender).unwrap_or(Gender::Male),
            turn_number: 0,
            timestamp: chrono::Utc::now(),
        }
    }

    /// Append profile snapshot for long-term tracking (append-only)
    ///
    /// CRITICAL: This stores the user's position vectors across all 5 embedding spaces.
    /// Purpose: Track psychological drift over time
    /// Use Case: Detect if user shifts from "Power" to "Trust" as rapport is built
    ///
    /// **Gender Persistence**: The detected_gender from the CognitiveState is stored
    /// in the snapshot to enable consistent gender-specific reference vector selection
    /// across sessions without re-classification.
    ///
    /// Input: Full CognitiveState containing all stream data
    pub async fn append_profile_snapshot(
        &self,
        user_id: &str,
        cognitive_state: &CognitiveState,
        turn_number: u32,
    ) -> Result<(), LanceDbError> {
        let snapshot = ProfileSnapshot {
            semantic_vector: cognitive_state.semantic_embedding,
            tone_vector: cognitive_state.x_vector,
            emotion_vector: cognitive_state.emotion_embedding,
            style_score: cognitive_state.style_score,
            action_logits: cognitive_state.dialog_acts,
            chronemics: cognitive_state.chronemics,
            archetype: cognitive_state.primary_archetype,
            vak_modality: cognitive_state.vak_modality,
            gender: cognitive_state.detected_gender,
            turn_number,
            timestamp: chrono::Utc::now(),
        };

        self.table
            .update()
            .where_clause(&format!("user_id = '{}'", user_id))
            .append("profile_history", serde_json::to_value(&snapshot)?)
            .execute()
            .await?;

        Ok(())
    }

    /// Retrieve the North Star Distances from the most recent profile snapshot
    ///
    /// Used by Physics Engine to calculate Drift Velocity (Current Dist - Previous Dist).
    /// Returns the archetype distances calculated at the previous turn, enabling
    /// temporal tracking of psychological movement toward receptive archetypes.
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    /// * `user_id` - The ID of the current user
    ///
    /// # Returns
    /// Map of ArchetypeId -> Distance (f32) from the previous turn.
    /// Returns None if this is the first turn (no history available).
    pub async fn get_previous_distances(
        &self,
        user_id: &str,
    ) -> Result<Option<HashMap<ArchetypeId, f32>>, LanceDbError> {
        let user_record = self.table
            .query()
            .where_clause(&format!("user_id = '{}'", user_id))
            .execute()
            .await?;

        if let Some(record) = user_record.first() {
            let history: Vec<ProfileSnapshot> = record.get("profile_history")?;

            // Return the distances from the most recent snapshot (if exists)
            if let Some(last_snapshot) = history.last() {
                // Retrieve pre-computed archetype distances stored in the snapshot
                // These distances are calculated during profiling and stored for TAD
                if let Some(distances) = &last_snapshot.archetype_distances {
                    return Ok(Some(distances.clone()));
                }
            }
        }

        Ok(None)
    }

    /// Analyze psychological drift over time
    ///
    /// Returns the trajectory of archetype shifts across the session
    pub async fn analyze_drift(
        &self,
        user_id: &str,
    ) -> Result<DriftAnalysis, LanceDbError> {
        let user_record = self.table
            .query()
            .where_clause(&format!("user_id = '{}'", user_id))
            .execute()
            .await?;

        if let Some(record) = user_record.first() {
            let history: Vec<ProfileSnapshot> = record.get("profile_history")?;

            // Analyze archetype transitions
            let mut transitions: Vec<ArchetypeTransition> = Vec::new();
            for window in history.windows(2) {
                if window[0].archetype != window[1].archetype {
                    transitions.push(ArchetypeTransition {
                        from: window[0].archetype,
                        to: window[1].archetype,
                        at_turn: window[1].turn_number,
                    });
                }
            }

            return Ok(DriftAnalysis {
                user_id: user_id.to_string(),
                initial_archetype: history.first().map(|s| s.archetype),
                current_archetype: history.last().map(|s| s.archetype),
                transitions,
                total_snapshots: history.len(),
            });
        }

        Err(LanceDbError::UserNotFound(user_id.to_string()))
    }

    /// Retrieve Holographic Execution for Ghost Replay
    ///
    /// Queries the strategy_executions table to find the best execution
    /// recording for a given strategy. Used to provide performance cues
    /// (Tone, Pace, Emotion targets) to the LLM.
    pub async fn get_hologram_for_strategy(
        &self,
        strategy_id: &str,
    ) -> Result<HolographicExecution, LanceDbError> {
        let executions_table = self.connection.open_table("strategy_executions").await?;

        // Find the highest-reward execution for this strategy
        let results = executions_table
            .query()
            .filter(&format!("strategy_id = '{}'", strategy_id))
            .limit(1)
            .execute()
            .await?;

        if let Some(record) = results.first() {
            Ok(HolographicExecution {
                strategy_id: record.get("strategy_id")?,
                transcript: record.get("transcript")?,
                tone_vector: record.get("tone_vector")?,
                emotion_vector: record.get("emotion_vector")?,
                valence: record.get("valence")?,
                arousal: record.get("arousal")?,
                wpm: record.get("wpm")?,
                latency_ms: record.get("latency_ms")?,
                style_score: record.get("style_score")?,
                reward_score: record.get("reward_score")?,
                timestamp: record.get("timestamp")?,
            })
        } else {
            Err(LanceDbError::HologramNotFound(strategy_id.to_string()))
        }
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ArchetypeTransition {
    pub from: ArchetypeId,
    pub to: ArchetypeId,
    pub at_turn: u32,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct DriftAnalysis {
    pub user_id: String,
    pub initial_archetype: Option<ArchetypeId>,
    pub current_archetype: Option<ArchetypeId>,
    pub transitions: Vec<ArchetypeTransition>,
    pub total_snapshots: usize,
}
```

### 4.3 Session Reasoning Brain (AgentDB)

**Role:** Short-term memory, Reasoning Bank, and RL State Transitions.

**Library:** `agentdb` (WASM/Rust)

**REQ-AGENTDB-001: The Learning Loop**

| Field | Type | Description |
|:------|:-----|:------------|
| `session_id` | UUID | Current session identifier |
| `turn_number` | u32 | Sequential turn counter |
| `cognitive_state` | CognitiveState | Unified state from parallel hexa-modal analysis |
| `action_taken` | ActionLabel | What the system did |
| `reward` | f32 | Calculated reward signal |
| `reasoning_trace` | String | Why this action was chosen |

```rust
use agentdb::{AgentDb, ReasoningBank, Transition};

/// Entry for the Shadow Slot post-session review system
///
/// Captures high-impact moments (|L| > 0.7) for human review and feedback.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct ShadowSlotEntry {
    /// Session identifier
    pub session_id: String,
    /// Turn number within the session
    pub turn_number: u32,
    /// AI-calculated reward for this turn
    pub ai_reward: f32,
    /// AI's reasoning trace for the action taken
    pub reasoning: String,
    /// Human vote applied post-session (None if not yet reviewed)
    pub human_vote: Option<HumanVote>,
}

/// Human feedback vote for RL learning adjustment
///
/// Applied during post-session Shadow Slot review to correct or reinforce AI behavior.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize, PartialEq)]
pub enum HumanVote {
    /// Positive Reinforcement: Increases edge weight in RuVector for the strategy
    Solidify,
    /// Negative Reinforcement: Marks StrategyNode as `is_antipattern=true` for this Intent context
    Punish,
    /// Calibration: AI success externally, but internal reasoning weights were incorrect
    Correct,
}

pub struct ReasoningBrain {
    db: AgentDb,
    reasoning_bank: ReasoningBank,
}

impl ReasoningBrain {
    pub const DB_PATH: &'static str = "./data/memory/agent.db";

    pub async fn new() -> Result<Self, AgentDbError> {
        let db = AgentDb::open(Self::DB_PATH).await?;
        let reasoning_bank = db.reasoning_bank();

        Ok(Self { db, reasoning_bank })
    }

    /// Get read access to causal memory for Prescience Engine queries
    ///
    /// Returns a reference that allows querying impact factors and causal
    /// links without modification. Used by Prescience Engine for MCTS weighting.
    pub fn get_causal_access(&self) -> &CausalMemory {
        self.db.causal_memory()
    }

    /// Record an RL transition for learning
    pub async fn record_transition(
        &self,
        session_id: &str,
        turn: u32,
        previous_state: &CognitiveState,
        action: &ActionLabel,
        reward: f32,
        current_state: &CognitiveState,
        reasoning: &str,
    ) -> Result<(), AgentDbError> {
        let transition = Transition {
            session_id: session_id.to_string(),
            turn_number: turn,
            previous_state: previous_state.clone(),
            action: action.clone(),
            reward,
            current_state: current_state.clone(),
            timestamp: chrono::Utc::now(),
        };

        self.db.store_transition(&transition).await?;

        // If this was a successful action (high reward), store reasoning
        if reward > 0.5 {
            self.reasoning_bank.store(
                session_id,
                turn,
                reasoning,
                reward,
            ).await?;
        }

        Ok(())
    }

    /// Retrieve critical moments (High |L|) for post-session Shadow Slot review
    ///
    /// Returns turns where |reward| > 0.7, representing high-impact decisions
    /// that warrant human review for learning reinforcement or correction.
    pub async fn get_shadow_slot_candidates(
        &self,
        session_id: &str,
    ) -> Result<Vec<ShadowSlotEntry>, AgentDbError> {
        let transitions = self.db.query_transitions(session_id).await?;

        let candidates: Vec<ShadowSlotEntry> = transitions
            .into_iter()
            .filter(|t| t.reward.abs() > 0.7)
            .map(|t| ShadowSlotEntry {
                session_id: t.session_id,
                turn_number: t.turn_number,
                ai_reward: t.reward,
                reasoning: self.reasoning_bank
                    .get(&t.session_id, t.turn_number)
                    .unwrap_or_default(),
                human_vote: None,
            })
            .collect();

        Ok(candidates)
    }

    /// Apply human feedback vote to a past transition
    ///
    /// Called from Frontend Shadow Slot review interface.
    /// Updates the transition record and triggers appropriate RL adjustment.
    pub async fn apply_human_vote(
        &self,
        session_id: &str,
        turn: u32,
        vote: HumanVote,
    ) -> Result<(), AgentDbError> {
        // Store the human vote in the transition record
        self.db.update_transition_vote(session_id, turn, &vote).await?;

        // Log the feedback event for audit trail
        self.db.log_event(&format!(
            "HITL_VOTE: session={}, turn={}, vote={:?}",
            session_id, turn, vote
        )).await?;

        Ok(())
    }
}
```

## 5. Audio Preprocessing Pipeline

### 5.1 Mandatory Audio Preprocessing

**REQ-AUDIO-001: Audio Normalization & VAD for Identity Verification**

The WavLM model requires clean speech to contribute effectively to the **0.97 Weighted Composite Confidence Score** required by `REQ-CONST-003`. Without proper preprocessing, the Voice Stream similarity degrades, making the composite threshold unreachable.

**CRITICAL RATIONALE**: Raw audio contains approximately 30% silence/noise. Feeding this directly into WavLM reduces the Voice Stream's similarity score (typically dropping to ~0.85). Since Voice carries a **60% weight** in the fusion algorithm, a degraded Voice score makes it mathematically impossible for the **Weighted Composite Confidence Score** to reach the **0.97 threshold** required for Fast-Track exit, even if the other 5 streams match perfectly.

| Step | Action | Rationale |
|:-----|:-------|:----------|
| 1 | Resample to 16kHz mono | WavLM expected input format |
| 2 | Normalize audio buffer to -3dB peak | Consistent volume levels across sessions |
| 3 | Apply Voice Activity Detection (VAD) | Ensure embedding represents speech only, not silence |
| 4 | Validate minimum duration (>= 1.0s) | Short samples produce unreliable X-Vectors |

**REQ-AUDIO-002: Minimum Duration Constraint**

If `post_vad_duration < 1.0s`, the sample MUST be discarded for identity verification purposes. Short samples produce unreliable X-Vectors.

**REQ-AUDIO-003: Preprocessing is Non-Optional**

The audio preprocessing pipeline is MANDATORY before any WavLM inference. The system MUST NOT bypass this pipeline under any circumstances.

```rust
/// CRITICAL: Audio preprocessing pipeline
/// This MUST be applied before any WavLM inference
/// Without this pipeline, 0.97 identity threshold is unreachable
pub struct AudioPreprocessor {
    /// Target sample rate (WavLM requirement)
    pub const TARGET_SAMPLE_RATE: u32 = 16000;
    /// Target channels (mono)
    pub const TARGET_CHANNELS: u8 = 1;
    /// Target normalization level
    pub const NORMALIZATION_TARGET_DB: f32 = -3.0;
    /// VAD energy threshold (frames below this are considered silence)
    pub const VAD_ENERGY_THRESHOLD: f32 = 0.01;
    /// VAD frame size (30ms at 16kHz)
    pub const VAD_FRAME_SIZE: usize = 480;
    /// Minimum post-VAD duration for identity verification (in seconds)
    pub const MIN_IDENTITY_DURATION_SECS: f32 = 1.0;
}

impl AudioPreprocessor {
    /// Full preprocessing pipeline for identity verification
    ///
    /// Steps:
    /// 1. Resample to 16kHz mono
    /// 2. Normalize to -3dB peak
    /// 3. Apply VAD to extract speech-only segments
    /// 4. Validate minimum duration
    ///
    /// Returns: Preprocessed audio ready for WavLM
    /// Error: NoSpeechDetected if VAD finds no speech
    /// Error: SilentAudio if audio is completely silent
    /// Error: InsufficientDuration if post-VAD audio < 1.0s
    pub fn preprocess_for_identity(
        &self,
        raw_audio: &AudioBuffer,
    ) -> Result<AudioBuffer, AudioError> {
        // Step 1: Resample to 16kHz mono
        let resampled = self.resample_to_16khz_mono(raw_audio)?;

        // Step 2: Normalize to -3dB peak
        let normalized = self.normalize_audio(&resampled)?;

        // Step 3: Apply VAD to extract speech-only segments
        let speech_only = self.apply_vad(&normalized)?;

        if speech_only.samples.is_empty() {
            return Err(AudioError::NoSpeechDetected);
        }

        // Step 4: Validate minimum duration for identity verification
        let duration_secs = speech_only.samples.len() as f32 / Self::TARGET_SAMPLE_RATE as f32;
        if duration_secs < Self::MIN_IDENTITY_DURATION_SECS {
            return Err(AudioError::InsufficientDuration {
                actual: duration_secs,
                required: Self::MIN_IDENTITY_DURATION_SECS,
            });
        }

        Ok(speech_only)
    }

    /// Normalize audio buffer to target dB level
    ///
    /// Target: -3dB peak amplitude
    /// Rationale: Consistent volume ensures embedding consistency across sessions
    fn normalize_audio(&self, buffer: &AudioBuffer) -> Result<AudioBuffer, AudioError> {
        let target_amplitude = 10.0_f32.powf(Self::NORMALIZATION_TARGET_DB / 20.0);
        let current_peak = buffer.samples.iter()
            .map(|s| s.abs())
            .fold(0.0_f32, f32::max);

        if current_peak < 1e-6 {
            return Err(AudioError::SilentAudio);
        }

        let gain = target_amplitude / current_peak;
        let normalized_samples: Vec<f32> = buffer.samples.iter()
            .map(|s| (s * gain).clamp(-1.0, 1.0))
            .collect();

        Ok(AudioBuffer {
            samples: normalized_samples,
            sample_rate: buffer.sample_rate,
        })
    }

    /// Apply Voice Activity Detection to extract speech-only segments
    ///
    /// Algorithm: Energy-based frame classification
    /// Frame size: 30ms (480 samples at 16kHz)
    /// Threshold: 0.01 RMS energy
    ///
    /// CRITICAL: Without VAD, silence dilutes the X-Vector embedding,
    /// making the 0.97 Weighted Composite Confidence Score unreachable.
    /// Voice similarity typically drops to ~0.85 without preprocessing.
    fn apply_vad(&self, buffer: &AudioBuffer) -> Result<AudioBuffer, AudioError> {
        let mut speech_samples = Vec::new();

        for frame in buffer.samples.chunks(Self::VAD_FRAME_SIZE) {
            // Calculate frame energy (RMS)
            let energy: f32 = frame.iter().map(|s| s * s).sum::<f32>() / frame.len() as f32;

            if energy > Self::VAD_ENERGY_THRESHOLD {
                // Frame contains speech - include it
                speech_samples.extend_from_slice(frame);
            }
            // Frames below threshold (silence) are discarded
        }

        Ok(AudioBuffer {
            samples: speech_samples,
            sample_rate: buffer.sample_rate,
        })
    }

    /// Resample audio to 16kHz mono
    fn resample_to_16khz_mono(&self, buffer: &AudioBuffer) -> Result<AudioBuffer, AudioError> {
        // Implementation using rubato or similar resampling library
        todo!()
    }
}

/// Audio error types
#[derive(Debug)]
pub enum AudioError {
    /// No speech detected after VAD processing
    NoSpeechDetected,
    /// Audio is completely silent (peak < 1e-6)
    SilentAudio,
    /// Post-VAD audio duration is below minimum threshold
    InsufficientDuration {
        actual: f32,
        required: f32,
    },
    /// Resampling failed
    ResampleError(String),
}
```

### 5.2 Vocal Biomarker Extraction

**REQ-AUDIO-004: Vocal Biomarker Extraction (cuFFT DX)**

The Audio Preprocessor MUST extract physiological signals using **cuFFT DX (Device Extensions)** running on Green Context A. This eliminates PCIe transfer latency by keeping audio in GPU memory throughout the analysis pipeline. CUDA 13.1 optimized cuFFT for small power-of-2 sizes, enabling 4096-point FFTs for medical-grade micro-tremor detection in real-time.

| Feature | Frequency Range | Inference Target |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Micro-Tremor** | 8-12 Hz | Cortisol / Stress Levels |
| **Respiration** | < 0.5 Hz | Breathing Rate / Anxiety |
| **Shimmer/Jitter** | N/A | Heart Rate Variability (HRV) |

```rust
/// Advanced DSP for Physiological Inference
pub struct BioSignalExtractor {
    /// Bandpass filter for 8-12Hz micro-tremors
    tremor_filter: IirFilter,
    /// Low-pass filter for respiration detection
    respiration_filter: IirFilter,
}

impl BioSignalExtractor {
    /// Create a new BioSignalExtractor with configured filters
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        Self {
            tremor_filter: IirFilter::bandpass(8.0, 12.0, 16000),
            respiration_filter: IirFilter::lowpass(0.5, 16000),
        }
    }

    /// Analyze audio buffer for physiological markers AND PAG features
    pub fn extract_biometrics(&self, buffer: &AudioBuffer) -> BiometricTelemetry {
        let micro_tremor_index = self.measure_tremor_intensity(buffer);
        let respiration_rate = self.detect_respiration_rate(buffer);
        let estimated_hr_bpm = self.estimate_heart_rate(buffer);

        // PAG Features
        let ibi = self.calculate_ibi(buffer);
        let (drift_velocity, drift_acceleration) = self.calculate_tonal_drift(buffer);

        BiometricTelemetry {
            estimated_hr_bpm,
            micro_tremor_index,
            respiration_rate,
            dissonance_probability: 0.0, // Calculated later by combining with Semantic Stream
            inter_breath_interval: ibi,
            tonal_drift_velocity: drift_velocity,
            tonal_drift_acceleration: drift_acceleration,
        }
    }

    /// Calculate Inter-Breath Interval (IBI)
    /// Detects inhalations in speech envelope
    /// Returns milliseconds between breath events
    fn calculate_ibi(&self, buffer: &AudioBuffer) -> f32 {
        // 1. Apply envelope detection to audio buffer
        // 2. Identify breath sounds (typically low-frequency bursts)
        // 3. Calculate time between consecutive inhalation events
        // 4. Return average IBI in milliseconds
        // Range: 400ms (High Arousal/Anger) to 2500ms (Calm)
        todo!("Implement IBI detection from speech envelope")
    }

    /// Calculate Tonal Drift (1st and 2nd derivatives of F0)
    /// Returns (velocity, acceleration) of pitch changes
    fn calculate_tonal_drift(&self, buffer: &AudioBuffer) -> (f32, f32) {
        // 1. Extract F0 contour from audio buffer via autocorrelation
        // 2. Calculate first derivative (velocity): rate of pitch change
        // 3. Calculate second derivative (acceleration): change in rate
        // 4. Return (velocity, acceleration) tuple
        // Rising fast velocity + positive acceleration = Anxiety/Anger trajectory
        todo!("Implement F0 contour derivative calculation")
    }

    /// Detect micro-tremors in the 8-12Hz range
    /// Higher values correlate with elevated cortisol/stress
    fn measure_tremor_intensity(&self, buffer: &AudioBuffer) -> f32 {
        let filtered = self.tremor_filter.apply(&buffer.samples);
        let energy: f32 = filtered.iter().map(|s| s * s).sum::<f32>() / filtered.len() as f32;
        energy.sqrt().clamp(0.0, 1.0)
    }

    /// Estimate heart rate from voice shimmer/jitter patterns
    fn estimate_heart_rate(&self, buffer: &AudioBuffer) -> f32 {
        // Analyze pitch perturbation patterns that correlate with cardiac rhythm
        let shimmer = self.calculate_shimmer(buffer);
        let jitter = self.calculate_jitter(buffer);

        // HRV estimation based on voice modulation patterns
        // Typical range: 60-100 BPM for normal adults
        let base_hr = 72.0;
        let modulation = (shimmer + jitter) * 20.0;
        (base_hr + modulation).clamp(50.0, 120.0)
    }

    /// Detect respiration rate from low-frequency amplitude modulation
    fn detect_respiration_rate(&self, buffer: &AudioBuffer) -> f32 {
        let filtered = self.respiration_filter.apply(&buffer.samples);
        // Count zero crossings to estimate breathing rate
        let zero_crossings = filtered.windows(2)
            .filter(|w| w[0].signum() != w[1].signum())
            .count();
        let duration_minutes = buffer.samples.len() as f32 / 16000.0 / 60.0;
        (zero_crossings as f32 / duration_minutes / 2.0).clamp(8.0, 30.0)
    }

    fn calculate_shimmer(&self, buffer: &AudioBuffer) -> f32 {
        // Amplitude perturbation quotient calculation
        let peaks: Vec<f32> = self.extract_peaks(&buffer.samples);
        if peaks.len() < 2 {
            return 0.0;
        }
        let diffs: f32 = peaks.windows(2)
            .map(|w| (w[1] - w[0]).abs())
            .sum();
        let mean_peak: f32 = peaks.iter().sum::<f32>() / peaks.len() as f32;
        (diffs / (peaks.len() - 1) as f32 / mean_peak).clamp(0.0, 1.0)
    }

    fn calculate_jitter(&self, buffer: &AudioBuffer) -> f32 {
        // Pitch perturbation quotient calculation
        let periods: Vec<f32> = self.extract_pitch_periods(&buffer.samples);
        if periods.len() < 2 {
            return 0.0;
        }
        let diffs: f32 = periods.windows(2)
            .map(|w| (w[1] - w[0]).abs())
            .sum();
        let mean_period: f32 = periods.iter().sum::<f32>() / periods.len() as f32;
        (diffs / (periods.len() - 1) as f32 / mean_period).clamp(0.0, 1.0)
    }

    fn extract_peaks(&self, samples: &[f32]) -> Vec<f32> {
        samples.windows(3)
            .filter_map(|w| {
                if w[1] > w[0] && w[1] > w[2] && w[1] > 0.1 {
                    Some(w[1])
                } else {
                    None
                }
            })
            .collect()
    }

    fn extract_pitch_periods(&self, samples: &[f32]) -> Vec<f32> {
        // Autocorrelation-based pitch period extraction
        let mut periods = Vec::new();
        let frame_size = 480; // 30ms at 16kHz

        for frame in samples.chunks(frame_size) {
            if let Some(period) = self.autocorrelation_pitch(frame) {
                periods.push(period);
            }
        }
        periods
    }

    fn autocorrelation_pitch(&self, frame: &[f32]) -> Option<f32> {
        // Find fundamental frequency via autocorrelation
        let min_lag = 16000 / 500; // 500Hz max
        let max_lag = 16000 / 50;  // 50Hz min

        let mut max_corr = 0.0_f32;
        let mut best_lag = 0;

        for lag in min_lag..max_lag.min(frame.len()) {
            let corr: f32 = frame.iter()
                .zip(frame.iter().skip(lag))
                .map(|(a, b)| a * b)
                .sum();
            if corr > max_corr {
                max_corr = corr;
                best_lag = lag;
            }
        }

        if max_corr > 0.3 {
            Some(best_lag as f32 / 16000.0)
        } else {
            None
        }
    }
}

/// Telemetry data from vocal biomarker extraction
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct BiometricTelemetry {
    /// Estimated Heart Rate (BPM) derived from speech rhythm and shimmer
    pub estimated_hr_bpm: f32,
    /// Voice Micro-Tremor intensity (0.0-1.0) - correlates to Cortisol levels
    pub micro_tremor_index: f32,
    /// Estimated respiration rate (breaths per minute)
    pub respiration_rate: f32,
    /// Probability user is concealing true emotion (calculated by comparing Bio vs Semantic)
    pub dissonance_probability: f32,
    // PAG Fields
    /// Inter-Breath Interval in milliseconds (400ms = High Arousal, 2500ms = Calm)
    pub inter_breath_interval: f32,
    /// First derivative of F0 contour (pitch change velocity)
    pub tonal_drift_velocity: f32,
    /// Second derivative of F0 contour (pitch change acceleration)
    pub tonal_drift_acceleration: f32,
}
```

### 5.3 The Trust Voice Protocol (Output DSP)

**REQ-AUDIO-006: Trust Voice Equalization & Dynamics**

The system MUST apply a specific DSP chain to all generated TTS audio *before* transmission to the user. This chain is scientifically calibrated to increase perceived competence, honesty, and authority ("The Trust Voice") based on Klofstad (2014) and Apicella & Feinberg studies.

This process applies to the **Output Stream** (TTS) only.

**DSP Chain Specifications:**

| Stage | Effect | Parameters | Rationale |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| **1** | High-Pass Filter | Cutoff: 85 Hz (Slope: 12dB/oct) | Removes low-end rumble/mud. |
| **2** | Low-Mid Boost (EQ) | Freq: 140 Hz, Gain: +3.0 dB, Q: 1.0 | Adds "Chest Resonance" (Warmth/Authority). |
| **3** | Presence Cut (EQ) | Freq: 3000 Hz, Gain: -3.0 dB, Q: 2.0 | Removes nasal harshness. |
| **4** | Compression | Ratio: 3:1, Threshold: -20 dB | Maintains steady volume (authority). |
| **5** | Saturation | Type: Tape/Valve Emulation, Drive: 5% | Adds analog warmth to survive phone codecs. |
| **6** | LFM Injection | γ-Glide: 17-21Hz, 350ms, Mix: -18dB | Triggered conditionally during Closing/Offers. Induces parasympathetic response. |

**REQ-AUDIO-006a: Trust Voice Logic (CUDA Tile IR Implementation)**

The Trust Voice DSP runs on Green Context A using Blackwell's Tile-based architecture. CUDA Tile IR allows processing audio chunks as single "Tiles" in SRAM, bypassing standard SIMT thread management overhead. Audio is DMA-ingested directly to GPU memory and streams from GPU memory to output, eliminating all PCIe transfer latency.

```rust
/// Trust Voice DSP Processor (CUDA Tile IR Implementation)
/// Runs on Green Context A using Blackwell Tile-based architecture.
/// Wraps a CUDA kernel that processes audio chunks as tiles in SRAM.
///
/// Pipeline: DMA Ingest → GPU Memory → Tile IR Kernel → GPU Memory → Stream Out
/// Zero PCIe transfer latency - audio never leaves GPU until final output.
pub struct TrustVoiceProcessor {
    /// Handle to the compiled CUDA Tile IR kernel
    /// Kernel implements: Load Tile → Biquad(HPF) → Biquad(Chest) → Biquad(Nasal) → Compression → Saturation → Store Tile
    tile_kernel: CudaFunction,
    /// GPU memory buffer for audio tiles (allocated on Context A)
    d_audio_buffer: DevicePointer<f32>,
    /// GPU memory for filter coefficients (baked at init, never transferred during runtime)
    d_filter_coeffs: DevicePointer<FilterCoefficients>,
    /// CUDA stream bound to Green Context A (guaranteed 10% SM allocation)
    context_a_stream: CudaStream,
}

/// Filter coefficients baked into GPU memory at initialization
/// These are computed from config and uploaded once during MemorySystem::new()
#[repr(C)]
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub struct FilterCoefficients {
    /// HPF biquad coefficients (85 Hz cutoff)
    pub hpf_coeffs: [f32; 6],
    /// Chest resonance boost coefficients (140 Hz, +3dB)
    pub chest_coeffs: [f32; 6],
    /// Nasal cut coefficients (3000 Hz, -3dB)
    pub nasal_coeffs: [f32; 6],
    /// Compression threshold (linear amplitude)
    pub comp_threshold: f32,
    /// Compression ratio (3.0 for 3:1)
    pub comp_ratio: f32,
    /// Saturation amount (0.05 for 5%)
    pub saturation_amount: f32,
    // === LFM Parameters ===
    /// LFM Start Frequency (17.0 Hz)
    pub lfm_freq_start: f32,
    /// LFM End Frequency (21.0 Hz)
    pub lfm_freq_end: f32,
    /// LFM Duration in samples (350ms @ 16kHz = 5600 samples)
    pub lfm_duration_samples: u32,
    /// LFM Mix Level (Linear amplitude for -18dB)
    pub lfm_mix_gain: f32,
}

impl TrustVoiceProcessor {
    /// Initialize Trust Voice with CUDA Tile IR kernel
    ///
    /// Loads compiled Tile IR kernel and allocates GPU memory on Context A.
    /// Filter coefficients are computed from config and baked into d_filter_coeffs.
    pub fn new(config: &TrustVoiceConfig, context_a: &GreenContext) -> CudaResult<Self> {
        // Load pre-compiled Tile IR kernel from module
        let module = CudaModule::load("cognitive-cuda/trust_voice_tile.cubin")?;
        let tile_kernel = module.get_function("trust_voice_tile_process")?;

        // Allocate audio buffer on GPU (Context A partition)
        let d_audio_buffer = context_a.alloc::<f32>(AUDIO_TILE_SIZE)?;

        // Compute and upload filter coefficients (one-time operation)
        let coeffs = FilterCoefficients::from_config(config);
        let d_filter_coeffs = context_a.alloc_and_copy(&coeffs)?;

        // Get dedicated stream for Context A
        let context_a_stream = context_a.create_stream()?;

        Ok(Self {
            tile_kernel,
            d_audio_buffer,
            d_filter_coeffs,
            context_a_stream,
        })
    }

    /// Execute the Tile IR kernel on GPU
    ///
    /// Logic executed in single fused kernel:
    /// 1. Load audio chunk as Tile into SRAM
    /// 2. Apply Biquad filter (HPF at 85Hz)
    /// 3. Apply Biquad filter (Chest Boost at 140Hz, +3dB)
    /// 4. Apply Biquad filter (Nasal Cut at 3kHz, -3dB)
    /// 5. Apply compression (3:1 ratio, -20dB threshold)
    /// 6. Apply saturation (5% tanh soft-clip)
    /// 7. [CONDITIONAL] LFM Injection:
    ///    If trigger_lfm is true, generate 17-21Hz sine sweep, apply envelope,
    ///    and mix at -18dB relative to carrier signal.
    /// 8. Store processed Tile back to GPU memory
    ///
    /// All operations occur in GPU SRAM - no memory round-trips.
    pub fn apply_trust_dsp_gpu(&mut self, trigger_lfm: bool) -> CudaResult<()> {
        unsafe {
            launch_kernel!(
                self.tile_kernel<<<1, TILE_THREADS, 0, self.context_a_stream>>>(
                    self.d_audio_buffer,
                    self.d_filter_coeffs,
                    AUDIO_TILE_SIZE as u32,
                    trigger_lfm // Pass trigger flag to kernel
                )
            )?;
        }
        self.context_a_stream.synchronize()
    }

    /// DMA ingest audio from host to GPU (async, non-blocking)
    pub fn ingest_audio_async(&mut self, host_audio: &[f32]) -> CudaResult<()> {
        self.d_audio_buffer.copy_from_host_async(host_audio, &self.context_a_stream)
    }

    /// Stream processed audio from GPU to output (async, non-blocking)
    pub fn stream_output_async(&self, host_output: &mut [f32]) -> CudaResult<()> {
        self.d_audio_buffer.copy_to_host_async(host_output, &self.context_a_stream)
    }
}

/// Audio tile size for CUDA Tile IR processing
/// Matches audio frame buffer for single-tile processing
const AUDIO_TILE_SIZE: usize = 1024;
/// Thread count for tile processing
const TILE_THREADS: u32 = 256;
```

### 5.4 Voice Phase Coherence Engine (VPCE)

**REQ-AUDIO-007: Phase-Locked Loop Implementation**

The system MUST maintain acoustic synchrony by phase-locking the TTS output to the user's most recent speech rhythm. This is executed on **Green Context A** using CUDA Tile IR.

**Phase Coherence Formula:**
$\Phi = |⟨e^{i\theta_{AI}} \times e^{-i\theta_{recipient}}⟩|$

**Logic Flow:**
1.  **Extraction:** Stream B extracts recipient F0 and Instantaneous Phase ($\theta_{recipient}$) using cuFFT DX Hilbert Transform.
2.  **Calculation:** Compute phase angle delta between recipient tail and TTS head.
3.  **Adjustment:** Apply micro-timing shift ($\pm 50ms$) to TTS onset via ring buffer pointer manipulation in GPU SRAM.
4.  **Modulation:** Modulate TTS F0 contour to harmonic of recipient F0 if $\Phi < 0.6$.

**REQ-AUDIO-007a: VPCE Processor Struct**

```rust
/// Voice Phase Coherence Engine
/// Runs on Green Context A. Manages phase-locking between input audio tail
/// and output TTS head.
pub struct VpceProcessor {
    /// Target phase coherence threshold (0.85)
    coherence_threshold: f32,
    /// Ring buffer for micro-timing delays
    delay_line: DevicePointer<f32>,
    /// Last known user phase angle
    last_user_phase: f32,
}

impl VpceProcessor {
    /// Adjust TTS buffer to align phase with user
    /// Returns the calculated Phase Coherence Coefficient ($\Phi$)
    pub fn align_phase(
        &mut self,
        tts_audio: &mut [f32],
        user_f0: &[f32],
        user_phase: f32
    ) -> f32 {

        // 1. Calculate phase delta
        // 2. Determine required micro-shift (max +/- 50ms)
        // 3. Apply shift via circular buffer offset
        // 4. Return predicted coherence score
        todo!("CUDA Tile IR Phase Locked Loop implementation")
    }
}
```
