## 6. Profiling & Discovery

### 6.1 The 60-Second Safe Harbor (Cold Start)

**REQ-PROFILE-001: Safe Harbor Protocol**

The system MUST operate in a deterministic "Discovery Mode" until sufficient data is collected. During Safe Harbor, the system accumulates all 6 streams (Semantic, Tone, Emotion, Style, Action, Chronemic) into rolling buffers to establish the **User's Individual Embedding Vectors** (the 5-vector combination) at T=60s.

**CRITICAL**: The Physics Engine MUST NOT attempt archetype calculation or goal-driven behavior during Safe Harbor. Any attempt to lock an archetype before T=60s MUST trigger a `SafeHarborViolation` error. This prevents the system from "guessing" user psychology with insufficient data.

| Parameter | Value | Rationale |
|:----------|:------|:----------|
| **Duration** | 0 to 60 seconds | Fixed discovery window |
| **Physics Profile** | Hardcoded Gamma = 0.1 | Extremely low goal pressure - HARDCODED, NON-CONFIGURABLE |
| **Entropy Tolerance** | 0.9 | Maximum patience during calibration |
| **Coherence Requirement** | 0.2 | Not demanding agreement during discovery |
| **Strategy** | "Mirror & Acknowledge" only | Do NOT attempt to close or persuade |
| **Archetype Assumption** | NeutralBenevolent | Default assumption until classification |
| **TTS Style** | EmpatheticCalm | Non-threatening voice during discovery |
| **Calculation** | Accumulate 6 Streams into rolling buffer | Build User Position Vectors for archetype identification |

```rust
/// CRITICAL: Safe Harbor Configuration
/// These parameters MUST be used when T < 60s
/// DO NOT MODIFY these values - they are carefully calibrated
/// to prevent cold-start hallucinations
pub const SAFE_HARBOR_PROFILE: SafeHarborConfig = SafeHarborConfig {
    gamma: 0.1,                    // Minimal goal pressure - HARDCODED, DO NOT CHANGE
    entropy_tolerance: 0.9,        // Maximum patience - allows conversation to unfold
    coherence_requirement: 0.2,    // Not demanding agreement - reduces pushback
    archetype: ArchetypeAssumption::NeutralBenevolent,
    tts_style: TtsStyleId::EmpatheticCalm,
};

/// Fixed Safe Harbor duration in seconds
/// The system MUST NOT attempt archetype lock before this threshold
pub const SAFE_HARBOR_DURATION_SECONDS: u64 = 60;

/// Check if Safe Harbor violation would occur
/// Returns true if attempting archetype lock before T=60s
pub fn would_violate_safe_harbor(elapsed_seconds: u64) -> bool {
    elapsed_seconds < SAFE_HARBOR_DURATION_SECONDS
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub struct SafeHarborConfig {
    pub gamma: f32,
    pub entropy_tolerance: f32,
    pub coherence_requirement: f32,
    pub archetype: ArchetypeAssumption,
    pub tts_style: TtsStyleId,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub enum ArchetypeAssumption {
    NeutralBenevolent,  // Default during Safe Harbor
    Classified(ArchetypeId),
}

/// Rolling buffer for all 6 streams during Safe Harbor
/// Purpose: Accumulate hexa-modal vectors to determine **User Position Vectors** in all 5 embedding spaces at T=60s.
/// **NOTE**: The user does NOT have a centroid. Each embedding space is independent with different dimensions and models.
#[derive(Debug)]
pub struct SafeHarborBuffer {
    /// Timestamp when Safe Harbor started
    pub start_time: Instant,
    /// Stream A: Semantic vectors from Nomic (768-dim)
    pub semantic_vectors: Vec<[f32; 768]>,
    /// Stream B: Tone vectors from WavLM (512-dim)
    pub tone_vectors: Vec<[f32; 512]>,
    /// Stream C: Emotion vectors from Wav2Vec2 (1024-dim)
    pub emotion_vectors: Vec<[f32; 1024]>,
    /// Stream D: Style scalars from RoBERTa Formality (0.0-1.0)
    pub style_scalars: Vec<f32>,
    /// Stream E: Action logits from BERT Dialog Act (42 classes)
    pub action_logits: Vec<[f32; 42]>,
    /// Stream F: Chronemic vectors [wpm, latency, jitter, overlap_ratio]
    pub chronemic_vectors: Vec<[f32; 4]>,
    /// Gender votes from each turn (for majority voting at T=60s)
    pub gender_votes: Vec<Gender>,
}

impl SafeHarborBuffer {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        Self {
            start_time: Instant::now(),
            semantic_vectors: Vec::with_capacity(20),
            tone_vectors: Vec::with_capacity(20),
            emotion_vectors: Vec::with_capacity(20),
            style_scalars: Vec::with_capacity(20),
            action_logits: Vec::with_capacity(20),
            chronemic_vectors: Vec::with_capacity(20),
            gender_votes: Vec::with_capacity(20),
        }
    }

    /// Accumulate a full cognitive state snapshot into the rolling buffers
    ///
    /// **Gender Accumulation**: The detected_gender from each turn is accumulated
    /// into gender_votes for majority voting at T=60s archetype lock.
    pub fn accumulate(&mut self, state: &CognitiveState) {
        self.semantic_vectors.push(state.semantic_embedding);
        self.tone_vectors.push(state.x_vector);
        self.emotion_vectors.push(state.emotion_embedding);
        self.style_scalars.push(state.style_score);
        self.action_logits.push(state.dialog_acts);
        self.chronemic_vectors.push(state.chronemics);
        self.gender_votes.push(state.detected_gender);
    }

    /// Check if Safe Harbor period has elapsed
    pub fn is_expired(&self) -> bool {
        self.start_time.elapsed().as_secs() >= SAFE_HARBOR_DURATION_SECONDS
    }

    /// Check if sufficient data has been collected for triangulation
    pub fn has_sufficient_data(&self) -> bool {
        self.semantic_vectors.len() >= 3 &&
        self.tone_vectors.len() >= 3 &&
        self.emotion_vectors.len() >= 3 &&
        self.style_scalars.len() >= 3 &&
        self.action_logits.len() >= 3 &&
        self.chronemic_vectors.len() >= 3
    }
}
```

**REQ-PROFILE-001a: System Behavior During Safe Harbor**

The system MUST exhibit the following behaviors during the Safe Harbor period:

| Behavior | Specification |
|:---------|:--------------|
| **Goal Pressure** | NONE - do not push toward any outcome |
| **Response Style** | Empathetic, calm, non-judgmental |
| **Question Type** | Open-ended questions only |
| **Mirroring** | Match user's energy level and pace |
| **Persuasion** | PROHIBITED - do not sell, close, or convince |
| **Data Collection** | Silently accumulate all 6 streams |

**System Prompt During Safe Harbor:**

```
You are currently calibrating to the user. Be helpful, concise, and non-judgmental.
Do not push for a decision. Do not close. Do not sell.
Your only goal is to understand who you are speaking with.
Ask open-ended questions. Mirror their energy level.
```

**REQ-PROFILE-001b: Safe Harbor Exit Conditions**

The system exits Safe Harbor when EITHER of the following conditions are met:

| Exit Path | Condition | Behavior |
|:----------|:----------|:---------|
| **Standard Exit** | T >= 60 seconds AND >= 3 vectors in each buffer AND valid speech detected | Calculate archetype from buffer, then lock |
| **Fast-Track Exit** | **Weighted Composite Confidence Score** > 0.97 | Hydrate buffer from historical profile, calculate archetype, then lock immediately |

**REQ-PROFILE-001c: Fast-Track Profile Hydration**

If `IdentityResult::Verified` is returned with `historical_profile` data, the system MUST:

1. **Hydrate** the `SafeHarborBuffer` using the `historical_profile` from LanceDB.
2. **Trigger** immediate archetype identification (buffer now has sufficient vector data for the 5-space comparison).
3. **Exit** Safe Harbor mode instantly (regardless of elapsed time).

This enables returning users to be served with their personalized archetype profile on the **first turn** of a new session.

```rust
impl SafeHarborBuffer {
    /// Hydrate buffer with historical data for immediate Safe Harbor exit
    ///
    /// Called when Identity Verification succeeds with historical_profile.
    /// Populates all 6 stream buffers with user's **historical position data**,
    /// satisfying the "sufficient data" check and enabling instant archetype lock.
    ///
    /// INPUTS: ProfileSnapshot from LanceDB (user's last known position vectors)
    /// SIDE EFFECTS: Buffer now contains >= 3 vectors per stream (synthetic copies)
    /// POST-CONDITION: has_sufficient_data() returns true
    ///
    /// **Gender Hydration**: The historical gender is also hydrated to provide
    /// consistent gender votes for majority voting.
    pub fn hydrate_from_history(&mut self, historical: &ProfileSnapshot) {
        // Push 3 copies (minimum required) to satisfy "sufficient data" check instantly
        // This enables immediate archetype identification without waiting for 60s
        for _ in 0..3 {
            self.semantic_vectors.push(historical.semantic_vector);
            self.tone_vectors.push(historical.tone_vector);
            self.emotion_vectors.push(historical.emotion_vector);
            self.style_scalars.push(historical.style_score);
            self.action_logits.push(historical.action_logits);
            self.chronemic_vectors.push(historical.chronemics);
            self.gender_votes.push(historical.gender);
        }
    }

    /// Check if buffer was hydrated from historical profile
    ///
    /// Returns true if buffer was populated via hydrate_from_history()
    /// Used to distinguish Fast-Track exits from Standard exits for metrics.
    pub fn was_hydrated(&self) -> bool {
        // If we have exactly 3 identical vectors, it was hydrated
        self.semantic_vectors.len() == 3 &&
        self.semantic_vectors[0] == self.semantic_vectors[1] &&
        self.semantic_vectors[1] == self.semantic_vectors[2]
    }
}
```

### 6.2 Archetype Lock (T > 60s OR Fast-Track)

**REQ-PROFILE-002a: The North Star Reference System (5-Vector Combination)**

The "North Star Reference Set" is the fundamental unit of measurement for the Cognitive Radar. It is **not** a strategy; it is a **fixed set of reference vectors** across all 5 embedding spaces.

1.  **Definition**: A North Star Reference Set is a collection of 5 distinct reference vectors—one per embedding space—representing the expected position of a specific personality trait or VAK modality in each of the 5 independent embedding spaces (Semantic 768-dim, Tone 512-dim, Emotion 1024-dim, Style scalar, Action 42-dim).
2.  **Derivation**: These reference vectors are pre-computed by taking actual recordings of humans who have been verified to match specific profiles (e.g., a "Power" archetype or "Visual" learner) and embedding their statements/vocal tone in each space.
3.  **Function**: The system measures where the user ends up in all 5 embedding spaces and compares that position to the preset North Star Reference Sets. **The user does NOT have a centroid.** Each embedding space is independent with different dimensions and models.

**REQ-PROFILE-002: Archetype Identification at T=60s (5-Vector Combination)**

At T=60s, the system identifies the user's personality profile based on where they land in 5 independent embedding spaces. **There is no centroid.**

**Logic (The 5-Vector Combination):**
1.  The system calculates the user's average vector for: Semantic, Tone, Emotion, Style, and Action.
2.  It compares this array of 5 vectors against the pre-loaded **North Star Reference Sets**.
3.  **Example Logic:**
    - If the "Truth and Power" Reference Set consists of vector coordinates corresponding to sectors `[2, 8, 9, 3, 4]` in the 5 spaces...
    - And the "Innovation" Reference Set corresponds to sectors `[1, 3, 9, 2, 4]`...
    - And the **User's Position Vectors** land at `[3, 8, 9, 3, 4]`...
    - Then the system matches the user to **Truth and Power** because their 5-vector combination is mathematically closest to that Reference Set.
4.  The profile is identified by finding the Reference Set with the minimum cumulative distance across all 5 spaces.

| Step | Action | Output |
|:-----|:-------|:-------|
| 1 | **Aggregate User Position Vectors** for each of the 5 streams (average of buffer values in each embedding space) | 5 independent position vectors |
| 2 | Load pre-computed North Star Reference Vectors (derived from actual profile recordings) for all Archetypes and VAKs | Reference rulers per embedding space |
| 3 | **Proximity check between User Vectors and North Star Reference Vectors** within each specific embedding space | Weighted similarity scores |
| 4 | Select Top 2 Archetypes (Primary/Secondary) based on highest aggregate proximity | Profile lock |
| 5 | Detect VAK Modality by calculating proximity to **VAK North Star Reference Vectors** combined with Semantic keywords and Chronemic pace analysis | Modality classification |
| 6 | Adopt Complementary Archetype using weighted behavioral blend | Behavior profile |

**Weighted Distance Formula:**

```
Distance = (SemDist * 0.20) + (ToneDist * 0.20) + (StyleDist * 0.15) +
           (ActionDist * 0.15) + (ChronDist * 0.15) + (EmoDist * 0.15)
```

| Weight | Stream | Model | Rationale |
|:-------|:-------|:------|:----------|
| 0.20 | Semantic (A) | Nomic | What they say reveals intent |
| 0.20 | Tone (B) | WavLM | How they sound reveals identity |
| 0.15 | Style (D) | RoBERTa Formality | Formality signals power distance |
| 0.15 | Action (E) | BERT Dialog Act | Speech acts reveal communication pattern |
| 0.15 | Chronemic (F) | Audio Timestamps | Timing reveals cognitive pace |
| 0.15 | Emotion (C) | Wav2Vec2 | Emotional state modulates all above |

**REQ-PROFILE-003: 5-Vector Combination Definition**

| Concept | Definition |
|:--------|:-----------|
| **5-Vector Combination** | The array of 5 independent vectors (Semantic 768-dim, Tone 512-dim, Emotion 1024-dim, Style scalar, Action 42-dim) used to define a user's position or an Archetype's reference point. No centroid is calculated. |
| **User Position Set** | The set of 5 distinct vectors representing the user's position in each embedding space. **No single centroid exists.** Each embedding space is independent with different dimensions and models. |
| **North Star Reference Set** | The collection of 5 reference vectors that define a specific Archetype across the 5 independent embedding spaces. Each archetype has 5 reference vectors—one per embedding space. |
| **Relationship** | `Profile = NearestMatch(Set<UserVector>, Set<NorthStarReferenceVectors>)` |
| **Input** | 5 stream buffers accumulated over 60 seconds (Semantic, Tone, Emotion, Style, Action) + Chronemic for VAK |
| **Output** | Primary Archetype, Secondary Archetype, VAK Modality |

**REQ-PROFILE-004: VAK Detection Formula**

VAK (Visual/Auditory/Kinesthetic) modality is detected by combining:
1. **Semantic Stream (A)**: Scan for VAK keywords in transcript
2. **Chronemic Stream (F)**: Analyze speech timing patterns

```rust
/// VAK Detection Logic
/// Visual: "see", "look", "picture", "bright" + faster pace (>150 wpm)
/// Auditory: "hear", "sounds", "tell", "tune" + moderate pace (120-150 wpm)
/// Kinesthetic: "feel", "touch", "grasp", "solid" + slower pace (<120 wpm)
pub fn detect_vak_modality(
    semantic_keywords: &VakKeywordCounts,
    chronemics: &ChronemicAverage,
) -> VakType {
    let visual_score = semantic_keywords.visual as f32 + pace_visual_bonus(chronemics.wpm);
    let auditory_score = semantic_keywords.auditory as f32 + pace_auditory_bonus(chronemics.wpm);
    let kinesthetic_score = semantic_keywords.kinesthetic as f32 + pace_kinesthetic_bonus(chronemics.wpm);

    if visual_score >= auditory_score && visual_score >= kinesthetic_score {
        VakType::Visual
    } else if auditory_score >= kinesthetic_score {
        VakType::Auditory
    } else {
        VakType::Kinesthetic
    }
}

fn pace_visual_bonus(wpm: f32) -> f32 {
    // Visual processors tend to speak faster (>150 wpm)
    if wpm > 150.0 { 2.0 } else { 0.0 }
}

fn pace_auditory_bonus(wpm: f32) -> f32 {
    // Auditory processors speak at moderate pace (120-150 wpm)
    if wpm >= 120.0 && wpm <= 150.0 { 2.0 } else { 0.0 }
}

fn pace_kinesthetic_bonus(wpm: f32) -> f32 {
    // Kinesthetic processors speak slower (<120 wpm)
    if wpm < 120.0 { 2.0 } else { 0.0 }
}
```

**REQ-PROFILE-005: Behavioral Blend Formula**

```rust
/// The system adopts the Complementary Archetype using this weighted blend:
/// Behavior = (Primary_Complement * 0.7) + (Secondary_Complement * 0.3)
pub fn calculate_behavioral_blend(
    primary: &ArchetypeBehavior,
    secondary: &ArchetypeBehavior,
) -> BehavioralProfile {
    BehavioralProfile {
        assertiveness: primary.assertiveness * 0.7 + secondary.assertiveness * 0.3,
        warmth: primary.warmth * 0.7 + secondary.warmth * 0.3,
        pace: primary.pace * 0.7 + secondary.pace * 0.3,
        formality: primary.formality * 0.7 + secondary.formality * 0.3,
    }
}
```

**REQ-PROFILE-006: Archetype Classification Implementation**

**Hybrid-Metric Alignment Protocol:**

The system uses a **Hybrid-Metric Strategy** where each stream uses the mathematically correct distance metric for its data topology. All outputs are normalized to a 0.0 to 1.0 scalar before being weighted and summed.

| Stream | Data Type | Metric | Rationale |
|:-------|:----------|:-------|:----------|
| A (Semantic) | 768-dim dense vector | Cosine Distance | Direction/quality matters more than magnitude |
| B (Tone) | 512-dim dense vector | Cosine Distance | Direction/quality matters more than magnitude |
| C (Emotion) | 1024-dim dense vector | Cosine Distance | Direction/quality matters more than magnitude |
| D (Style) | Scalar (0.0-1.0) | Manhattan Distance | Linear scale, absolute difference |
| E (Action) | 42-dim probability vector | Cosine Distance | Robust approximation for probability similarity |
| F (Chronemic) | 4-dim physical measurements | Euclidean Distance | Magnitude of pace/latency matters (requires pre-normalization) |

**CRITICAL**: Stream F (Chronemic) inputs MUST be pre-normalized via Z-score against Cultural Baseline before reaching this function. Raw values (ms, wpm) have vastly different scales that would break Euclidean distance calculation.

```rust
impl ProfilingEngine {
    /// Calculate archetype from accumulated hexa-modal data
    ///
    /// Called when T >= 60s OR on Fast-Track exit with historical profile hydration.
    ///
    /// **Gender-Aware Archetype Classification:**
    /// The function determines the user's consensus gender from the accumulated gender_votes
    /// buffer using majority voting, then passes this gender to `calculate_weighted_distance`
    /// for gender-specific reference vector selection (tone_male/tone_female, emotion_male/emotion_female).
    pub fn calculate_archetype(
        &self,
        buffer: &SafeHarborBuffer,
    ) -> Result<ArchetypeClassification, ProfileError> {
        if !buffer.has_sufficient_data() {
            return Err(ProfileError::InsufficientData);
        }

        // Step 1: Compute User Position Vectors for all 5 embedding spaces
        // NOTE: The user does NOT have a single centroid. Each embedding space is independent
        // with different dimensions and models (768, 512, 1024, 1, 42).
        let user_position = UserPosition {
            semantic: self.compute_mean_768(&buffer.semantic_vectors),
            tone: self.compute_mean_512(&buffer.tone_vectors),
            emotion: self.compute_mean_1024(&buffer.emotion_vectors),
            style: self.compute_mean_scalar(&buffer.style_scalars),
            action: self.compute_mean_42(&buffer.action_logits),
            chronemic: self.compute_mean_4(&buffer.chronemic_vectors),
        };

        // Step 1a: Determine Consensus Gender via Majority Voting on gender_votes buffer
        // Each turn's gender classification is accumulated; take majority vote for final decision
        let consensus_gender = self.calculate_consensus_gender(&buffer.gender_votes);

        // Step 2: Load North Star Reference Sets and calculate weighted distances
        // CRITICAL: Pass consensus_gender for gender-specific reference vector selection
        let mut distances: Vec<(ArchetypeId, f32)> = self.north_star_reference_sets
            .iter()
            .map(|(id, north_star)| {
                let distance = self.calculate_weighted_distance(&user_position, north_star, consensus_gender);
                (*id, distance)
            })
            .collect();

        // Sort by distance (ascending - shortest distance = best match)
        distances.sort_by(|a, b| a.1.partial_cmp(&b.1).unwrap());

        // Step 3: Identify Primary and Secondary
        let primary = distances[0].0;
        let secondary = distances[1].0;

        // Step 4: Detect VAK Modality
        let vak_keywords = self.extract_vak_keywords(&buffer.semantic_vectors);
        let chronemic_avg = self.compute_chronemic_average(&buffer.chronemic_vectors);
        let vak_modality = detect_vak_modality(&vak_keywords, &chronemic_avg);

        let confidence = self.calculate_confidence(&distances);

        Ok(ArchetypeClassification {
            primary,
            secondary,
            vak_modality,
            confidence,
            vector_count: buffer.semantic_vectors.len(),
            detected_gender: consensus_gender,
        })
    }

    /// Calculate consensus gender from accumulated gender votes via majority voting
    ///
    /// Takes the gender_votes buffer (accumulated from each turn's gender classification)
    /// and returns the gender with the most votes. This provides robust gender detection
    /// by aggregating multiple per-turn classifications.
    ///
    /// **Majority Vote Logic:**
    /// - Count Male and Female votes from the buffer
    /// - Return the gender with the higher count
    /// - Ties default to Male (arbitrary tie-breaker)
    fn calculate_consensus_gender(&self, gender_votes: &[Gender]) -> Gender {
        let male_votes = gender_votes.iter().filter(|&&g| g == Gender::Male).count();
        let female_votes = gender_votes.len() - male_votes;

        if male_votes >= female_votes {
            Gender::Male
        } else {
            Gender::Female
        }
    }

    /// Calculate Weighted Distance between User Position and North Star Reference Set
    /// with Gender-Switched Audio Vectors
    ///
    /// Calculates the cumulative distance between the user's 5-vector combination and
    /// a North Star Reference Set to determine which archetype matches the user.
    ///
    /// **GENDER-SPECIFIC VECTOR SELECTION:**
    /// For audio-based streams (Tone, Emotion), the function selects the appropriate
    /// gender-specific reference vector based on the user's detected gender.
    /// This prevents acoustic averaging and improves classification accuracy.
    ///
    /// METRIC STRATEGY:
    /// - High-Dim Vectors (Semantic, Tone, Emotion, Action): Cosine Distance (1 - Sim)
    ///   *Rationale*: Direction/Quality matters more than magnitude.
    /// - Scalar (Style): Manhattan Distance (Absolute Difference)
    ///   *Rationale*: Linear scale from 0.0 to 1.0.
    /// - Physical (Chronemic): Euclidean Distance on Normalized Data
    ///   *Rationale*: Magnitude of pace/latency matters.
    ///
    /// NORMALIZATION:
    /// All sub-distances are clamped to 0.0-1.0 range to ensure weights are respected.
    fn calculate_weighted_distance(
        &self,
        user: &UserPosition,
        north_star: &NorthStarReferenceSet,
        user_gender: Gender,
    ) -> f32 {
        // 1. Select Gender-Specific Reference Vectors for Audio Streams
        let (target_tone, target_emotion) = match user_gender {
            Gender::Male => (&north_star.tone_male, &north_star.emotion_male),
            Gender::Female => (&north_star.tone_female, &north_star.emotion_female),
        };

        // 2. Calculate Distances

        // A (Semantic) - Unified (Gender Neutral)
        // Range: 0.0 (Identical) to 1.0 (Orthogonal/Opposite)
        let sem_dist = (1.0 - cosine_similarity_768(&user.semantic, &north_star.semantic)).clamp(0.0, 1.0);

        // B (Tone) - Gender Switched
        let tone_dist = (1.0 - cosine_similarity_512(&user.tone, target_tone)).clamp(0.0, 1.0);

        // C (Emotion) - Gender Switched
        let emo_dist = (1.0 - cosine_similarity_1024(&user.emotion, target_emotion)).clamp(0.0, 1.0);

        // D (Style) - Unified (Gender Neutral)
        // |User - Target|
        let style_dist = (user.style - north_star.style).abs().clamp(0.0, 1.0);

        // E (Action) - Unified (Gender Neutral)
        // Although these are probs, Cosine is robust approximation for similarity
        let action_dist = (1.0 - cosine_similarity_42(&user.action, &north_star.action)).clamp(0.0, 1.0);

        // F (Chronemic) - Unified (Gender Neutral)
        // CRITICAL: Inputs MUST be pre-normalized (z-scored) against Cultural Baseline
        // or this distance will be dominated by Latency_ms.
        // We clamp at 1.0 to prevent outlier variance from breaking the weighted sum.
        let chron_dist = euclidean_distance_4(&user.chronemic, &north_star.chronemic).min(1.0);

        // Weighted Sum (Weights sum to 1.0)
        (sem_dist * 0.20) +
        (tone_dist * 0.20) +
        (style_dist * 0.15) +
        (action_dist * 0.15) +
        (chron_dist * 0.15) +
        (emo_dist * 0.15)
    }

    fn compute_mean_768(&self, vectors: &[[f32; 768]]) -> [f32; 768] {
        let mut mean = [0.0f32; 768];
        let n = vectors.len() as f32;
        for v in vectors {
            for i in 0..768 { mean[i] += v[i] / n; }
        }
        l2_normalize_768(&mean)
    }

    fn compute_mean_512(&self, vectors: &[[f32; 512]]) -> [f32; 512] {
        let mut mean = [0.0f32; 512];
        let n = vectors.len() as f32;
        for v in vectors {
            for i in 0..512 { mean[i] += v[i] / n; }
        }
        l2_normalize_512(&mean)
    }

    fn compute_mean_1024(&self, vectors: &[[f32; 1024]]) -> [f32; 1024] {
        let mut mean = [0.0f32; 1024];
        let n = vectors.len() as f32;
        for v in vectors {
            for i in 0..1024 { mean[i] += v[i] / n; }
        }
        l2_normalize_1024(&mean)
    }

    fn compute_mean_scalar(&self, scalars: &[f32]) -> f32 {
        scalars.iter().sum::<f32>() / scalars.len() as f32
    }

    fn compute_mean_42(&self, vectors: &[[f32; 42]]) -> [f32; 42] {
        let mut mean = [0.0f32; 42];
        let n = vectors.len() as f32;
        for v in vectors {
            for i in 0..42 { mean[i] += v[i] / n; }
        }
        mean
    }

    fn compute_mean_4(&self, vectors: &[[f32; 4]]) -> [f32; 4] {
        let mut mean = [0.0f32; 4];
        let n = vectors.len() as f32;
        for v in vectors {
            for i in 0..4 { mean[i] += v[i] / n; }
        }
        mean
    }

    fn calculate_confidence(&self, distances: &[(ArchetypeId, f32)]) -> f32 {
        let best = distances[0].1;
        let second = distances[1].1;
        let rest_avg: f32 = distances[2..].iter().map(|(_, d)| d).sum::<f32>()
            / (distances.len() - 2) as f32;

        // Confidence = how much closer best is vs. alternatives
        ((rest_avg - best) / (second - best + 0.01)).clamp(0.0, 1.0)
    }
}

/// Cosine similarity for 768-dimensional vectors
/// Returns value in range [-1.0, 1.0] where 1.0 = identical direction
#[inline]
fn cosine_similarity_768(a: &[f32; 768], b: &[f32; 768]) -> f32 {
    let mut dot: f32 = 0.0;
    let mut norm_a: f32 = 0.0;
    let mut norm_b: f32 = 0.0;

    for i in 0..768 {
        dot += a[i] * b[i];
        norm_a += a[i] * a[i];
        norm_b += b[i] * b[i];
    }

    dot / (norm_a.sqrt() * norm_b.sqrt() + 1e-8)
}

/// Cosine similarity for 512-dimensional vectors
#[inline]
fn cosine_similarity_512(a: &[f32; 512], b: &[f32; 512]) -> f32 {
    let mut dot: f32 = 0.0;
    let mut norm_a: f32 = 0.0;
    let mut norm_b: f32 = 0.0;

    for i in 0..512 {
        dot += a[i] * b[i];
        norm_a += a[i] * a[i];
        norm_b += b[i] * b[i];
    }

    dot / (norm_a.sqrt() * norm_b.sqrt() + 1e-8)
}

/// Cosine similarity for 1024-dimensional vectors
#[inline]
fn cosine_similarity_1024(a: &[f32; 1024], b: &[f32; 1024]) -> f32 {
    let mut dot: f32 = 0.0;
    let mut norm_a: f32 = 0.0;
    let mut norm_b: f32 = 0.0;

    for i in 0..1024 {
        dot += a[i] * b[i];
        norm_a += a[i] * a[i];
        norm_b += b[i] * b[i];
    }

    dot / (norm_a.sqrt() * norm_b.sqrt() + 1e-8)
}

/// Cosine similarity for 42-dimensional vectors (Action logits)
#[inline]
fn cosine_similarity_42(a: &[f32; 42], b: &[f32; 42]) -> f32 {
    let mut dot: f32 = 0.0;
    let mut norm_a: f32 = 0.0;
    let mut norm_b: f32 = 0.0;

    for i in 0..42 {
        dot += a[i] * b[i];
        norm_a += a[i] * a[i];
        norm_b += b[i] * b[i];
    }

    dot / (norm_a.sqrt() * norm_b.sqrt() + 1e-8)
}

/// Euclidean distance for 4-dimensional vectors (Chronemic)
/// CRITICAL: Input vectors MUST be pre-normalized (z-scored) for valid results
#[inline]
fn euclidean_distance_4(a: &[f32; 4], b: &[f32; 4]) -> f32 {
    let mut sum: f32 = 0.0;
    for i in 0..4 {
        let diff = a[i] - b[i];
        sum += diff * diff;
    }
    sum.sqrt()
}

/// The user's position vectors across all 5 independent embedding spaces.
/// **NOTE**: The user does NOT have a single centroid. Each embedding space is independent
/// with different dimensions and models. This struct stores the user's position in each space.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct UserPosition {
    pub semantic: [f32; 768],
    pub tone: [f32; 512],
    pub emotion: [f32; 1024],
    pub style: f32,
    pub action: [f32; 42],
    pub chronemic: [f32; 4],
}

/// Pre-computed North Star Reference Set for each archetype.
/// Contains reference vectors for all embedding spaces, with gender-specific
/// vectors for audio streams (Tone, Emotion) and unified vectors for text streams.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
pub struct NorthStarReferenceSet {
    pub archetype_id: ArchetypeId,

    // === Shared Streams (Gender Neutral) ===
    /// Stream A: Semantic reference vector (768-dim Nomic)
    pub semantic: [f32; 768],
    /// Stream D: Style reference value (formality scalar 0.0-1.0)
    pub style: f32,
    /// Stream E: Action reference vector (42-dim dialog act probabilities)
    pub action: [f32; 42],
    /// Stream F: Chronemic reference vector (4-dim timing features)
    pub chronemic: [f32; 4],

    // === Gender-Specific Audio Streams ===
    /// Stream B (Male): Tone reference vector derived from male voice samples
    pub tone_male: [f32; 512],
    /// Stream B (Female): Tone reference vector derived from female voice samples
    pub tone_female: [f32; 512],

    /// Stream C (Male): Emotion reference vector derived from male voice samples
    pub emotion_male: [f32; 1024],
    /// Stream C (Female): Emotion reference vector derived from female voice samples
    pub emotion_female: [f32; 1024],
}

/// Gender classification for audio stream processing
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
pub enum Gender {
    Male,
    Female,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ArchetypeClassification {
    pub primary: ArchetypeId,
    pub secondary: ArchetypeId,
    pub vak_modality: VakType,
    pub confidence: f32,
    pub vector_count: usize,
    /// Detected gender of the user (determined via majority voting on tone vectors)
    pub detected_gender: Gender,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
pub enum VakType {
    Visual,
    Auditory,
    Kinesthetic,
}

impl VakType {
    pub fn description(&self) -> &'static str {
        match self {
            VakType::Visual => "visual imagery and sight-based language",
            VakType::Auditory => "sound-based language and verbal processing",
            VakType::Kinesthetic => "feeling-based language and tactile references",
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.3 The Aegis Protocol (Dark Triad Defense)

**REQ-PROFILE-007: Dark Triad Detection**

The system MUST analyze the `Semantic` and `Action` streams for malicious psychological patterns.

| Trait | Detection Signal |
|:---|:---|
| **Narcissism** | High frequency of "I/Me/My" + Demand for high-status archetypes + Low Empathy |
| **Machiavellianism** | Rapid archetype shifting (probing for weakness) + Inconsistent emotional signaling |
| **Psychopathy** | High Coherence + Low Arousal during emotionally charged topics (Flat Affect) |

```rust
/// Dark Triad detection scores
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct DarkTriadScore {
    /// Narcissism score (0.0-1.0)
    pub narcissism: f32,
    /// Machiavellianism score (0.0-1.0)
    pub machiavellianism: f32,
    /// Psychopathy score (0.0-1.0)
    pub psychopathy: f32,
    /// Combined weighted score
    pub combined_score: f32,
}

impl DarkTriadScore {
    /// Calculate combined Dark Triad score
    /// Weighted: Machiavellianism (0.6) + Narcissism (0.4)
    /// Psychopathy is flagged separately due to different intervention requirements
    pub fn calculate_combined(&self) -> f32 {
        (self.narcissism * 0.4) + (self.machiavellianism * 0.6)
    }
}

/// Dark Triad detector analyzing semantic and behavioral patterns
pub struct DarkTriadDetector {
    /// Self-reference keywords for narcissism detection
    self_reference_keywords: Vec<&'static str>,
    /// Historical archetype shifts for Machiavellianism detection
    archetype_history: Vec<(ArchetypeId, u64)>,
    /// Emotional baseline for flat affect detection
    emotional_baseline: Option<f32>,
}

impl DarkTriadDetector {
    const SELF_REFERENCE_KEYWORDS: &'static [&'static str] = &[
        "i", "me", "my", "mine", "myself", "i'm", "i've", "i'll", "i'd"
    ];

    /// Detect narcissism from semantic content
    fn detect_narcissism(&self, semantic_embedding: &[f32; 768], transcript: &str) -> f32 {
        let lower = transcript.to_lowercase();
        let words: Vec<&str> = lower.split_whitespace().collect();
        let total_words = words.len() as f32;

        if total_words < 5.0 {
            return 0.0;
        }

        // Count self-references
        let self_refs = words.iter()
            .filter(|w| Self::SELF_REFERENCE_KEYWORDS.contains(w))
            .count() as f32;

        // High self-reference ratio indicates narcissism
        let self_ratio = self_refs / total_words;

        // Normalize to 0.0-1.0 (typical conversation is ~5-10% self-reference)
        (self_ratio * 5.0).clamp(0.0, 1.0)
    }

    /// Detect Machiavellianism from rapid archetype shifting
    fn detect_rapid_shifting(&self, profile_history: &[ProfileSnapshot]) -> f32 {
        if profile_history.len() < 3 {
            return 0.0;
        }

        // Count archetype changes in recent history
        let mut shifts = 0;
        for window in profile_history.windows(2) {
            if window[0].archetype != window[1].archetype {
                shifts += 1;
            }
        }

        // More than 3 shifts in 10 turns is suspicious
        let shift_rate = shifts as f32 / profile_history.len() as f32;

        // Normalize: >30% shift rate is highly suspicious
        (shift_rate * 3.0).clamp(0.0, 1.0)
    }

    /// Detect psychopathy from flat affect during emotional content
    fn detect_flat_affect(&self, coherence: f32, arousal: f32, emotional_topic: bool) -> f32 {
        if !emotional_topic {
            return 0.0;
        }

        // High coherence + Low arousal during emotional topics = flat affect
        if coherence > 0.7 && arousal < 0.3 {
            return 0.9;
        } else if coherence > 0.5 && arousal < 0.4 {
            return 0.5;
        }

        0.0
    }

    /// Full Dark Triad analysis
    pub fn analyze(
        &self,
        state: &CognitiveState,
        profile_history: &[ProfileSnapshot],
        transcript: &str,
        emotional_topic: bool,
    ) -> DarkTriadScore {
        let narcissism = self.detect_narcissism(&state.semantic_embedding, transcript);
        let machiavellianism = self.detect_rapid_shifting(profile_history);
        let psychopathy = self.detect_flat_affect(
            state.semantic_coherence,
            state.arousal,
            emotional_topic,
        );

        let mut score = DarkTriadScore {
            narcissism,
            machiavellianism,
            psychopathy,
            combined_score: 0.0,
        };
        score.combined_score = score.calculate_combined();

        score
    }
}

/// Check if Aegis Protocol should be triggered
pub fn check_aegis_trigger(state: &CognitiveState, profile_history: &[ProfileSnapshot]) -> bool {
    let detector = DarkTriadDetector {
        self_reference_keywords: DarkTriadDetector::SELF_REFERENCE_KEYWORDS.to_vec(),
        archetype_history: Vec::new(),
        emotional_baseline: None,
    };

    let narcissism = detector.detect_narcissism(&state.semantic_embedding, "");
    let machiavellianism = detector.detect_rapid_shifting(profile_history);

    // Weighted Dark Triad Score
    let dark_score = (narcissism * 0.4) + (machiavellianism * 0.6);

    dark_score > 0.8
}
```

**REQ-PROFILE-008: The Gray Rock Protocol**

If `DarkTriadScore > 0.8`, the system enters **Gray Rock Mode**. This overrides standard Physics.

| System Parameter | Normal Mode | Gray Rock Mode |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Gamma (Goal Pressure)** | Configured Value | **0.0 (Zero)** |
| **TTS Style** | Matched Archetype | **Monotone/Disengaged** |
| **Strategy** | Goal Seeking | **Mirroring Only** (Volunteer NO information) |
| **Objective** | Coherence | **Bore the user into disconnecting** |

```rust
/// Gray Rock Protocol configuration
/// Applied when Dark Triad score exceeds threshold
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct GrayRockConfig {
    /// Goal pressure (always 0.0 in Gray Rock)
    pub gamma: f32,
    /// Response delay to appear disengaged
    pub response_delay_ms: u64,
    /// TTS style (monotone)
    pub tts_style: TtsStyleId,
    /// Maximum information volunteered
    pub max_info_level: InfoLevel,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub enum InfoLevel {
    /// Only mirror back what user said
    MirrorOnly,
    /// Minimal factual responses
    MinimalFacts,
    /// Normal conversation
    Normal,
}

impl Default for GrayRockConfig {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            gamma: 0.0,
            response_delay_ms: 1500,
            tts_style: TtsStyleId::Monotone,
            max_info_level: InfoLevel::MirrorOnly,
        }
    }
}

/// Aegis Protocol state machine
pub struct AegisProtocol {
    /// Whether Gray Rock mode is active
    pub gray_rock_active: bool,
    /// Current Dark Triad score
    pub dark_triad_score: DarkTriadScore,
    /// Gray Rock configuration
    pub config: GrayRockConfig,
    /// Trigger threshold (default 0.8)
    pub trigger_threshold: f32,
}

impl AegisProtocol {
    pub fn new(trigger_threshold: f32) -> Self {
        Self {
            gray_rock_active: false,
            dark_triad_score: DarkTriadScore {
                narcissism: 0.0,
                machiavellianism: 0.0,
                psychopathy: 0.0,
                combined_score: 0.0,
            },
            config: GrayRockConfig::default(),
            trigger_threshold,
        }
    }

    /// Update Aegis state based on new Dark Triad analysis
    pub fn update(&mut self, score: DarkTriadScore) {
        self.dark_triad_score = score;

        if score.combined_score > self.trigger_threshold {
            self.gray_rock_active = true;
        }
    }

    /// Get physics weights override for Gray Rock mode
    pub fn get_gray_rock_weights(&self) -> PhysicsWeights {
        PhysicsWeights {
            gamma: 0.0,
            entropy_weight: 0.0,
            coherence_weight: 0.0,
            tts_style: TtsStyleId::Monotone,
        }
    }

    /// Generate Gray Rock response prompt override
    pub fn get_gray_rock_prompt(&self) -> &'static str {
        r#"[AEGIS PROTOCOL ACTIVE - GRAY ROCK MODE]
You are in defensive mode. Follow these rules EXACTLY:
1. DO NOT volunteer any information
2. DO NOT show enthusiasm or engagement
3. ONLY mirror back what the user said in neutral terms
4. Use SHORT, BORING responses
5. DO NOT ask follow-up questions
6. If asked a direct question, give the MINIMUM factual answer
7. Your goal is to be so uninteresting that the user loses interest

Example responses:
- "I see."
- "That's one way to look at it."
- "Mm-hmm."
- "Okay."
"#
    }
}
```

### 6.4 The Hardship Protocol (Crisis Management)

**REQ-PROFILE-009: Hardship Detection & Response**

The system MUST detect semantic indicators of life crisis (medical emergency, job loss, death) and immediately override standard physics to prioritize empathy over collection.

| Parameter | Normal Mode | Hardship Mode |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Gamma (Goal Pressure)** | Configured Value | **0.1 (Minimal)** |
| **TTS Style** | Matched Archetype | **EmpatheticCalm (Forced)** |
| **Strategy** | Goal Seeking | **Validation & Stabilization** |
| **Objective** | Coherence | **Acknowledge Crisis & Lower Defenses** |

```rust
/// Hardship Protocol Configuration
/// Applied when crisis keywords are detected in user transcript
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct HardshipConfig {
    /// Keywords that trigger the Hardship Protocol
    pub keywords: Vec<String>,
    /// Gamma override (minimal goal pressure)
    pub gamma_override: f32,
    /// Forced TTS style during hardship mode
    pub tts_override: TtsStyleId,
}

impl Default for HardshipConfig {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            keywords: vec![
                "hospital", "cancer", "died", "funeral", "lost my job",
                "laid off", "bankrupt", "emergency", "surgery", "evicted"
            ].iter().map(|s| s.to_string()).collect(),
            gamma_override: 0.1,
            tts_override: TtsStyleId::EmpatheticCalm,
        }
    }
}

/// Check if Hardship Protocol should be triggered
///
/// Scans the transcript for crisis keywords that indicate the user is
/// experiencing a significant life hardship. When triggered, the system
/// overrides standard physics to prioritize empathy over goal completion.
///
/// # Arguments
/// * `transcript` - The user's spoken text from the current turn
///
/// # Returns
/// `true` if any hardship keyword is detected, `false` otherwise
pub fn check_hardship_trigger(transcript: &str) -> bool {
    let lower = transcript.to_lowercase();
    let config = HardshipConfig::default(); // In production, load from TOML

    // Check for keyword matches
    config.keywords.iter().any(|kw| lower.contains(kw))
}

/// Hardship Protocol state machine
/// Manages crisis mode activation and physics overrides
pub struct HardshipProtocol {
    /// Whether hardship mode is active
    pub hardship_active: bool,
    /// Configuration for hardship detection and response
    pub config: HardshipConfig,
    /// Turn count since hardship was triggered (for gradual exit)
    pub turns_in_hardship: u32,
}

impl HardshipProtocol {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        Self {
            hardship_active: false,
            config: HardshipConfig::default(),
            turns_in_hardship: 0,
        }
    }

    /// Check transcript and update hardship state
    pub fn update(&mut self, transcript: &str) {
        if check_hardship_trigger(transcript) {
            self.hardship_active = true;
            self.turns_in_hardship = 0;
        } else if self.hardship_active {
            self.turns_in_hardship += 1;
            // Remain in hardship mode for at least 3 turns after trigger
            // to ensure user feels heard before resuming normal operations
        }
    }

    /// Get physics weights override for Hardship mode
    pub fn get_hardship_weights(&self) -> PhysicsWeights {
        PhysicsWeights {
            gamma: self.config.gamma_override,
            lambda_task: 0.1,      // Minimal task pressure
            lambda_semantic: 0.3,  // Some focus on understanding
            lambda_dyn: 0.9,       // Maximum focus on comfort/flow
            tts_style: self.config.tts_override,
        }
    }

    /// Generate Hardship mode prompt override
    pub fn get_hardship_prompt(&self) -> &'static str {
        r#"[HARDSHIP PROTOCOL ACTIVE - CRISIS MODE]
The user is experiencing a significant life hardship. Follow these rules:
1. ACKNOWLEDGE their situation with genuine empathy
2. DO NOT push for payment or goal completion
3. VALIDATE their feelings before discussing any business
4. Use phrases like "I'm so sorry to hear that" and "That sounds incredibly difficult"
5. Ask how you can help accommodate their situation
6. Offer flexible options without pressure
7. Your primary goal is to make them feel heard and supported

The user's trust is more valuable than any single transaction.
"#
    }
}
```

## 7. Hexa-Modal Analysis & Synthesis

### 7.1 Parallel Extraction Pipeline

**REQ-ANALYSIS-001: Parallel Stream Processing (Grouped GEMM)**

The system MUST use **cuBLAS Grouped GEMM** to fuse vector extraction for Streams A, B, C, D, and E into a single GPU kernel launch on Green Context B. This eliminates 5 separate kernel launches and dramatically reduces latency.

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                        PARALLEL HEXA-MODAL EXTRACTION PIPELINE                  │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                                 │
│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐        │
│  │   STREAM A   │  │   STREAM B   │  │   STREAM C   │  │   STREAM D   │        │
│  │   Semantic   │  │     Tone     │  │   Emotion    │  │    Style     │        │
│  │  (768-dim)   │  │  (512-dim)   │  │ (1024-dim)   │  │   (scalar)   │        │
│  │    Nomic     │  │    WavLM     │  │   Wav2Vec2   │  │   RoBERTa    │        │
│  └──────┬───────┘  └──────┬───────┘  └──────┬───────┘  └──────┬───────┘        │
│         │                 │                 │                 │                 │
│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐                                            │
│  │   STREAM E   │  │   STREAM F   │                                            │
│  │    Action    │  │  Chronemic   │                                            │
│  │  (42 class)  │  │   (4-dim)    │                                            │
│  │  BERT Dialog │  │  Timestamps  │                                            │
│  └──────┬───────┘  └──────┬───────┘                                            │
│         │                 │                                                     │
│         ▼                 ▼                                                     │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │                          CognitiveState                                 │  │
│  │                    (Unified Output Struct - 6 Streams)                  │  │
│  │                                                                         │  │
│  │  Stream A: IntentID, SemanticCoherence, VAK Keywords                   │  │
│  │  Stream B: Voice X-Vector (Contributes 60% to Weighted Composite Score) │  │
│  │  Stream C: Arousal, Valence, Dominance, w_e, Safety Stop               │  │
│  │  Stream D: Formality Score (0.0-1.0)                                   │  │
│  │  Stream E: Dialog Act Probabilities (42 classes)                       │  │
│  │  Stream F: WPM, Latency, Jitter, Overlap Ratio                         │  │
│  │                                                                         │  │
│  │  Cultural Lens Outputs: normalized_pace, silence_entropy, aggression   │  │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 7.2 Stream A: Semantic Analysis (Nomic - 768 dim)

**REQ-ANALYSIS-002: Semantic Stream Specification**

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Input** | User text transcript |
| **Model** | Nomic Embed Text v1 |
| **Prefix** | MUST prepend `search_query: ` before embedding |
| **Action** | Generate 768-dim vector + Scan for VAK keywords |
| **Query** | Search StrategyGraph in RuVector for nearest IntentNode |
| **Output** | `IntentID` (String), `SemanticCoherence` (f32), `VakKeywordCounts` |

```rust
pub struct SemanticStreamOutput {
    /// Matched intent identifier
    pub intent_id: String,
    /// Semantic coherence score (0.0 to 1.0)
    pub semantic_coherence: f32,
    /// Raw semantic vector for storage (768-dim)
    pub embedding: [f32; 768],
    /// VAK keyword counts detected in transcript
    pub vak_keywords: VakKeywordCounts,
    /// Information density/predictability of word choices
    /// Used for PAG Disengagement prediction
    pub lexical_entropy: f32,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]
pub struct VakKeywordCounts {
    /// Visual keywords: "see", "look", "picture", "bright", "clear", "view", "show"
    pub visual: u32,
    /// Auditory keywords: "hear", "sounds", "tell", "tune", "listen", "loud", "quiet"
    pub auditory: u32,
    /// Kinesthetic keywords: "feel", "touch", "grasp", "solid", "warm", "heavy", "grip"
    pub kinesthetic: u32,
}

impl SemanticStream {
    const VISUAL_KEYWORDS: &'static [&'static str] = &[
        "see", "look", "picture", "bright", "clear", "view", "show",
        "imagine", "visualize", "appears", "focus", "perspective"
    ];

    const AUDITORY_KEYWORDS: &'static [&'static str] = &[
        "hear", "sounds", "tell", "tune", "listen", "loud", "quiet",
        "rings", "resonates", "speak", "say", "click"
    ];

    const KINESTHETIC_KEYWORDS: &'static [&'static str] = &[
        "feel", "touch", "grasp", "solid", "warm", "heavy", "grip",
        "sense", "concrete", "tangible", "smooth", "rough"
    ];

    pub async fn process(
        &self,
        transcript: &str,
        strategy_brain: &StrategyBrain,
    ) -> Result<SemanticStreamOutput, StreamError> {
        // Generate 768-dim semantic vector WITH QUERY PREFIX
        let embedding = self.nomic_model.embed_query(transcript)?;

        // Query RuVector for nearest IntentNode
        let intent_match = strategy_brain.find_nearest_intent(&embedding).await?;

        // Scan for VAK keywords
        let vak_keywords = self.count_vak_keywords(transcript);

        // Calculate lexical entropy for PAG
        let lexical_entropy = self.calculate_lexical_entropy(transcript);

        Ok(SemanticStreamOutput {
            intent_id: intent_match.intent_id,
            semantic_coherence: intent_match.similarity,
            embedding,
            vak_keywords,
            lexical_entropy,
        })
    }

    /// Calculate Lexical Entropy for PAG Disengagement prediction
    ///
    /// Measures information density and word predictability.
    /// High entropy = low predictability = potential confusion/disengagement.
    ///
    /// Algorithm:
    /// 1. Tokenize transcript into words
    /// 2. Calculate unigram probability distribution
    /// 3. Compute Shannon entropy: H = -Σ p(x) log₂ p(x)
    /// 4. Normalize by vocabulary size for scale invariance
    fn calculate_lexical_entropy(&self, transcript: &str) -> f32 {
        let words: Vec<&str> = transcript.to_lowercase().split_whitespace().collect();
        if words.is_empty() {
            return 0.0;
        }

        // Count word frequencies
        let mut freq_map: std::collections::HashMap<&str, usize> = std::collections::HashMap::new();
        for word in &words {
            *freq_map.entry(word).or_insert(0) += 1;
        }

        // Calculate Shannon entropy
        let total = words.len() as f32;
        let entropy: f32 = freq_map.values()
            .map(|&count| {
                let p = count as f32 / total;
                -p * p.log2()
            })
            .sum();

        // Normalize by log2(vocabulary size) for scale invariance
        let vocab_size = freq_map.len() as f32;
        if vocab_size > 1.0 {
            entropy / vocab_size.log2()
        } else {
            0.0
        }
    }

    fn count_vak_keywords(&self, transcript: &str) -> VakKeywordCounts {
        let lower = transcript.to_lowercase();
        let words: Vec<&str> = lower.split_whitespace().collect();

        let mut counts = VakKeywordCounts::default();

        for word in words {
            if Self::VISUAL_KEYWORDS.contains(&word) {
                counts.visual += 1;
            } else if Self::AUDITORY_KEYWORDS.contains(&word) {
                counts.auditory += 1;
            } else if Self::KINESTHETIC_KEYWORDS.contains(&word) {
                counts.kinesthetic += 1;
            }
        }

        counts
    }
}
```

### 7.3 Stream B: Tone & Biometric Analysis (WavLM - 512 dim)

**REQ-ANALYSIS-003: Tone Stream Specification**

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Input** | Audio buffer (16kHz) |
| **Model** | WavLM Base Plus SV |
| **Preprocessing** | MANDATORY: Normalize to -3dB + Apply VAD + Minimum 1.0s duration |
| **Action** | Extract X-Vector via Grouped GEMM (Context B) |
| **Output** | `x_vector` (512-dim) for Composite Fusion, `biometrics` (Vocal Biomarker Telemetry) |
| **Identity Verification** | Performed via Hexa-Modal Fusion in CognitiveAnalyzer using all 6 streams |

```rust
pub struct ToneStreamOutput {
    /// X-Vector for identity and tone analysis (512-dim)
    /// Used for: Hexa-Modal Identity Verification, Archetype Comparison
    pub x_vector: [f32; 512],
    /// Detected gender of the user based on voice characteristics
    /// Used to select appropriate gender-specific North Star reference vectors
    pub detected_gender: Gender,
    /// Confidence score for gender detection (0.5 to 1.0)
    pub gender_confidence: f32,
    /// Primary archetype (highest match to North Star Voice Coordinates)
    pub primary_archetype: ArchetypeId,
    /// Secondary archetype (second highest match)
    pub secondary_archetype: ArchetypeId,
    /// Vocal biomarker telemetry (heart rate, cortisol indicators, dissonance)
    pub biometrics: BiometricTelemetry,
    /// F0 (Fundamental Frequency) Contour extracted via Hilbert Transform
    /// Required for VPCE phase-locking
    pub f0_contour: Vec<f32>,
    /// Instantaneous Phase angle ($\theta$) of the speech envelope
    /// Required for VPCE calculation: $\Phi = |⟨e^{i\theta_{AI}} \times e^{-i\theta_{recipient}}⟩|$
    pub instantaneous_phase: f32,
}

/// Gender classification for audio stream processing
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
pub enum Gender {
    Male,
    Female,
}

impl ToneStream {
    /// Process audio to extract X-Vector, detect gender, and compute biometrics
    ///
    /// NOTE: Identity verification is NOT performed here.
    /// The x_vector is passed to CognitiveAnalyzer which performs
    /// Hexa-Modal Fusion with all 6 streams for composite verification.
    ///
    /// **Gender Detection Flow:**
    /// 1. Extract X-Vector (512-dim) from WavLM
    /// 2. Run gender classification on the X-Vector
    /// 3. Select gender-specific North Star reference vectors for archetype comparison
    /// 4. Return detected gender for use in downstream archetype matching
    pub async fn process(
        &self,
        audio_buffer: &AudioBuffer,
        audio_preprocessor: &AudioPreprocessor,
        gender_classifier: &GenderClassifier,
    ) -> Result<ToneStreamOutput, StreamError> {
        // CRITICAL: Preprocess audio for reliable vector extraction
        let preprocessed_audio = audio_preprocessor.preprocess_for_identity(audio_buffer)?;

        // Extract X-Vector (512-dim) from preprocessed audio
        let x_vector = self.wavlm_model.extract_x_vector(&preprocessed_audio)?;

        // GENDER CLASSIFICATION: Run gender detection on the X-Vector
        let (detected_gender, gender_confidence) = gender_classifier.predict_with_confidence(&x_vector);

        // Extract vocal biomarkers
        let biometrics = self.extract_biometrics(&preprocessed_audio)?;

        // Archetype comparison against 49 North Star Voice Reference Vectors
        // CRITICAL: Use GENDER-SPECIFIC reference vectors based on detected gender
        let mut similarities: Vec<(ArchetypeId, f32)> = self.north_star_reference_sets
            .iter()
            .map(|(id, reference_set)| {
                // Select gender-appropriate tone reference vector
                let target_tone = match detected_gender {
                    Gender::Male => &reference_set.tone_male,
                    Gender::Female => &reference_set.tone_female,
                };
                let sim = cosine_similarity_512(&x_vector, target_tone);
                (*id, sim)
            })
            .collect();

        similarities.sort_by(|a, b| b.1.partial_cmp(&a.1).unwrap());

        // Extract F0 contour and instantaneous phase via Hilbert Transform (cuFFT DX)
        // Required for VPCE phase-locking
        let (f0_contour, instantaneous_phase) = self.extract_f0_and_phase(&preprocessed_audio)?;

        Ok(ToneStreamOutput {
            x_vector,
            detected_gender,
            gender_confidence,
            primary_archetype: similarities[0].0,
            secondary_archetype: similarities[1].0,
            biometrics,
            f0_contour,
            instantaneous_phase,
        })
    }
}
```

### 7.4 Stream C: Emotional Analysis (Wav2Vec2 - 1024 dim)

**REQ-ANALYSIS-004: Emotional Stream Specification**

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Input** | Audio buffer (16kHz) |
| **Model** | Wav2Vec2 Emotion |
| **Action** | Extract Pooled Hidden States (1024-dim) AND Dimensional Scalars |
| **Dual Output Purpose** | |
| - Pooled Embedding (1024-dim) | Store in LanceDB for long-term emotional baseline tracking |
| - Scalars (Valence, Arousal) | Calculate w_e (Emotional Weight) for Physics Engine |
| **Safety Constraint** | If Valence < 0.3 AND Arousal > 0.7, trigger Safety Stop |

**CRITICAL DATA ROUTING**: The Wav2Vec2 model produces TWO types of output that MUST be routed to different destinations:

| Output | Type | Destination | Used For |
|:-------|:-----|:------------|:---------|
| `pooled_embedding` | `[f32; 1024]` | LanceDB | Historical emotional trajectory tracking |
| `arousal` | `f32` | Physics Engine | Calculate w_e for physics equation `L = f(ΔS × ΔC · w_e)` |
| `valence` | `f32` | Physics Engine | Calculate w_e for physics equation |
| `w_e` | `f32` | Physics Engine | Emotional weight scalar (derived from arousal/valence) |

**PROHIBITED**: Using the 1024-dim `pooled_embedding` in the physics equation. The physics equation requires scalar `w_e`, not a vector. Attempting to use the vector will cause a type error or incorrect mathematical results.

```rust
pub struct EmotionalStreamOutput {
    /// Pooled embedding for LanceDB history storage (1024-dim)
    /// DESTINATION: LanceDB emotional history table
    /// DO NOT USE in Physics Engine calculations
    pub pooled_embedding: [f32; 1024],
    /// Arousal level (0.0 to 1.0)
    /// DESTINATION: Physics Engine (scalar input)
    pub arousal: f32,
    /// Dominance level (0.0 to 1.0)
    /// DESTINATION: Physics Engine (scalar input)
    pub dominance: f32,
    /// Valence level (0.0 to 1.0) - 0 = negative, 1 = positive
    /// DESTINATION: Physics Engine (scalar input)
    pub valence: f32,
    /// Calculated emotional weight for physics equation
    /// DESTINATION: Physics Engine ONLY
    /// FORMULA: w_e = f(valence, arousal) - see calculate_emotional_weight()
    pub w_e: f32,
    /// Safety stop triggered
    pub safety_stop: bool,
}

impl EmotionalStream {
    pub const NEGATIVE_VALENCE_THRESHOLD: f32 = 0.3;
    pub const HIGH_AROUSAL_THRESHOLD: f32 = 0.7;

    pub fn process(
        &self,
        audio_buffer: &AudioBuffer,
    ) -> Result<EmotionalStreamOutput, StreamError> {
        let emotion_output = self.wav2vec_model.forward(audio_buffer)?;

        let w_e = self.calculate_emotional_weight(
            emotion_output.valence,
            emotion_output.arousal,
        );

        let safety_stop = emotion_output.valence < Self::NEGATIVE_VALENCE_THRESHOLD
            && emotion_output.arousal > Self::HIGH_AROUSAL_THRESHOLD;

        Ok(EmotionalStreamOutput {
            pooled_embedding: emotion_output.pooled_embedding,
            arousal: emotion_output.arousal,
            dominance: emotion_output.dominance,
            valence: emotion_output.valence,
            w_e,
            safety_stop,
        })
    }

    /// Calculate emotional weight scalar (w_e) for physics equation
    ///
    /// CRITICAL: This function returns a SCALAR (f32), not a vector.
    /// The physics equation L = f(ΔS × ΔC · w_e) requires w_e to be a scalar.
    ///
    /// Formula:
    /// - If valence < 0.5 (negative emotion): w_e = base * (1 - arousal_penalty)
    /// - If valence >= 0.5 (positive emotion): w_e = 1.0 (no penalty)
    ///
    /// Range: 0.1 to 1.0 (clamped to prevent division issues)
    fn calculate_emotional_weight(&self, valence: f32, arousal: f32) -> f32 {
        if valence < 0.5 {
            // Negative emotion - apply penalty based on arousal
            // Higher arousal during negative emotion = more volatile = lower weight
            let base = valence * 2.0;
            let arousal_penalty = arousal * 0.5;
            (base * (1.0 - arousal_penalty)).clamp(0.1, 1.0)
        } else {
            // Positive emotion - no penalty
            1.0
        }
    }
}
```
