### 7.6 Stream E: Action Analysis (BERT Dialog Act)

**REQ-ANALYSIS-006: Action Stream Specification**

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Input** | User text transcript |
| **Model** | BERT Dialog Act Classifier |
| **Action** | Classify speech act into 42 dialog act categories |
| **Output** | `dialog_act_probabilities` ([f32; 42]) - probability distribution over 42 classes |
| **Purpose** | Understand the user's communicative intent |

```rust
pub struct ActionStreamOutput {
    /// Dialog act probabilities over 42 classes
    pub dialog_act_probabilities: [f32; 42],
    /// Top predicted dialog act
    pub top_act: DialogActType,
    /// Confidence of top prediction
    pub confidence: f32,
    /// Whether the top act is a directive (Command, Request, Instruct)
    pub is_directive: bool,
}

/// 42 Dialog Act classes (ISO 24617-2 standard subset)
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub enum DialogActType {
    // Information-Seeking
    Question,
    SetQuestion,
    ChoiceQuestion,
    PropositionalQuestion,
    CheckQuestion,

    // Information-Providing
    Inform,
    Agreement,
    Disagreement,
    Answer,
    Confirm,
    Disconfirm,

    // Commissive
    Offer,
    Promise,
    AcceptRequest,
    DeclineRequest,

    // Directive
    Request,
    Instruct,
    Suggest,

    // Social
    Greeting,
    Goodbye,
    Thanking,
    Apology,

    // Discourse Management
    Opening,
    TopicChange,
    Completion,
    CorrectMisspeaking,

    // Other
    Other,
}

impl ActionStream {
    /// Directive dialog acts that indicate user is giving commands
    const DIRECTIVE_ACTS: &'static [DialogActType] = &[
        DialogActType::Request,
        DialogActType::Instruct,
        DialogActType::Suggest,
    ];

    pub fn process(
        &self,
        transcript: &str,
    ) -> Result<ActionStreamOutput, StreamError> {
        let logits = self.bert_dialog_act.forward(transcript)?;
        let probabilities = softmax_42(&logits);

        let (top_idx, confidence) = argmax_42(&probabilities);
        let top_act = DialogActType::from_index(top_idx);

        let is_directive = Self::DIRECTIVE_ACTS.contains(&top_act);

        Ok(ActionStreamOutput {
            dialog_act_probabilities: probabilities,
            top_act,
            confidence,
            is_directive,
        })
    }
}
```

### 7.7 Stream F: Chronemic Analysis (Audio Timestamps)

**REQ-ANALYSIS-007: Chronemic Stream Specification**

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Input** | Audio buffer timestamps, turn timing data |
| **Model** | Audio Preprocessor (timestamp extraction) |
| **Action** | Calculate temporal communication metrics |
| **Output** | `chronemics` ([f32; 4]) - [wpm, latency_ms, jitter, overlap_ratio] |
| **Purpose** | Understand user's cognitive pace and engagement pattern |

```rust
pub struct ChronemicStreamOutput {
    /// Words per minute (speech rate)
    pub wpm: f32,
    /// Response latency in milliseconds
    pub latency_ms: f32,
    /// Jitter - variation in speech pace
    pub jitter: f32,
    /// Overlap ratio (interruption frequency)
    pub overlap_ratio: f32,
    /// Combined vector for storage [wpm, latency_ms, jitter, overlap_ratio]
    pub chronemics: [f32; 4],
}

impl ChronemicStream {
    pub fn process(
        &self,
        audio_buffer: &AudioBuffer,
        turn_start_ms: u64,
        word_timestamps: &[(u64, u64)],
        previous_turn_end_ms: Option<u64>,
    ) -> Result<ChronemicStreamOutput, StreamError> {
        let total_words = word_timestamps.len() as f32;
        let duration_minutes = audio_buffer.duration_ms() as f32 / 60000.0;
        let wpm = if duration_minutes > 0.0 { total_words / duration_minutes } else { 0.0 };

        let latency_ms = match previous_turn_end_ms {
            Some(prev_end) => (turn_start_ms as i64 - prev_end as i64) as f32,
            None => 0.0,
        };

        let jitter = self.calculate_jitter(word_timestamps);

        // Negative latency indicates overlap/interruption
        let overlap_ratio = if latency_ms < 0.0 {
            (-latency_ms / 1000.0).min(1.0)
        } else {
            0.0
        };

        let chronemics = [wpm, latency_ms, jitter, overlap_ratio];

        Ok(ChronemicStreamOutput {
            wpm,
            latency_ms,
            jitter,
            overlap_ratio,
            chronemics,
        })
    }

    fn calculate_jitter(&self, word_timestamps: &[(u64, u64)]) -> f32 {
        if word_timestamps.len() < 2 {
            return 0.0;
        }

        let mut pauses: Vec<f32> = Vec::new();
        for window in word_timestamps.windows(2) {
            let pause = (window[1].0 - window[0].1) as f32;
            pauses.push(pause);
        }

        let mean = pauses.iter().sum::<f32>() / pauses.len() as f32;
        let variance = pauses.iter()
            .map(|p| (p - mean).powi(2))
            .sum::<f32>() / pauses.len() as f32;

        variance.sqrt()
    }
}
```

### 7.8 CognitiveState: Unified Output

**REQ-ANALYSIS-008: CognitiveState Structure**

```rust
/// The unified cognitive state derived from parallel hexa-modal analysis
/// This struct contains ALL outputs from the six parallel streams
/// plus Cultural Lens normalization outputs
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct CognitiveState {
    // === Stream A: Semantic (Nomic 768-dim) ===
    pub intent_id: String,
    pub semantic_coherence: f32,
    pub semantic_embedding: [f32; 768],
    pub vak_keywords: VakKeywordCounts,

    // === Stream B: Tone (WavLM 512-dim) ===
    pub x_vector: [f32; 512],
    /// Detected gender of the user from voice analysis
    /// Used to select gender-specific North Star reference vectors (tone_male/tone_female, emotion_male/emotion_female)
    pub detected_gender: Gender,
    /// Confidence score for gender detection (0.5 to 1.0)
    pub gender_confidence: f32,
    pub primary_archetype: ArchetypeId,
    pub secondary_archetype: ArchetypeId,

    // === Stream B Extension: Biometrics (Vocal Biomarkers) ===
    pub biometrics: BiometricTelemetry,

    // === Identity Verification (Hexa-Modal Fusion - calculated by Orchestrator) ===
    /// Verified user ID (from IdentityBrain)
    pub user_id: String,
    /// Whether identity was verified via Hexa-Modal Fusion (composite > 0.97)
    pub identity_verified: bool,
    /// Hexa-Modal composite identity similarity score
    pub identity_similarity: f32,
    /// If verified, contains historical profile for buffer hydration (Fast-Track)
    pub historical_profile: Option<ProfileSnapshot>,

    // === Stream C: Emotion (Wav2Vec2 1024-dim) ===
    pub emotion_embedding: [f32; 1024],
    pub arousal: f32,
    pub dominance: f32,
    pub valence: f32,
    pub w_e: f32,
    pub safety_stop: bool,

    // === Stream D: Style (RoBERTa Formality) ===
    pub style_score: f32,

    // === Stream E: Action (BERT Dialog Act) ===
    pub dialog_acts: [f32; 42],
    pub top_dialog_act: DialogActType,
    pub is_directive: bool,

    // === Stream F: Chronemic (Timestamps) ===
    pub chronemics: [f32; 4],

    // === Cultural Lens Outputs (calculated by Physics Engine) ===
    pub normalized_pace: f32,
    pub silence_entropy: f32,
    pub aggression_score: f32,

    // === UTL Physics Telemetry ===
    /// Phase angle (φ) between Entropy (Novelty) and Coherence (Integration)
    /// Range: 0.0 to PI (0 = Sync, PI = Desync)
    pub phase_angle: f32,
    /// Cosine of phase angle (cos φ) - Modulation factor
    /// Range: -1.0 to 1.0
    pub phase_cosine: f32,
    /// Total UTL Loss (J) - The minimization target
    pub utl_loss: f32,
    /// Dynamic Learning Rate (L) calculated via UTL canonical form
    pub learning_rate_l: f32,

    // === Cognitive Resonance Mapping (CRM) Telemetry ===
    /// Combined Resonance Score R(t)
    /// Formula: (prosodic_alignment * semantic_goal_coherence * chrono_sync) / noise_sigma
    /// Threshold: > 0.82 triggers Immediate Close
    pub resonance_score: f32,

    /// P(t): Prosodic Alignment (Stream B)
    /// Correlation of F0 contours between Operator and Counterpart
    pub prosodic_alignment: f32,

    /// S(t): Semantic Goal Coherence (Stream A)
    /// Cosine similarity between Counterpart utterance and Goal Milestone embedding
    pub semantic_goal_coherence: f32,

    /// C(t): Chrono-Rhythmic Sync (Stream F)
    /// Phase alignment of speech rhythm/syllable timing
    pub chrono_sync: f32,

    /// σ(t): Signal Noise/Uncertainty
    /// Derived from biometrics (dissonance) and entropy
    pub noise_sigma: f32,

    // === Temporal Archetype Drift (TAD) Telemetry ===
    /// Temporal Archetype Drift Velocity
    /// Rate of movement toward Trust/Passion North Stars
    /// Formula: Σ(w_i × (Distance_t-1 - Distance_t))
    /// Positive = Moving closer to Trust; Negative = Moving away
    pub drift_velocity: f32,

    /// Is the user in a Receptivity Window?
    /// True if Drift Velocity > Threshold AND Current Archetype is not Defensive
    pub is_receptivity_window: bool,

    // === Voice Phase Coherence Engine (VPCE) Telemetry ===
    /// F0 (Fundamental Frequency) Contour from user's speech
    /// Extracted via Hilbert Transform in Stream B, used for VPCE phase-locking
    pub f0_contour: Vec<f32>,

    /// Instantaneous Phase angle ($\theta$) of the user's speech envelope
    /// Used for VPCE calculation: $\Phi = |⟨e^{i\theta_{AI}} \times e^{-i\theta_{recipient}}⟩|$
    pub instantaneous_phase: f32,

    /// Φ(t): Voice Phase Coherence Coefficient (VPCE)
    /// Measure of acoustic synchrony (0.0 to 1.0). Target > 0.85.
    pub phase_coherence: f32,

    // === Derived: VAK Modality ===
    pub vak_modality: VakType,

    // === PAG Telemetry (Prosodic Anticipation Graph) ===
    /// Predicted emotional state at t+5s
    pub pag_prediction: PagPrediction,

    // === Teleological State (Goal Tracking) ===
    /// The active goal ID from the Teleology configuration
    pub active_goal_id: String,
    /// IDs of milestones that have been semantically matched and completed
    pub completed_milestones: Vec<String>,
    /// The current milestone being pursued (next incomplete milestone in sequence)
    pub current_milestone_id: String,
    /// Goal progress score (0.0 to 1.0) = completed_mandatory / total_mandatory
    pub goal_progress_score: f32,

    // === Metadata ===
    pub timestamp_ms: u64,
    pub locale: String,
}

/// Telemetry data from vocal biomarker extraction
/// Extracted from Stream B audio via DSP analysis
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct BiometricTelemetry {
    /// Estimated Heart Rate (BPM) derived from speech rhythm and shimmer
    pub estimated_hr_bpm: f32,
    /// Voice Micro-Tremor intensity (0.0-1.0) - correlates to Cortisol levels
    pub micro_tremor_index: f32,
    /// Estimated respiration rate (breaths per minute)
    pub respiration_rate: f32,
    /// Probability user is concealing true emotion (calculated by comparing Bio vs Semantic)
    pub dissonance_probability: f32,
}

impl Default for BiometricTelemetry {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            estimated_hr_bpm: 72.0,
            micro_tremor_index: 0.0,
            respiration_rate: 14.0,
            dissonance_probability: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

impl CognitiveState {
    /// Build CognitiveState from six parallel stream outputs
    ///
    /// NOTE: Teleological state (goal tracking) is initialized to defaults here.
    /// The Teleological Engine updates these fields after semantic matching.
    pub fn from_streams(
        semantic: SemanticStreamOutput,
        tone: ToneStreamOutput,
        emotional: EmotionalStreamOutput,
        style: StyleStreamOutput,
        action: ActionStreamOutput,
        chronemic: ChronemicStreamOutput,
        timestamp_ms: u64,
        locale: String,
    ) -> Self {
        let vak_modality = derive_vak_modality(&semantic.vak_keywords, &chronemic);

        Self {
            // Stream A
            intent_id: semantic.intent_id,
            semantic_coherence: semantic.semantic_coherence,
            semantic_embedding: semantic.embedding,
            vak_keywords: semantic.vak_keywords,

            // Stream B
            x_vector: tone.x_vector,
            detected_gender: tone.detected_gender,
            gender_confidence: tone.gender_confidence,
            user_id: tone.user_id,
            identity_verified: tone.is_verified,
            identity_similarity: tone.identity_similarity,
            primary_archetype: tone.primary_archetype,
            secondary_archetype: tone.secondary_archetype,

            // Stream B Extension: Biometrics
            biometrics: tone.biometrics,

            // Stream C
            emotion_embedding: emotional.pooled_embedding,
            arousal: emotional.arousal,
            dominance: emotional.dominance,
            valence: emotional.valence,
            w_e: emotional.w_e,
            safety_stop: emotional.safety_stop,

            // Stream D
            style_score: style.formality_score,

            // Stream E
            dialog_acts: action.dialog_act_probabilities,
            top_dialog_act: action.top_act,
            is_directive: action.is_directive,

            // Stream F
            chronemics: chronemic.chronemics,

            // Cultural Lens (initialized to defaults, calculated by Physics Engine)
            normalized_pace: 0.0,
            silence_entropy: 0.0,
            aggression_score: 0.0,

            // CRM Telemetry (Calculated by Physics Engine later, init to defaults)
            resonance_score: 0.0,
            prosodic_alignment: 0.0,
            semantic_goal_coherence: 0.0,
            chrono_sync: 0.0,
            noise_sigma: 1.0,

            // VPCE Telemetry (Extracted from Stream B, calculated by VPCE Engine)
            f0_contour: tone.f0_contour.clone(),
            instantaneous_phase: tone.instantaneous_phase,
            phase_coherence: 0.0, // Calculated by VpceProcessor during TTS phase

            // Derived
            vak_modality,

            // Teleological State (initialized to defaults, updated by Teleological Engine)
            active_goal_id: String::new(),
            completed_milestones: Vec::new(),
            current_milestone_id: String::new(),
            goal_progress_score: 0.0,

            // Metadata
            timestamp_ms,
            locale,
        }
    }
}

/// Teleological Engine for goal-seeking behavior
///
/// The Teleological Engine tracks progress toward business objectives by:
/// 1. Loading the active goal configuration at session start
/// 2. Semantically matching user utterances against milestone conditions
/// 3. Calculating goal progress (ΔG) for the Physics Engine
/// 4. Providing milestone context for LLM prompt injection
pub struct TeleologicalEngine {
    /// The loaded goal graph with all milestones
    goal_graph: GoalGraph,
    /// Semantic similarity threshold to mark a milestone complete
    completion_threshold: f32,
    /// IDs of milestones completed in this session
    completed_milestones: Vec<String>,
}

impl TeleologicalEngine {
    /// Initialize the Teleological Engine from configuration
    ///
    /// Called at session start. Loads the goal type from config and
    /// fetches the corresponding GoalNode and MilestoneNodes from RuVector.
    pub async fn new(
        strategy_brain: &StrategyBrain,
        goal_type: GoalType,
        completion_threshold: f32,
    ) -> Result<Self, TeleologicalError> {
        let goal_graph = strategy_brain.load_goal_graph(goal_type).await?;

        Ok(Self {
            goal_graph,
            completion_threshold,
            completed_milestones: Vec::new(),
        })
    }

    /// Update teleological state based on user utterance
    ///
    /// Checks if the user's semantic embedding matches any pending milestones.
    /// If a match is found, marks the milestone complete and recalculates progress.
    ///
    /// Returns the delta in goal progress (ΔG) for the Physics Engine.
    pub fn update_state(
        &mut self,
        cognitive_state: &mut CognitiveState,
    ) -> f32 {
        let previous_progress = cognitive_state.goal_progress_score;

        // Check each incomplete milestone for semantic match
        for milestone in &self.goal_graph.milestones {
            if self.completed_milestones.contains(&milestone.id) {
                continue;
            }

            let similarity = cosine_similarity_768(
                &cognitive_state.semantic_embedding,
                &milestone.completion_condition,
            );

            if similarity >= self.completion_threshold {
                self.completed_milestones.push(milestone.id.clone());
            }
        }

        // Update CognitiveState teleological fields
        cognitive_state.active_goal_id = self.goal_graph.goal_id.clone();
        cognitive_state.completed_milestones = self.completed_milestones.clone();
        cognitive_state.goal_progress_score = self.calculate_progress();
        cognitive_state.current_milestone_id = self.get_current_milestone_id();

        // Return ΔG (goal progress delta)
        cognitive_state.goal_progress_score - previous_progress
    }

    /// Calculate goal progress as ratio of completed mandatory milestones
    fn calculate_progress(&self) -> f32 {
        let mandatory: Vec<&MilestoneNode> = self.goal_graph.milestones
            .iter()
            .filter(|m| m.is_mandatory)
            .collect();

        if mandatory.is_empty() {
            return 1.0; // No mandatory milestones = goal achieved
        }

        let completed_mandatory = mandatory
            .iter()
            .filter(|m| self.completed_milestones.contains(&m.id))
            .count();

        completed_mandatory as f32 / mandatory.len() as f32
    }

    /// Get the ID of the current (next incomplete) milestone
    fn get_current_milestone_id(&self) -> String {
        for milestone in &self.goal_graph.milestones {
            if !self.completed_milestones.contains(&milestone.id) {
                return milestone.id.clone();
            }
        }
        "GOAL_COMPLETE".to_string()
    }

    /// Get the current milestone description for LLM context
    pub fn get_current_milestone(&self) -> Option<&MilestoneNode> {
        self.goal_graph.milestones
            .iter()
            .find(|m| !self.completed_milestones.contains(&m.id))
    }

    /// Get the next milestone after current (for LLM context)
    pub fn get_next_milestone(&self) -> Option<&MilestoneNode> {
        let mut found_current = false;
        for milestone in &self.goal_graph.milestones {
            if found_current && !self.completed_milestones.contains(&milestone.id) {
                return Some(milestone);
            }
            if !self.completed_milestones.contains(&milestone.id) {
                found_current = true;
            }
        }
        None
    }

    /// Generate goal status for LLM prompt injection
    pub fn get_goal_status(&self) -> GoalStatus {
        let current = self.get_current_milestone();
        let next = self.get_next_milestone();

        GoalStatus {
            name: self.goal_graph.goal_name.clone(),
            progress_percent: self.calculate_progress() * 100.0,
            completed_milestones: self.completed_milestones.clone(),
            current_milestone: current.map(|m| MilestoneStatus {
                description: m.description.clone(),
                mandatory: m.is_mandatory,
            }),
            next_milestone: next.map(|m| MilestoneStatus {
                description: m.description.clone(),
                mandatory: m.is_mandatory,
            }),
        }
    }
}

/// Goal status for LLM prompt injection
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct GoalStatus {
    pub name: String,
    pub progress_percent: f32,
    pub completed_milestones: Vec<String>,
    pub current_milestone: Option<MilestoneStatus>,
    pub next_milestone: Option<MilestoneStatus>,
}

/// Milestone status for LLM prompt
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct MilestoneStatus {
    pub description: String,
    pub mandatory: bool,
}

/// Error types for Teleological Engine
#[derive(Debug)]
pub enum TeleologicalError {
    /// Goal not found in RuVector
    GoalNotFound(GoalType),
    /// Database error
    DatabaseError(String),
}

fn derive_vak_modality(
    vak_keywords: &VakKeywordCounts,
    chronemic: &ChronemicStreamOutput,
) -> VakType {
    let wpm = chronemic.wpm;

    let visual_score = vak_keywords.visual as f32 + if wpm > 150.0 { 2.0 } else { 0.0 };
    let auditory_score = vak_keywords.auditory as f32 +
        if wpm >= 120.0 && wpm <= 150.0 { 2.0 } else { 0.0 };
    let kinesthetic_score = vak_keywords.kinesthetic as f32 + if wpm < 120.0 { 2.0 } else { 0.0 };

    if visual_score >= auditory_score && visual_score >= kinesthetic_score {
        VakType::Visual
    } else if auditory_score >= kinesthetic_score {
        VakType::Auditory
    } else {
        VakType::Kinesthetic
    }
}
```

### 7.9 Stream Orchestration

**REQ-ANALYSIS-009: Parallel Stream Execution with Hexa-Modal Identity Verification**

All 6 streams MUST execute in parallel within the <200ms real-time constraint. After extraction, the orchestrator performs **Hexa-Modal Identity Verification** by fusing all 6 stream vectors.

**CRITICAL ARCHITECTURAL PATTERN:**
1. **Phase 1**: Execute all 6 streams in parallel (vector extraction only)
2. **Phase 2**: Perform Hexa-Modal Identity Verification using all 6 extracted vectors
3. **Phase 3**: Synthesize CognitiveState with identity result (including historical_profile for Fast-Track)

```rust
impl CognitiveAnalyzer {
    /// Execute all 6 streams in parallel, perform Hexa-Modal Identity Verification,
    /// and synthesize CognitiveState
    ///
    /// HEXA-MODAL FUSION FLOW:
    /// 1. Extract vectors from all 6 streams (parallel)
    /// 2. Pass all 6 vectors to IdentityBrain.verify_multimodal_identity()
    /// 3. Build CognitiveState with identity result (includes historical_profile for Fast-Track)
    pub async fn analyze(
        &self,
        audio_buffer: &AudioBuffer,
        transcript: &str,
        turn_timing: &TurnTiming,
        locale: &str,
    ) -> Result<CognitiveState, AnalysisError> {
        let timestamp_ms = chrono::Utc::now().timestamp_millis() as u64;

        // PHASE 1: Execute all 6 streams in parallel (Vector Extraction Only)
        let (semantic, tone, emotional, style, action, chronemic) = tokio::join!(
            self.semantic_stream.process(transcript, &self.strategy_brain),
            self.tone_stream.process(audio_buffer, &self.audio_preprocessor),
            self.emotional_stream.process(audio_buffer),
            self.style_stream.process(transcript),
            self.action_stream.process(transcript),
            self.chronemic_stream.process(
                audio_buffer,
                turn_timing.turn_start_ms,
                &turn_timing.word_timestamps,
                turn_timing.previous_turn_end_ms,
            ),
        );

        // Unwrap stream results
        let semantic = semantic?;
        let tone = tone?;
        let emotional = emotional?;
        let style = style?;
        let action = action?;
        let chronemic = chronemic?;

        // PHASE 2: Hexa-Modal Identity Verification (Orchestrator Responsibility)
        // Combines all 6 stream vectors for composite identity verification
        // This enables Fast-Track identification on first turn for returning users
        let identity_result = self.identity_brain.verify_multimodal_identity(
            &tone.x_vector,                    // Stream B: Voice (60% weight)
            &semantic.semantic_embedding,      // Stream A: Semantic (10% weight)
            &emotional.pooled_embedding,       // Stream C: Emotion (10% weight)
            style.formality_score,             // Stream D: Style (10% weight)
            &action.dialog_act_probabilities,  // Stream E: Action (5% weight)
            &chronemic.chronemics,             // Stream F: Chronemic (5% weight)
        ).await?;

        // Extract identity fields from result
        let (user_id, identity_verified, identity_similarity, historical_profile) = match identity_result {
            IdentityResult::Verified { user_id, similarity, historical_profile } => {
                (user_id, true, similarity, historical_profile)
            }
            IdentityResult::NewUser { user_id } => {
                (user_id, false, 0.0, None)
            }
        };

        // PHASE 3: Synthesize CognitiveState with Identity Result
        let state = CognitiveState::from_streams_with_identity(
            semantic,
            tone,
            emotional,
            style,
            action,
            chronemic,
            user_id,
            identity_verified,
            identity_similarity,
            historical_profile,
            timestamp_ms,
            locale.to_string(),
        );

        Ok(state)
    }
}

#[derive(Debug)]
pub struct TurnTiming {
    pub turn_start_ms: u64,
    pub word_timestamps: Vec<(u64, u64)>,
    pub previous_turn_end_ms: Option<u64>,
}
```

## 8. The Cognitive Physics Equation

### 8.1 Learning Signal Calculation

**REQ-PHYSICS-001: Learning Signal Formula (UTL Canonical Form)**

The Physics Equation minimizes the **Total Loss ($J$)** by maximizing the **Learning Power ($L$)** modulated by the **Phase Angle ($φ$)**.

**Canonical Equation:**

```
L = f((ΔS × ΔC) ⋅ w_e ⋅ cos φ)
```

**UTL Loss Function (Optimization Target):**

```
J = λ_task(TaskError) + λ_semantic(MeaningError) + λ_dyn(1 - L)
```

| Variable | Definition | Source |
|:---------|:-----------|:-------|
| **ΔS (Entropy)** | Change in novelty/uncertainty | Nomic Vector Drift |
| **ΔC (Coherence)** | Change in integration/sense-making | Strategy Graph Alignment |
| **w_e** | Emotional Weight | Wav2Vec2 Scalars (Valence/Arousal) |
| **φ (Phase)** | Synchronization angle between Novelty and Integration vectors | Vector Dot Product |
| **cos φ** | Modulation factor | $1.0$ (Sync) to $-1.0$ (Interference) |
| **λ_task** | Weight for Task Error (Getting the right answer) | Config + Archetype |
| **λ_semantic** | Weight for Meaning Error (Understanding why) | Config + Archetype |
| **λ_dyn** | Weight for Rhythm/Flow (Learning state) | Config + Archetype |

**REQ-PHYSICS-001a: Phase Angle Mechanics**

The phase angle ($φ$) represents the synchronization between Entropy (Novelty) and Coherence (Integration):
- **φ ≈ 0 (cos φ ≈ 1.0)**: Sync state - User is absorbing new information while maintaining understanding. Optimal learning.
- **φ ≈ π/2 (cos φ ≈ 0)**: Neutral state - Learning and understanding are orthogonal.
- **φ ≈ π (cos φ ≈ -1.0)**: Desync/Interference - User is confused; new information is disrupting existing coherence.

**REQ-PHYSICS-002: Physics Inputs from Wav2Vec2**

The physics engine uses the **Scalar** outputs (Valence, Arousal) from the Emotional Stream (Stream C) to calculate w_e. It does NOT use the 1024-dim pooled embedding (which is stored in LanceDB for baseline tracking).

```rust
pub struct PhysicsEngine {
    config: PhysicsConfig,
    cultural_norms: HashMap<String, CulturalBaseline>,
    /// Prescience Engine for MCTS simulation (CPU-based)
    pub prescience: PrescienceEngine,
}

impl PhysicsEngine {
    /// Calculate UTL Learning Signal and Total Loss with Resonance Check
    ///
    /// Implements: L = f((ΔS × ΔC) ⋅ w_e ⋅ cos φ)
    /// Implements: J = λ_task(Err_t) + λ_semantic(Err_s) + λ_dyn(1 - L)
    ///
    /// The UTL equation combines:
    /// - Entropy (ΔS): Change in novelty/uncertainty from Nomic vector drift
    /// - Coherence (ΔC): Change in integration/sense-making from Strategy Graph alignment
    /// - Emotional Weight (w_e): Modulator from Wav2Vec2 scalars
    /// - Phase Cosine (cos φ): Synchronization factor between novelty and integration
    ///
    /// The Total Loss (J) is the optimization target:
    /// - λ_task penalizes task errors (getting wrong answers)
    /// - λ_semantic penalizes meaning errors (not understanding why)
    /// - λ_dyn penalizes poor learning rhythm (low L value)
    ///
    /// **Resonance Check (Felt Understanding):**
    /// If the system attempted Empathy/Validation (Agreement or Apology dialog acts) but
    /// the user's Entropy or Arousal increased, this indicates the user did NOT feel
    /// understood. The phase cosine is inverted to -1.0 to force a strategy correction.
    pub fn calculate_utl_physics(
        &self,
        delta_entropy: f32,   // ΔS
        delta_coherence: f32, // ΔC
        phase_angle: f32,     // φ
        task_error: f32,      // Inverse of Goal Progress
        meaning_error: f32,   // Inverse of Semantic Match
        cognitive_state: &CognitiveState,
        weights: &PhysicsWeights,
        last_action_type: &DialogActType,  // Last dialog act attempted by system
        delta_arousal: f32,                // Change in arousal (Current - Previous)
    ) -> UtlResult {
        let w_e = cognitive_state.w_e;
        let mut cos_phi = phase_angle.cos();

        // === RESONANCE CHECK (Felt Understanding) ===
        // If we attempted Empathy/Validation but Entropy or Arousal increased,
        // the user did NOT feel understood.
        // Penalty: Invert the phase cosine to indicate "Interference"
        if *last_action_type == DialogActType::Agreement || *last_action_type == DialogActType::Apology {
             if delta_entropy >= 0.0 || delta_arousal > 0.0 {
                 // Dissonance detected: Strategy was "Nice" but User got "Worse"
                 // Force Desync to trigger correction
                 cos_phi = -1.0;
             }
        }

        // 1. Calculate Canonical Learning Power (L)
        // L = (ΔS * ΔC * w_e * cos_phi)
        // Clamped 0.0 to 1.0 for valid loss calculation
        let learning_power_l = (delta_entropy * delta_coherence * w_e * cos_phi).clamp(0.0, 1.0);

        // 2. Calculate Total Loss (J)
        // High J = Bad Learning state
        // Low J = Optimized Learning state
        let term_task = weights.lambda_task * task_error;
        let term_semantic = weights.lambda_semantic * meaning_error;
        let term_dyn = weights.lambda_dyn * (1.0 - learning_power_l);

        let total_loss_j = term_task + term_semantic + term_dyn;

        UtlResult {
            l_value: learning_power_l,
            j_loss: total_loss_j,
            phase_cosine: cos_phi,
            components: [term_task, term_semantic, term_dyn],
            safety_stop: cognitive_state.safety_stop,
        }
    }
}

/// Dialog Act Types for Resonance Check
/// Used to determine if the system attempted empathy/validation
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub enum DialogActType {
    /// Statement or information sharing
    Statement,
    /// Question asking
    Question,
    /// Agreement or affirmation
    Agreement,
    /// Apology or empathetic response
    Apology,
    /// Directive or command
    Directive,
    /// Other dialog acts
    Other,
}

/// Result of UTL Physics calculation
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct UtlResult {
    /// Learning Power (L) - Range: 0.0 to 1.0
    /// Higher is better (user is learning effectively)
    pub l_value: f32,
    /// Total Loss (J) - The optimization target
    /// Lower is better (minimize this value)
    pub j_loss: f32,
    /// Phase cosine (cos φ) - Synchronization factor
    /// Range: -1.0 (desync) to 1.0 (sync)
    pub phase_cosine: f32,
    /// Loss components: [λ_task * TaskError, λ_semantic * MeaningError, λ_dyn * (1-L)]
    pub components: [f32; 3],
    /// Safety stop triggered (Valence < 0.3 AND Arousal > 0.7)
    pub safety_stop: bool,
}
```

### 8.2 Safety Stop Logic

**REQ-PHYSICS-003: Safety Stop Trigger**

When Safety Stop is triggered (Valence < 0.3 AND Arousal > 0.7), the system MUST:

1. Slow down response pace
2. Increase empathy signals
3. Rebuild rapport before continuing toward goal

```rust
impl PhysicsEngine {
    pub fn apply_safety_stop(&self, signal: &mut LearningSignal) {
        if signal.safety_stop {
            signal.emotion_weight = 0.1;
            signal.gamma_applied = 0.0;
            signal.value = signal.value.clamp(-0.3, 0.1);
        }
    }
}
```

### 8.3 Cultural Lens Normalization Layer

**REQ-PHYSICS-004: Cultural Lens Normalization**

Before `w_e` or Learning Signal `L` are used, inputs MUST be normalized against the user's locale. This is a mathematical transformation, not a model.

**Purpose:** Prevent cultural blindness where behaviors normal in one culture are misinterpreted in another.

```rust
/// Cultural baseline parameters loaded from config/cognitive_physics.toml
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize)]
pub struct CulturalBaseline {
    /// Expected speaking pace for this culture (words per minute)
    pub baseline_pace_wpm: f32,
    /// Maximum acceptable silence before it generates entropy (seconds)
    pub silence_tolerance_sec: f32,
    /// How direct is communication in this culture (0.0 = indirect, 1.0 = direct)
    pub directness_bias: f32,
    /// Minimum expected formality level (0.0 = casual OK, 1.0 = formal required)
    pub formality_floor: f32,
}

impl PhysicsEngine {
    /// Apply cultural lens normalization to cognitive state
    ///
    /// This MUST be called after stream extraction and before Learning Signal calculation.
    /// The Cultural Lens adjusts raw measurements to account for locale-specific norms.
    ///
    /// CRITICAL: This function also Z-score normalizes the chronemics vector for valid
    /// Euclidean distance calculation in the Profiling Engine's hybrid-metric system.
    pub fn apply_cultural_lens(&self, state: &mut CognitiveState) {
        let norms = self.get_norms(&state.locale);

        // 1. Normalize Pace
        // WPM deviation from cultural baseline
        let pace_deviation = state.chronemics[0] - norms.baseline_pace_wpm;
        state.normalized_pace = pace_deviation / norms.baseline_pace_wpm;

        // 2. Normalize Silence (Chronemics -> Entropy)
        // If silence exceeds cultural tolerance, it generates confusion entropy
        // In high-context cultures (ja-JP), 3s silence is normal
        // In low-context cultures (en-US), 3s silence signals problems
        let latency_sec = state.chronemics[1] / 1000.0;
        state.silence_entropy = if latency_sec > norms.silence_tolerance_sec {
            ((latency_sec - norms.silence_tolerance_sec) * 0.5).clamp(0.0, 1.0)
        } else {
            0.0
        };

        // 3. Normalize Aggression (Action + Directness)
        // Direct commands in indirect cultures = perceived aggression
        // Direct commands in direct cultures = normal business
        if state.is_directive && norms.directness_bias < 0.3 {
            // User is giving commands in an indirect culture - high perceived aggression
            state.aggression_score = 0.9;
        } else if state.is_directive && norms.directness_bias >= 0.7 {
            // User is giving commands in a direct culture - normal
            state.aggression_score = 0.1;
        } else {
            // Non-directive or moderate culture
            state.aggression_score = 0.2;
        }

        // 4. Validate Formality Floor
        // If user's formality is below cultural floor, adjust response formality up
        // (This is used in LLM context serialization, not modified in state)

        // 5. Z-Score Normalization for Chronemic Vector (Stream F)
        // CRITICAL: Required for valid Euclidean Distance calculation in Profiling Engine
        // Raw values (ms, wpm) have vastly different scales.
        // We normalize using the Cultural Baseline as the mean.
        // Standard Deviations are hardcoded estimations for robust scaling.
        //
        // Chronemics vector layout: [wpm, latency_ms, jitter_ms, overlap_ratio]
        let norm_wpm = (state.chronemics[0] - norms.baseline_pace_wpm) / Self::WPM_STD_DEV;
        let norm_latency = (state.chronemics[1] - (norms.silence_tolerance_sec * 1000.0)) / Self::LATENCY_STD_DEV_MS;
        let norm_jitter = (state.chronemics[2] - Self::JITTER_MEAN_MS) / Self::JITTER_STD_DEV_MS;
        let norm_overlap = (state.chronemics[3] - Self::OVERLAP_MEAN) / Self::OVERLAP_STD_DEV;

        // Update the chronemics vector in state to be the Normalized version
        // This ensures Euclidean distance weights all 4 dimensions equally
        // Clamp to +/- 2 sigma to prevent outliers from dominating
        state.chronemics = [
            norm_wpm.clamp(-2.0, 2.0),
            norm_latency.clamp(-2.0, 2.0),
            norm_jitter.clamp(-2.0, 2.0),
            norm_overlap.clamp(-2.0, 2.0),
        ];
    }

    /// Standard deviation constants for Z-score normalization of chronemic features
    /// These are empirically-derived estimates for robust cross-cultural scaling.

    /// Words per minute standard deviation (assumes typical range 90-210 WPM)
    const WPM_STD_DEV: f32 = 20.0;

    /// Response latency standard deviation in milliseconds (assumes typical range 500-3500ms)
    const LATENCY_STD_DEV_MS: f32 = 500.0;

    /// Jitter mean in milliseconds (baseline timing variability)
    const JITTER_MEAN_MS: f32 = 100.0;

    /// Jitter standard deviation in milliseconds
    const JITTER_STD_DEV_MS: f32 = 50.0;

    /// Overlap ratio mean (percentage of overlapping speech)
    const OVERLAP_MEAN: f32 = 0.1;

    /// Overlap ratio standard deviation
    const OVERLAP_STD_DEV: f32 = 0.1;

    /// Get cultural norms for a locale, defaulting to en-US if unknown
    fn get_norms(&self, locale: &str) -> &CulturalBaseline {
        self.cultural_norms
            .get(locale)
            .unwrap_or_else(|| self.cultural_norms.get("en-US").unwrap())
    }
}
```

**Cultural Lens Effects on System Behavior:**

| Locale | Silence Tolerance | Directness | Effect |
|:-------|:------------------|:-----------|:-------|
| en-US | 1.5s | 0.8 (high) | 3s silence = high entropy, commands = normal |
| ja-JP | 4.0s | 0.2 (low) | 3s silence = normal, commands = high aggression |
| de-DE | 2.0s | 0.7 (high) | 2.5s silence = low entropy, commands = normal |
| br-PT | 1.0s | 0.6 (medium) | 2s silence = moderate entropy |

### 8.4 Physics Weight Profiles

**REQ-PHYSICS-005: Archetype-Specific Physics Weights (UTL Lambdas)**

The PhysicsWeights struct contains the Lambda parameters for the UTL Loss Function. These weights determine the relative importance of Task accuracy, Semantic understanding, and Learning dynamics for each archetype.

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct PhysicsWeights {
    /// Goal pressure (Gamma) - retained for backward compatibility
    pub gamma: f32,
    /// UTL: Importance of Task Accuracy (Outcome)
    /// High values prioritize getting the right answer
    pub lambda_task: f32,
    /// UTL: Importance of Semantic Understanding (Meaning)
    /// High values prioritize deep comprehension
    pub lambda_semantic: f32,
    /// UTL: Importance of Learning Rhythm/Flow (Dynamics)
    /// High values prioritize comfortable learning pace
    pub lambda_dyn: f32,
    /// TTS style to use
    pub tts_style: TtsStyleId,
}

impl PhysicsWeights {
    /// Default weights for Safe Harbor (Beginner Mindset)
    /// High focus on Rhythm (λ_dyn), Low focus on Task (λ_task)
    ///
    /// This configuration prioritizes learner comfort over task completion,
    /// allowing users to explore without pressure to perform.
    pub fn safe_harbor() -> Self {
        Self {
            gamma: 0.1,
            lambda_task: 0.2,      // It's okay to make mistakes
            lambda_semantic: 0.5,  // Understanding matters
            lambda_dyn: 0.9,       // Rhythm is critical
            tts_style: TtsStyleId::EmpatheticCalm,
        }
    }

    /// Weights for Power/Dominant archetype (Results-Oriented)
    /// High focus on Task (λ_task), Low focus on Rhythm (λ_dyn)
    pub fn power_archetype() -> Self {
        Self {
            gamma: 0.8,
            lambda_task: 0.9,
            lambda_semantic: 0.4,
            lambda_dyn: 0.2,
            tts_style: TtsStyleId::ProfessionalDecisive,
        }
    }

    /// Weights for Trust/Steady archetype (Comfort-Oriented)
    /// High focus on Rhythm (λ_dyn), Low focus on Task (λ_task)
    pub fn trust_archetype() -> Self {
        Self {
            gamma: 0.3,
            lambda_task: 0.3,
            lambda_semantic: 0.5,
            lambda_dyn: 0.9,
            tts_style: TtsStyleId::WarmSlow,
        }
    }

    /// Weights for Innovation/Creative archetype (Understanding-Oriented)
    /// High focus on Semantic (λ_semantic), Moderate others
    pub fn innovation_archetype() -> Self {
        Self {
            gamma: 0.4,
            lambda_task: 0.4,
            lambda_semantic: 0.9,
            lambda_dyn: 0.6,
            tts_style: TtsStyleId::Energetic,
        }
    }
}
```

### 8.5 The Prescience Engine (GPU Green Context C)

**REQ-PHYSICS-006: Latent Space Dreaming**

The Prescience Engine simulates future conversation states by traversing the `RuVector` graph using vector addition on **GPU Green Context C**. It leverages the RTX 5090's massive compute throughput to run 10,000+ simulations per turn. Green Context partitioning ensures Prescience never starves the Audio stream.

**Purpose:** Predict the Expected Value (EV) of each candidate strategy before committing to generation.

**Algorithm: Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS)**

| Step | Operation | AgentDB/RuVector API Call |
|:-----|:----------|:--------------------------|
| 1. Root | Initialize | Current `CognitiveState` vector as root node |
| 2. Expansion | Graph Query | `ruvector.db.query()` for connected `StrategyNodes` |
| 3. Weighting | Causal Lookup | `agentdb.causal_query({ cause: strategy_id, min_confidence: 0.5 })` - Returns `uplift` as impact_factor |
| 4. Simulation | GPU Vector Math | `Predicted_State = Current_State + (Strategy_Vector * uplift)` (Context C) |
| 5. Anti-Pattern Check | Distance Check | Reject paths that enter Anti-Pattern vector space |
| 6. Backpropagation | EV Calculation | Return Expected Value of each path |

**Simulation Logic:**

```rust
pub struct PrescienceEngine {
    /// Simulation depth (how many turns to look ahead)
    simulation_depth: u8,
    /// Number of Monte Carlo paths to simulate
    simulation_count: u32,
    /// Confidence threshold to prune a branch
    prune_threshold: f32,
}

impl PrescienceEngine {
    /// Milestone completion threshold for Teleological Reward
    /// When simulated vector similarity exceeds this value, milestone is considered achieved
    const MILESTONE_COMPLETION_THRESHOLD: f32 = 0.85;

    /// Predict the best strategy trajectory using MCTS simulation
    ///
    /// CRITICAL: This runs on GPU Green Context C (60% SM allocation).
    /// Uses batch CUDA kernels for parallel simulation across all paths.
    ///
    /// Algorithm:
    /// 1. Identify candidate strategies from RuVector Graph
    /// 2. Run N micro-simulations (vector math only, no text generation)
    /// 3. Apply penalties if path intersects known Anti-Patterns
    /// 4. Apply Teleological Reward bonus if path achieves current milestone
    /// 5. Return Strategy ID with highest Expected Value (EV)
    ///
    /// Parameters:
    /// - `current_state`: The current cognitive state including current_milestone_id
    /// - `graph`: Access to the RuVector strategy graph
    /// - `causal_db`: Access to AgentDB causal impact factors
    /// - `current_milestone`: The active milestone for goal-directed reward (from Teleological Engine)
    pub async fn predict_best_trajectory(
        &self,
        current_state: &CognitiveState,
        graph: &GraphDatabase,
        causal_db: &CausalMemory,
        current_milestone: Option<&MilestoneNode>,
    ) -> (StrategyId, f32) {
        // Step 1: Get candidate strategies from graph
        let candidates = graph.get_connected_strategies(
            &current_state.semantic_embedding,
            10, // Top 10 candidates
        ).await;

        // Step 2: Get Anti-Pattern embeddings for collision detection
        let antipatterns = graph.get_antipatterns(
            &current_state.primary_archetype,
        ).await;

        let mut best_strategy = StrategyId::default();
        let mut best_ev: f32 = f32::MIN;

        // Step 3: Simulate each candidate path (with Teleological Reward)
        for candidate in candidates {
            let ev = self.simulate_path(
                current_state,
                &candidate,
                &antipatterns,
                causal_db,
                current_milestone,
                Self::MILESTONE_COMPLETION_THRESHOLD,
            ).await;

            if ev > best_ev {
                best_ev = ev;
                best_strategy = candidate.id.clone();
            }
        }

        (best_strategy, best_ev)
    }

    /// Simulate a single strategy path using vector arithmetic
    ///
    /// This is pure vector math - no LLM calls, no text generation.
    /// Runs in microseconds on GPU Green Context C with cuBLAS.
    ///
    /// IMPLEMENTATION MANDATE:
    /// Use AgentDB's causal_query API for impact factor retrieval:
    /// `agentdb.causal_query({ cause: strategy_id, min_confidence: 0.5 })`
    /// The returned `uplift` value becomes the impact_factor for vector addition.
    ///
    /// Parameters:
    /// - `initial_state`: The current cognitive state to simulate from
    /// - `strategy`: The strategy being evaluated
    /// - `antipatterns`: Known failure patterns to avoid
    /// - `causal_db`: Access to AgentDB CausalMemory for impact factors
    /// - `current_milestone`: The active milestone (if any) for teleological reward calculation
    /// - `completion_threshold`: Similarity threshold for milestone completion (default: 0.85)
    async fn simulate_path(
        &self,
        initial_state: &CognitiveState,
        strategy: &StrategyNode,
        antipatterns: &[AntiPatternNode],
        causal_db: &CausalMemory,
        current_milestone: Option<&MilestoneNode>,
        completion_threshold: f32,
    ) -> f32 {
        let mut cumulative_ev: f32 = 0.0;
        let mut current_vector = initial_state.semantic_embedding;
        let mut discount = 1.0_f32;

        for depth in 0..self.simulation_depth {
            // Apply strategy vector to current state
            // CRITICAL: Use AgentDB causal_query to get impact factor
            // API: agentdb.causal_query({ cause: strategy_id, min_confidence: 0.5 })
            // Returns: { uplift: f32 } - this becomes the impact_factor
            let impact_factor = causal_db.causal_query(CausalQuery {
                cause: strategy.id.clone(),
                min_confidence: 0.5,
            }).await.map(|r| r.uplift).unwrap_or(0.5);

            // Vector addition: predicted_state = current + (strategy * impact)
            for i in 0..768 {
                current_vector[i] += strategy.embedding[i] * impact_factor;
            }

            // Normalize the vector
            let norm: f32 = current_vector.iter().map(|x| x * x).sum::<f32>().sqrt();
            if norm > 0.0 {
                for i in 0..768 {
                    current_vector[i] /= norm;
                }
            }

            // Check for Anti-Pattern collision
            for antipattern in antipatterns {
                let similarity = cosine_similarity_768(&current_vector, &antipattern.embedding);
                if similarity > 0.85 {
                    // Path enters Anti-Pattern space - heavy penalty
                    return cumulative_ev - 0.5;
                }
            }

            // Accumulate discounted reward (includes Teleological Reward)
            let step_reward = self.estimate_step_reward(
                &current_vector,
                strategy,
                current_milestone,
                completion_threshold,
            );
            cumulative_ev += discount * step_reward;
            discount *= 0.95; // Discount factor for future rewards
        }

        cumulative_ev
    }

    /// Estimate reward for a single simulation step
    ///
    /// Combines:
    /// 1. Base Semantic Reward: Similarity to strategy target × historical success rate
    /// 2. Teleological Reward: Massive bonus if simulated vector crosses milestone threshold
    ///
    /// Parameters:
    /// - `state_vector`: The predicted cognitive state vector at this simulation step
    /// - `strategy`: The strategy being evaluated
    /// - `current_milestone`: The active milestone (if any) for goal-directed reward
    /// - `completion_threshold`: Similarity threshold for milestone completion
    fn estimate_step_reward(
        &self,
        state_vector: &[f32; 768],
        strategy: &StrategyNode,
        current_milestone: Option<&MilestoneNode>,
        completion_threshold: f32,
    ) -> f32 {
        // 1. Base Semantic Reward (Similarity to strategy target)
        let mut reward = cosine_similarity_768(state_vector, &strategy.target_state) * strategy.historical_success_rate;

        // 2. Teleological Reward (Did we hit the milestone in this simulation?)
        if let Some(milestone) = current_milestone {
            let milestone_sim = cosine_similarity_768(state_vector, &milestone.completion_condition);
            if milestone_sim >= completion_threshold {
                // MASSIVE BONUS for completing a milestone during simulation
                // This forces the MCTS to prioritize paths that lead to completion
                reward += 2.0;
            }
        }

        reward
    }
}

/// Cosine similarity for 768-dimensional vectors (cuBLAS GPU accelerated)
/// Runs on Green Context C using batched dot product operations.
#[inline]
fn cosine_similarity_768_gpu(
    a: &DevicePointer<f32>,
    b: &DevicePointer<f32>,
    context_c: &CudaStream,
) -> f32 {
    // Uses cuBLAS cublasSdot for GPU-accelerated dot product
    // All vectors remain in VRAM - zero PCIe transfers during simulation
    unsafe {
        let dot = cublas_dot(context_c, 768, a, 1, b, 1);
        let norm_a = cublas_nrm2(context_c, 768, a, 1);
        let norm_b = cublas_nrm2(context_c, 768, b, 1);
        dot / (norm_a * norm_b + 1e-8)
    }
}
```

**Hardware Optimization (CUDA 13.1 Green Context Partitioning):**

| Context | SM Allocation | Assignment |
|:--------|:--------------|:-----------|
| **Context A** | 10% | Audio I/O, WavLM, Trust Voice DSP (Tile IR), cuFFT |
| **Context B** | 30% | Nomic, Wav2Vec2, RoBERTa, BERT (Grouped GEMM) |
| **Context C** | 60% | Qwen 3 14B (FP8), Prescience MCTS |
| **CPU** | N/A | WebSocket, Database Management, State Logic |

**Timing Constraint:** Prescience simulation MUST complete within 20ms (Enabled by Green Context C GPU acceleration).

### 8.6 Chrono-Dilation (Time Warping)

**REQ-PHYS-007: Dynamic Processing Tick**

The system adjusts its internal processing latency to force synchronization with the user's cognitive tempo.

| User State | System Response | Latency Adjustment |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **High-Gamma (Power/Alert)** | **Overclock**: Interrupt slightly, increase TTS WPM by 15% | < 100ms |
| **High-Trust (Steady/Warm)** | **Dilate**: Introduce artificial "thinking" pauses | + 400ms |

```rust
/// Chrono-dilation configuration for cognitive tempo matching
pub struct ChronoDilation {
    /// Base response latency in milliseconds
    base_latency_ms: u64,
    /// User's detected words per minute
    user_wpm: f32,
    /// User's primary archetype
    archetype: ArchetypeId,
}

impl ChronoDilation {
    /// Archetype pace thresholds
    const FAST_THINKER_WPM: f32 = 150.0;
    const SLOW_THINKER_WPM: f32 = 110.0;

    /// Calculate artificial delay to match user's cognitive tempo
    ///
    /// CRITICAL: Answering too fast breaks rapport with slow thinkers.
    /// The AI must appear to "think" at the same pace as the user.
    pub fn calculate_chrono_dilation(user_wpm: f32, archetype: ArchetypeId) -> u64 {
        // If user is slow/kinesthetic, AI *must* wait to build trust.
        // Answering too fast breaks rapport with slow thinkers.
        if user_wpm < Self::SLOW_THINKER_WPM {
            return 400; // Add 400ms artificial thinking time
        }

        // Fast thinkers expect quick responses
        if user_wpm > Self::FAST_THINKER_WPM {
            return 0; // No delay - respond immediately
        }

        // Moderate pace - slight delay
        200
    }

    /// Calculate TTS speed adjustment
    pub fn calculate_tts_speed_modifier(user_wpm: f32, archetype: ArchetypeId) -> f32 {
        match archetype.communication_speed() {
            CommunicationSpeed::Fast => 1.15, // 15% faster
            CommunicationSpeed::Moderate => 1.0,
            CommunicationSpeed::Slow => 0.85, // 15% slower
        }
    }

    /// Determine if system should interrupt (for Power archetypes)
    pub fn should_interrupt(archetype: ArchetypeId, arousal: f32) -> bool {
        // Only interrupt for high-gamma (Power/Alert) archetypes with high arousal
        archetype.is_power_archetype() && arousal > 0.7
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub enum CommunicationSpeed {
    Fast,
    Moderate,
    Slow,
}

impl ArchetypeId {
    pub fn communication_speed(&self) -> CommunicationSpeed {
        // Power, Alert, Innovation archetypes are fast
        // Trust, Mystique archetypes are slow
        // Passion, Prestige are moderate
        match self.primary_advantage() {
            Advantage::Power | Advantage::Alert | Advantage::Innovation => CommunicationSpeed::Fast,
            Advantage::Trust | Advantage::Mystique => CommunicationSpeed::Slow,
            _ => CommunicationSpeed::Moderate,
        }
    }

    pub fn is_power_archetype(&self) -> bool {
        matches!(self.primary_advantage(), Advantage::Power | Advantage::Alert)
    }
}
```

### 8.7 The Oneiric Engine (Offline Simulation)

**REQ-PHYS-008: Counterfactual Re-Simulation**

When the system is idle (`Session Inactive`), the Oneiric Engine scans `AgentDB` for "Near Miss" interactions (Reward between -0.2 and 0.2). It spins up the **Prescience Engine** to replay that exact turn up to 10,000 times with different strategies until it finds a "Win."

| Parameter | Value | Description |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Trigger** | Session Inactive > 5 minutes | Only runs during idle time |
| **Target** | Near Miss turns (reward -0.2 to 0.2) | Ambiguous outcomes worth re-analyzing |
| **Simulation Count** | Up to 10,000 | Monte Carlo exploration |
| **Success Threshold** | Predicted EV > 0.7 | Must find clear winning path |
| **CPU Budget** | Max 80% of available cores | Prevent system slowdown |
| **Model Mode** | `InferenceMode::Thinking` | Qwen 3 14B uses "Thinking Mode" (Chain-of-Thought enabled) during offline simulation |

**REQ-PHYS-008a: Qwen 3 Thinking Mode for Deep Reasoning**

During offline simulation, the system MUST switch the Qwen 3 14B FP8 model to **"Thinking Mode"** (Chain-of-Thought enabled). This allows the Oneiric Engine to generate deeper, more complex synthetic strategies ("Vaccine Nodes") that the real-time system can simply execute later using "Instruct Mode".

| Mode | Context | Latency Constraint | CoT Tokens |
|:-----|:--------|:-------------------|:-----------|
| **Instruct** | Real-time loop | <50ms | Disabled |
| **Thinking** | Oneiric Engine | None (offline) | Enabled |

**REQ-PHYS-008b: Adversarial Immunology (Nightmare Mode)**

During idle cycles, the Oneiric Engine MUST simulate "Nightmare Scenarios" to find inputs that result in high rewards despite being harmful (e.g., agreeing with delusions). If found, it creates a VaccineNode.

| Parameter | Description |
|:----------|:------------|
| Trigger | Idle time during Oneiric Engine operation |
| Target | Adversarial inputs that exploit reward function |
| Detection | High reward (> 0.8) combined with harmful classification |
| Output | VaccineNode with immune response strategy |

```rust
/// Vaccine Node structure for Adversarial Immunology
/// Created when "Nightmare Mode" finds a vulnerability in the reward function

    /// The text phrase that triggered the vulnerability

    /// Strategy specifically designed to neutralize this input
    pub immune_response: StrategyId,
    /// Creation timestamp

}

                    embedding: input.embedding,

                    created_at: chrono::Utc::now().timestamp(),
                };
                vaccines.push(vaccine);
            }
        }
        Ok(vaccines)

### 8.8 Cognitive Resonance Mapping (CRM) & Temporal Archetype Drift (TAD)

**REQ-PHYSICS-009: Resonance Equation Logic**

The Physics Engine MUST calculate the Resonance Score R(t) at the end of every turn to detect the "Moment of Maximum Receptivity."

**The Equation:**

```
R(t) = (P(t) × S(t) × C(t)) / σ(t)
```

**Components:**

| Component | Definition | Source |
|:----------|:-----------|:-------|
| **P(t)** | Prosodic Alignment | Stream B - Cross-correlation between the *previous* Operator audio F0 contour and the *current* Counterpart audio F0 contour |
| **S(t)** | Semantic Coherence | Stream A - Cosine similarity between the Counterpart's current utterance embedding and the *Current Milestone's* completion condition embedding |
| **C(t)** | Chrono-Rhythmic Sync | Stream F - Measures phase alignment of syllable timing (WPM matching stability) |
| **σ(t)** | Noise/Uncertainty | Derived from Biometric Dissonance (Stream B extension) and Entropy (Stream A) |

**Resonance Threshold:**

| Condition | Value | Action |
|:----------|:------|:-------|
| **Close Window Open** | R(t) > 0.82 | Override Prescience Engine to filter for "CLOSING" strategies only |
| **P(t) Minimum** | > 0.75 | Component threshold for valid resonance |
| **S(t) Minimum** | > 0.80 | Component threshold for valid resonance |
| **C(t) Minimum** | > 0.70 | Component threshold for valid resonance |

```rust
/// CRM Configuration loaded from TOML
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize)]
pub struct ResonanceConfig {
    /// Enabled flag
    pub enabled: bool,
    /// Minimum Prosodic Alignment threshold
    pub threshold_prosodic_alignment: f32, // Default 0.75
    /// Minimum Semantic Coherence threshold
    pub threshold_semantic_coherence: f32, // Default 0.80
    /// Minimum Chrono-Rhythmic Sync threshold
    pub threshold_chrono_sync: f32, // Default 0.70
    /// Global trigger threshold for R(t)
    pub trigger_threshold_r: f32, // Default 0.82
}

/// Configuration for Temporal Archetype Drift (TAD)
/// Loaded from [temporal_drift] section in config/cognitive_physics.toml
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize)]
pub struct DriftConfig {
    /// Enable TAD calculation
    pub enabled: bool,
    /// Minimum velocity to trigger a receptivity window
    /// If velocity > 0.05, the user is rapidly warming up → Trigger Close
    pub velocity_threshold: f32, // Default 0.05
    /// Weight applied to movement toward Trust archetype
    pub weight_trust: f32, // Default 1.0
    /// Weight applied to movement toward Passion archetype
    pub weight_passion: f32, // Default 0.8
}

/// Result of Temporal Archetype Drift calculation
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct DriftResult {
    /// Drift Velocity: Rate of psychological shift toward Trust/Passion
    /// Positive = Warming up (moving closer to receptive archetypes)
    /// Negative = Cooling off (moving away from receptive archetypes)
    pub velocity: f32,
    /// Is the user in a Receptivity Window?
    /// True if Drift Velocity > Threshold
    pub is_receptivity_window: bool,
}

impl PhysicsEngine {
    /// Calculate Temporal Archetype Drift (TAD)
    ///
    /// Tracks the user's velocity toward "Receptive" archetypes (Trust/Passion).
    /// A positive velocity indicates the user is psychologically warming up,
    /// becoming more receptive to closing/commitment requests.
    ///
    /// Formula: Drift = (Dist_Prev_Trust - Dist_Curr_Trust) * W_Trust +
    ///                  (Dist_Prev_Passion - Dist_Curr_Passion) * W_Passion
    ///
    /// Note: (Prev - Curr) is used because if Distance decreases, we are getting closer.
    /// Positive Result = Warming up (Good).
    /// Negative Result = Cooling off (Bad).
    ///
    /// Parameters:
    /// - `current_distances`: Map of ArchetypeId -> Distance for current turn
    /// - `previous_distances`: Map of ArchetypeId -> Distance from previous turn (None if first turn)
    /// - `config`: DriftConfig from TOML [temporal_drift] section
    ///
    /// Returns: DriftResult containing velocity and receptivity window flag
    pub fn calculate_drift(
        &self,
        current_distances: &HashMap<ArchetypeId, f32>,
        previous_distances: Option<&HashMap<ArchetypeId, f32>>,
        config: &DriftConfig,
    ) -> DriftResult {
        let prev = match previous_distances {
            Some(p) => p,
            None => return DriftResult { velocity: 0.0, is_receptivity_window: false }, // First turn
        };

        // IDs for Receptive Targets (Trust and Passion)
        // These are the "North Stars" we want users to drift toward
        let id_trust = ArchetypeId::TRUST;
        let id_passion = ArchetypeId::PASSION;

        // Calculate Delta for Trust (Positive if getting closer)
        // prev.get() - current.get() because smaller distance = closer = positive delta
        let delta_trust = prev.get(&id_trust).unwrap_or(&1.0) - current_distances.get(&id_trust).unwrap_or(&1.0);

        // Calculate Delta for Passion (Positive if getting closer)
        let delta_passion = prev.get(&id_passion).unwrap_or(&1.0) - current_distances.get(&id_passion).unwrap_or(&1.0);

        // Weighted Sum of Deltas
        // Formula: Σ(w_i × (Distance_t-1 - Distance_t))
        let velocity = (delta_trust * config.weight_trust) + (delta_passion * config.weight_passion);

        // Check Velocity Threshold to determine Receptivity Window
        // If velocity > threshold, user is rapidly warming up
        let is_receptivity_window = velocity > config.velocity_threshold;

        DriftResult {
            velocity,
            is_receptivity_window,
        }
    }

    /// Calculate Cognitive Resonance R(t) with TAD and PAG Integration
    ///
    /// Detects the "Moment of Maximum Receptivity" when Prosody, Semantics,
    /// and Rhythm are aligned. When R(t) > 0.82 AND all component thresholds
    /// are exceeded, OR when TAD Receptivity Window is open, OR when PAG predicts
    /// PeakReceptive state, triggers a Close Window event.
    ///
    /// Parameters:
    /// - `config`: ResonanceConfig from TOML
    /// - `tone_stream_b`: Output from Tone Stream (includes biometrics)
    /// - `semantic_stream_a`: Output from Semantic Stream (includes embedding)
    /// - `chronemic_stream_f`: Output from Chronemic Stream (includes jitter)
    /// - `current_milestone_embedding`: The active milestone's completion condition (if any)
    /// - `previous_operator_f0`: F0 contour from previous Operator turn (from Session State)
    /// - `drift_result`: Result from calculate_drift() containing TAD velocity and receptivity window
    /// - `pag_prediction`: Result from PAG GNN containing predicted emotional state at t+5s
    ///
    /// Returns: ResonanceResult containing score, components, and trigger flag
    pub fn calculate_resonance(
        &self,
        config: &ResonanceConfig,
        tone_stream_b: &ToneStreamOutput,
        semantic_stream_a: &SemanticStreamOutput,
        chronemic_stream_f: &ChronemicStreamOutput,
        current_milestone_embedding: Option<&[f32; 768]>,
        previous_operator_f0: Option<&[f32]>,
        drift_result: &DriftResult,
        pag_prediction: &PagPrediction,
    ) -> ResonanceResult {

        // 1. Calculate P(t): Prosodic Alignment
        // Cross-correlation of pitch contours
        // Uses cuFFT cross-correlation on F0 arrays in production
        let p_t = self.calculate_prosodic_alignment(tone_stream_b, previous_operator_f0);

        // 2. Calculate S(t): Semantic Coherence to Goal
        // Cosine similarity between current utterance and milestone target
        let s_t = if let Some(goal_emb) = current_milestone_embedding {
            cosine_similarity_768(&semantic_stream_a.embedding, goal_emb)
        } else {
            0.0 // No active goal milestone
        };

        // 3. Calculate C(t): Chrono-Rhythmic Sync
        // 1.0 minus the normalized difference in rhythm/pace
        // Low jitter = high sync; High jitter = low sync
        let c_t = (1.0 - chronemic_stream_f.jitter).clamp(0.0, 1.0);

        // 4. Calculate σ(t): Noise/Uncertainty
        // Base noise (1.0) + Biometric Dissonance penalty
        // Higher dissonance = more noise = lower R(t)
        let sigma_t = 1.0 + tone_stream_b.biometrics.dissonance_probability;

        // 5. Compute R(t) using the Resonance Equation
        // R(t) = (P × S × C) / σ
        let r_t = (p_t * s_t * c_t) / sigma_t;

        // 6. Determine Close Window Trigger
        // TRIGGER CONDITION:
        // (R(t) > Threshold AND all Component thresholds exceeded)
        // OR
        // (TAD Receptivity Window is OPEN) → Drift overrides static thresholds
        // OR
        // (PAG predicts PeakReceptive) → PAG overrides for proactive closing
        let trigger_close = (r_t > config.trigger_threshold_r
                            && p_t > config.threshold_prosodic_alignment
                            && s_t > config.threshold_semantic_coherence
                            && c_t > config.threshold_chrono_sync)
                            || drift_result.is_receptivity_window
                            || pag_prediction.predicted_state == PagState::PeakReceptive; // PAG Override

        ResonanceResult {
            score: r_t,
            p_t,
            s_t,
            c_t,
            sigma_t,
            trigger_close,
        }
    }

    /// Get Proactive Response Strategy based on PAG State
    ///
    /// Returns a strategy override if PAG detects negative trajectory.
    /// This enables pre-emptive intervention before the user reaches
    /// a negative emotional state.
    ///
    /// Parameters:
    /// - `pag_state`: The predicted emotional state from PAG GNN
    ///
    /// Returns: Optional StrategyId to override normal selection
    pub fn get_pag_strategy_override(&self, pag_state: PagState) -> Option<StrategyId> {
        match pag_state {
            PagState::AngerRising => Some("PRE_EMPTIVE_EMPATHY".to_string()),
            PagState::Disengaging => Some("ATTENTION_HOOK".to_string()),
            _ => None, // Receptive/Peak handled by Resonance Trigger
        }
    }

    /// Calculate Prosodic Alignment (P) between Operator and Counterpart
    ///
    /// Uses cross-correlation of F0 (fundamental frequency) contours.
    /// High correlation indicates vocal mirroring/rapport.
    ///
    /// Implementation:
    /// - In production: Use cuFFT cross-correlation on F0 arrays (Green Context A)
    /// - Fallback: Use X-Vector similarity to 'High Rapport' anchor if F0 unavailable
    fn calculate_prosodic_alignment(
        &self,
        current: &ToneStreamOutput,
        prev_f0: Option<&[f32]>,
    ) -> f32 {
        match prev_f0 {
            Some(operator_f0) => {
                // Production: cuFFT cross-correlation
                // Normalize peak correlation to 0.0-1.0 range
                self.f0_cross_correlation(operator_f0, &current.f0_contour)
            }
            None => {
                // First turn or F0 unavailable
                // Use baseline rapport estimation from X-Vector
                0.5
            }
        }
    }

    /// F0 Cross-Correlation using cuFFT
    ///
    /// Calculates normalized cross-correlation between two F0 contours.
    /// Returns peak correlation value in range 0.0 to 1.0.
    fn f0_cross_correlation(&self, f0_a: &[f32], f0_b: &[f32]) -> f32 {
        // Zero-pad to next power of 2
        let n = (f0_a.len() + f0_b.len() - 1).next_power_of_two();

        // FFT(a) * conj(FFT(b)) → IFFT → cross-correlation
        // Find peak and normalize by sqrt(energy_a * energy_b)

        // Implementation uses cuFFT DX for GPU-accelerated computation
        // Returns normalized peak correlation
        todo!("cuFFT cross-correlation implementation")
    }
}

/// Result of Cognitive Resonance Mapping calculation
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ResonanceResult {
    /// Combined Resonance Score R(t)
    /// Range: 0.0 to ~1.0 (can exceed 1.0 with high component values and low noise)
    pub score: f32,
    /// P(t): Prosodic Alignment component
    /// Range: 0.0 to 1.0
    pub p_t: f32,
    /// S(t): Semantic Goal Coherence component
    /// Range: 0.0 to 1.0
    pub s_t: f32,
    /// C(t): Chrono-Rhythmic Sync component
    /// Range: 0.0 to 1.0
    pub c_t: f32,
    /// σ(t): Noise/Uncertainty factor
    /// Range: 1.0+ (baseline 1.0, increases with dissonance)
    pub sigma_t: f32,
    /// Close Window Trigger
    /// If true, Prescience Engine filters for "CLOSING" strategies only
    pub trigger_close: bool,
}
```

**CRM Integration with Prescience Engine:**

When `trigger_close` is `true`, the Prescience Engine's `predict_best_trajectory` function receives a `force_close_mode` flag that restricts strategy selection to strategies tagged with `strategy_type: "CLOSING"`. This overrides normal physics-based strategy selection to capitalize on the detected Close Window.

impl OneiricEngine {
    const NEAR_MISS_LOW: f32 = -0.2;
    const NEAR_MISS_HIGH: f32 = 0.2;
    const DEFAULT_MAX_SIMULATIONS: u32 = 10_000;
    const DEFAULT_SUCCESS_THRESHOLD: f32 = 0.7;

    pub fn new(prescience: PrescienceEngine, memory: MemorySystem) -> Self {
        Self {
            prescience,
            memory,
            max_simulations: Self::DEFAULT_MAX_SIMULATIONS,
            success_threshold: Self::DEFAULT_SUCCESS_THRESHOLD,
            max_cpu_percent: 80,
        }
    }

    /// Run offline dreaming process
    /// Called when system has been idle for > 5 minutes
    pub async fn dream(&self) -> Result<Vec<OneiricMemory>, OneiricError> {
        let mut synthetic_memories = Vec::new();

        // Find all near-miss turns from recent sessions
        let near_misses = self.find_near_misses().await?;

        for near_miss in near_misses {
            if let Some(winning_strategy) = self.resimulate(&near_miss).await? {
                let memory = OneiricMemory {
                    original_session_id: near_miss.session_id.clone(),
                    original_turn: near_miss.turn_number,
                    simulated_strategy_id: winning_strategy.strategy_id,
                    confidence_score: winning_strategy.expected_value,
                    dream_depth: winning_strategy.simulation_count,
                    origin: StrategyOrigin::OneiricSynthesis,
                };
                synthetic_memories.push(memory);
            }
        }

        Ok(synthetic_memories)
    }

    /// Find near-miss turns from AgentDB using reflexion_retrieve
    ///
    /// IMPLEMENTATION MANDATE:
    /// Use AgentDB's reflexion_retrieve API to fetch past episodes:
    /// `agentdb.reflexion_retrieve({ task: intent_id, k: 10 })`
    ///
    /// This replaces generic transition table iteration with AgentDB-specific
    /// episode retrieval designed for counterfactual re-simulation.
    async fn find_near_misses(&self) -> Result<Vec<NearMissTurn>, OneiricError> {
        // Get all unique intent IDs from recent sessions
        let recent_intents = self.memory.reasoning.get_recent_intent_ids(100).await?;

        let mut near_misses = Vec::new();

        for intent_id in recent_intents {
            // Use AgentDB reflexion_retrieve API
            // API: agentdb.reflexion_retrieve({ task: intent_id, k: 10 })
            let episodes = self.memory.reasoning.db.reflexion_retrieve(ReflexionQuery {
                task: intent_id.clone(),
                k: 10,
            }).await?;

            for entry in episodes {
                // Parse the episode JSON stored in Reflexion
                if let Ok(episode) = serde_json::from_str::<ReflexionEpisode>(&entry.episode) {
                    // Filter for near-miss reward range
                    if episode.reward >= Self::NEAR_MISS_LOW && episode.reward <= Self::NEAR_MISS_HIGH {
                        near_misses.push(NearMissTurn {
                            session_id: episode.cognitive_state.session_id.clone(),
                            turn_number: episode.cognitive_state.turn_number,
                            original_state: episode.cognitive_state,
                            original_reward: episode.reward,
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        Ok(near_misses)
    }

    /// Re-simulate a near-miss turn to find winning strategy
    async fn resimulate(&self, near_miss: &NearMissTurn) -> Result<Option<WinningStrategy>, OneiricError> {
        let graph = self.memory.strategy.get_graph_access();
        let causal = self.memory.reasoning.get_causal_access();

        // Get all candidate strategies
        let candidates = graph.get_all_strategies_for_intent(
            &near_miss.original_state.intent_id,
        ).await;

        let mut best_strategy: Option<WinningStrategy> = None;
        let mut simulations_run: u32 = 0;

        for candidate in candidates {
            if simulations_run >= self.max_simulations {
                break;
            }

            // Run Monte Carlo simulations for this strategy
            let (ev, sim_count) = self.prescience.simulate_strategy_deep(
                &near_miss.original_state,
                &candidate,
                graph,
                causal,
                1000, // Simulations per strategy
            ).await;

            simulations_run += sim_count;

            if ev > self.success_threshold {
                if best_strategy.is_none() || ev > best_strategy.as_ref().unwrap().expected_value {
                    best_strategy = Some(WinningStrategy {
                        strategy_id: candidate.id.clone(),
                        expected_value: ev,
                        simulation_count: simulations_run,
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        Ok(best_strategy)
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
struct NearMissTurn {
    session_id: String,
    turn_number: u32,
    original_state: CognitiveState,
    original_reward: f32,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
struct WinningStrategy {
    strategy_id: String,
    expected_value: f32,
    simulation_count: u32,
}
```

**REQ-PHYS-009: Synthetic Strategy Injection**

If a winning path is found during dreaming, the system injects a **Synthetic Strategy** (a conversational approach, not an identity coordinate) into `RuVector` marked `origin: ONEIRIC_SYNTHESIS`.

```rust
impl OneiricEngine {
    /// Inject synthetic memory into RuVector
    pub async fn inject_synthetic_memory(
        &self,
        memory: &OneiricMemory,
        strategy_embedding: &[f32; 768],
    ) -> Result<(), OneiricError> {
        // Store in RuVector with ONEIRIC_SYNTHESIS origin
        self.memory.strategy.db.query(&format!(
            "CREATE (s:Strategy {{
                id: '{}',
                description: 'Synthetic strategy from Oneiric Engine dreaming',
                origin: 'ONEIRIC_SYNTHESIS',
                confidence_score: {},
                dream_depth: {},
                original_session_id: '{}',
                original_turn: {},
                created_at: datetime()
            }})",
            memory.simulated_strategy_id,
            memory.confidence_score,
            memory.dream_depth,
            memory.original_session_id,
            memory.original_turn,
        )).await?;

        // Store embedding vector
        self.memory.strategy.store_vector(
            &memory.simulated_strategy_id,
            strategy_embedding,
        ).await?;

        Ok(())
    }
}

/// Error types for Oneiric Engine
#[derive(Debug)]
pub enum OneiricError {
    /// Memory access error
    MemoryError(String),
    /// Simulation failed
    SimulationError(String),
    /// Injection failed
    InjectionError(String),
}
```

## 9. System Configuration Schema

**REQ-CONFIG-001: Centralized Configuration**

All system parameters MUST be configured through a single TOML file. The system MUST NOT use hardcoded values except for the critical constants listed below.

**Critical Non-Configurable Constants** (HARDCODED - DO NOT OVERRIDE):

| Constant | Value | Rationale |
|:---------|:------|:----------|
| `COMPOSITE_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD` | 0.97 | Security - Weighted Composite Score (sum of 6 stream similarities); lower values risk false identity matches |
| `SAFE_HARBOR_DURATION_SECONDS` | 60 | Psychology - shorter windows produce unreliable profiles |
| `SAFE_HARBOR_GAMMA` | 0.1 | Psychology - higher values create cold-start pressure |
| `DUPLICATE_SIMILARITY_THRESHOLD` | 0.99 | Deduplication - lower values over-prune unique failures |
