## 10. Layer 0: Universal Psychology

**REQ-L0-001: Universal Psychology Model**

| Content | Count | Status |
|:--------|:------|:-------|
| Hogshead Archetypes | 49 | Immutable (`&'static`) |
| Archetype Reference Sets | 49 Sets (Each set contains 5 independent vectors: 768, 512, 1024, 1, 42 dims) | Immutable |
| Emotion Reference Vectors | 7 (1024-dim each) | Immutable |
| Sentiment Reference Vectors | 2 (positive/negative, 768-dim) | Immutable |

**REQ-L0-002: Archetype Reference Sets Data**

The system acts on the assumption that 49 verified reference sets exist.

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **File Path** | `./data/profiles/hogshead_reference_vectors.bin` |
| **Format** | Binary serialized `HashMap<ArchetypeId, NorthStarReferenceSet>` |
| **Loading** | Deserialized at startup using `bincode` |
| **Validation** | Binary MUST panic at startup if file is missing |
| **Agent Responsibility** | Load reference sets only. Agent does NOT generate these vectors. |

```rust
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::fs::File;
use std::io::BufReader;

/// Path to the pre-computed archetype reference sets (5-vector per archetype)
pub const ARCHETYPE_REFERENCE_SETS_PATH: &str = "./data/profiles/hogshead_reference_vectors.bin";

/// Load archetype reference sets at startup
///
/// CRITICAL: Panics if file is missing - this is intentional.
pub fn load_archetype_reference_sets() -> HashMap<ArchetypeId, NorthStarReferenceSet> {
    let file = File::open(ARCHETYPE_REFERENCE_SETS_PATH)
        .expect("FATAL: Archetype reference sets file not found. System cannot start.");

    let reader = BufReader::new(file);

    let reference_sets: HashMap<ArchetypeId, NorthStarReferenceSet> = bincode::deserialize_from(reader)
        .expect("FATAL: Failed to deserialize archetype reference sets.");

    if reference_sets.len() != 49 {
        panic!(
            "FATAL: Expected 49 archetype reference sets, found {}.",
            reference_sets.len()
        );
    }

    reference_sets
}
```

### 10.1 The 49 Personality Archetypes

The system uses 49 archetypes derived from 7 Primary × 7 Secondary Hogshead Advantage combinations.

| Primary Advantage | Description | Physics Profile |
|:------------------|:------------|:----------------|
| Innovation | Creates new ideas | Low gamma, high entropy tolerance |
| Passion | Builds relationships | Medium gamma, balanced |
| Power | Commands attention | High gamma, low entropy tolerance |
| Prestige | Sets standards | High gamma, precise |
| Trust | Builds loyalty | Low gamma, high stability |
| Mystique | Observes carefully | Medium gamma, reserved |
| Alert | Focuses details | Medium gamma, precise |

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
pub struct ArchetypeId(pub u8);

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct Archetype {
    pub id: ArchetypeId,
    pub name: &'static str,
    pub primary_advantage: Advantage,
    pub secondary_advantage: Advantage,
    pub complementary_id: ArchetypeId,
    pub physics_weights: PhysicsWeights,
    pub behavior: ArchetypeBehavior,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
pub struct ArchetypeBehavior {
    pub assertiveness: f32,  // 0.0 to 1.0
    pub warmth: f32,         // 0.0 to 1.0
    pub pace: f32,           // 0.0 to 1.0 (slow to fast)
    pub formality: f32,      // 0.0 to 1.0
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
pub enum Advantage {
    Innovation,
    Passion,
    Power,
    Prestige,
    Trust,
    Mystique,
    Alert,
}

#[derive(Debug)]
pub struct UniversalPsychology {
    pub archetypes: Vec<Archetype>,
    pub north_star_reference_sets: HashMap<ArchetypeId, NorthStarReferenceSet>,
    pub emotion_reference_vectors: HashMap<Emotion, [f32; 1024]>,
    pub sentiment_reference_vectors: SentimentReferenceVectors,
    pub cultural_baselines: HashMap<String, CulturalBaseline>,
}

#[derive(Debug)]
pub struct SentimentReferenceVectors {
    pub positive: [f32; 768],
    pub negative: [f32; 768],
}
```

### 10.2 Cultural Baseline Definition

**REQ-L0-003: Cultural Baseline Structure**

```rust
/// Cultural baseline parameters for locale-specific normalization
/// Loaded from config/cognitive_physics.toml [cultural_norms.*] sections
#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Deserialize)]
pub struct CulturalBaseline {
    /// Expected speaking pace for this culture (words per minute)
    /// en-US: 150, ja-JP: 110, de-DE: 130
    pub baseline_pace_wpm: f32,

    /// Maximum acceptable silence before it generates entropy (seconds)
    /// en-US: 1.5s, ja-JP: 4.0s (high-context = silence is normal)
    pub silence_tolerance_sec: f32,

    /// How direct is communication in this culture (0.0 = indirect, 1.0 = direct)
    /// en-US: 0.8, ja-JP: 0.2, de-DE: 0.7
    pub directness_bias: f32,

    /// Minimum expected formality level (0.0 = casual OK, 1.0 = formal required)
    /// en-US: 0.3, ja-JP: 0.8
    pub formality_floor: f32,
}

impl CulturalBaseline {
    /// Default baseline (en-US)
    pub fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            baseline_pace_wpm: 150.0,
            silence_tolerance_sec: 1.5,
            directness_bias: 0.8,
            formality_floor: 0.3,
        }
    }
}
```

### 10.3 North Star Reference Set Structure

**REQ-L0-004: North Star Reference Set Structure**

Each of the 49 archetypes has a pre-computed set of reference vectors used for classification. Audio-based streams (Tone, Emotion) are split by gender to account for acoustic physiological differences between male and female voices, preventing acoustic averaging ("muddying") of centroids. Text-based streams (Semantic, Style, Action, Chronemic) remain gender-neutral.

```rust
/// Pre-computed set of reference vectors.
/// Audio streams (Tone, Emotion) are split by gender to account for acoustic physiological differences.
/// Text/Logic streams (Semantic, Style, Action, Chronemic) remain unified.
#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
pub struct NorthStarReferenceSet {
    pub archetype_id: ArchetypeId,

    // === Shared Streams (Gender Neutral) ===
    /// Stream A: Semantic reference vector (768-dim Nomic)
    pub semantic: [f32; 768],
    /// Stream D: Style reference value (formality scalar 0.0-1.0)
    pub style: f32,
    /// Stream E: Action reference vector (42-dim dialog act probabilities)
    pub action: [f32; 42],
    /// Stream F: Chronemic reference vector (4-dim timing features)
    pub chronemic: [f32; 4],

    // === Gender-Specific Audio Streams ===
    /// Stream B (Male): Tone reference vector derived from male voice samples
    pub tone_male: [f32; 512],
    /// Stream B (Female): Tone reference vector derived from female voice samples
    pub tone_female: [f32; 512],

    /// Stream C (Male): Emotion reference vector derived from male voice samples
    pub emotion_male: [f32; 1024],
    /// Stream C (Female): Emotion reference vector derived from female voice samples
    pub emotion_female: [f32; 1024],
}

/// Gender classification for audio stream processing
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
pub enum Gender {
    Male,
    Female,
}
```

**REQ-L0-004a: Gender-Specific Vector Selection at Runtime**

At runtime, the system selects the appropriate gender-specific reference vectors based on the detected gender of the user:

| User Gender | Tone Reference Used | Emotion Reference Used |
|:------------|:--------------------|:-----------------------|
| Male | `tone_male` | `emotion_male` |
| Female | `tone_female` | `emotion_female` |

**Rationale for Gender Separation:**

| Acoustic Property | Male Voice Characteristics | Female Voice Characteristics |
|:------------------|:---------------------------|:-----------------------------|
| **Fundamental Frequency** | 85-180 Hz | 165-255 Hz |
| **Formant Frequencies** | Lower F1-F4 values | Higher F1-F4 values |
| **Vocal Tract Length** | ~17 cm average | ~14 cm average |
| **Harmonic Richness** | More overtones in lower register | Clearer upper harmonics |

These physiological differences cause gender-averaged centroids to occupy a "middle ground" in the embedding space that represents neither male nor female voices accurately, reducing classification precision.

### 11.1 Unified Binary Architecture

```
cognitive-radar/

│   ├── cognitive-core/        # Physics engine, Prescience Engine (GPU MCTS), profiling
│   │   ├── src/
```

### 11.2 Frontend Communication Layer

**REQ-ARCH-004: Frontend Real-Time Bridge**

The system exposes a WebSocket server via the `cognitive-bridge` crate to power the Hexa-Modal Cockpit.

| Data Type | Direction | Frequency | Payload Description |
|:----------|:----------|:----------|:--------------------|
| **Stream Telemetry** | Server → Client | 60Hz | Hexa-modal output (Valence, Arousal, Entropy, Identity similarity) |
| **Trajectory Update** | Server → Client | 1Hz | Reduced dimension coordinates for UMAP visualization |
| **Critical Alerts** | Server → Client | Event-Driven | Safety Stop triggers, Identity Mismatch warnings |
| **Manual Takeover** | Client → Server | Event-Driven | Stop TTS, enable operator microphone |
| **Archetype Override** | Client → Server | Event-Driven | Operator manually selects correct archetype |
| **Strategy Injection** | Client → Server | Event-Driven | New strategy text for embedding and storage |

### 11.3 Database Role Clarification

**REQ-ARCH-002: Storage System Roles**

| Database | Purpose | Capabilities Used |
|:---------|:--------|:------------------|
| **RuVector** | Strategy Brain | **`@ruvector/graph-node`**: `GraphDatabase` class for Hypergraph storage of Intent↔Strategy mapping. Uses `createNode`, `createEdge`, `query()` APIs. **`@ruvector/core`**: HNSW indexing for semantic vector search via `vectorSearch()`. Distance metric: Cosine. |
| **LanceDB** | Identity Brain | **Native Rust**: Append-only storage for high-dimensional Voice X-Vectors (512-dim WavLM) and "Ghost Replay" execution holograms (vectors + metadata for performance cues). |
| **AgentDB** | Reasoning Brain | **`ReasoningBank`**: `db.reasoningBank.store({ pattern, context, reasoning, outcome, confidence })` for storing successful strategy patterns. **`CausalMemory`**: `causal_add_edge({ cause, effect, uplift, confidence })` for tracking Strategy→Goal uplift (Impact Factor for MCTS). `causal_query({ cause, min_confidence })` for retrieval. **`Reflexion`**: `reflexion_store({ task, episode, outcome })` and `reflexion_retrieve({ task, k })` for storing/retrieving near-miss episodes for Oneiric Engine replay. |

**REQ-ARCH-002a: MemorySystem Definition**

```rust
/// Unified memory system providing access to all storage databases
pub struct MemorySystem {
    /// Strategy storage (RuVector GraphDatabase): North Stars, Anti-Patterns, GoalNodes, MilestoneNodes
    /// Uses @ruvector/graph-node APIs: createNode, createEdge, query, vectorSearch
    pub strategy: StrategyBrain,
    /// Identity & Holographic storage (LanceDB): Voice X-Vectors, Profile history, Ghost Replay holograms
    pub identity: IdentityBrain,
    /// Reasoning storage (AgentDB): ReasoningBank patterns, CausalMemory impact factors, Reflexion episodes
    /// Uses AgentDB APIs: reasoningBank.store, causal_add_edge, causal_query, reflexion_store, reflexion_retrieve
    pub reasoning: ReasoningBrain,
}

impl MemorySystem {
    pub async fn new() -> Result<Self, MemoryError> {
        Ok(Self {
            strategy: StrategyBrain::new().await?,
            identity: IdentityBrain::new().await?,
            reasoning: ReasoningBrain::new().await?,
        })
    }
}
```

### 11.4 Processing Pipeline

**REQ-ARCH-003: Turn Processing Flow with Cultural Lens**

**REQ-PRIMING-001: Priming Controller Implementation**

The Priming Controller implements vocabulary steering via Prompt Injection for Candle/GGUF compatibility (CONST-010). Token-level logit bias is not supported by the inference engine.

```rust
// cognitive-inference/src/priming.rs

/// Priming implementation for Candle/GGUF (CONST-010: no logit bias support)
/// Uses prompt injection + post-hoc validation instead of token manipulation
pub struct PrimingController {
    /// Priming words to encourage in responses
    pub priming_words: Vec<String>,
    /// Session-scoped tracking of priming word usage
    pub words_used_this_session: usize,
    /// Target density per minute (from config)
    pub target_density_per_minute: f32,
    /// Minimum density threshold for validation (from config)
    pub validation_threshold: f32,
    /// Whether priming is enabled (from config)
    pub enabled: bool,
}

/// Configuration for Priming (loaded from [priming] TOML section)
#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Deserialize)]
pub struct PrimingConfig {
    pub enabled: bool,
    pub words: Vec<String>,
    pub target_density_per_minute: f32,
    pub validation_threshold: f32,
}

impl PrimingController {
    /// Create new PrimingController from configuration
    pub fn new(config: &PrimingConfig) -> Self {
        Self {
            priming_words: config.words.clone(),
            words_used_this_session: 0,
            target_density_per_minute: config.target_density_per_minute,
            validation_threshold: config.validation_threshold,
            enabled: config.enabled,
        }
    }

    /// Generate system prompt injection for priming
    ///
    /// CONST-010 COMPLIANCE: This is the core mechanism for vocabulary steering
    /// without logit bias. The injection string becomes part of the system prompt.
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    /// * `elapsed_secs` - Seconds elapsed in current session
    /// * `phase` - Current conversation phase (affects priming intensity)
    ///
    /// # Returns
    /// Prompt injection string (empty if no priming needed)
    pub fn generate_prompt_injection(
        &self,
        elapsed_secs: u64,
        phase: ConversationPhase,
    ) -> String {
        if !self.enabled {
            return String::new();
        }

        // Calculate expected vs actual priming word usage
        let expected = (elapsed_secs as f32 / 60.0 * self.target_density_per_minute) as usize;
        let deficit = expected.saturating_sub(self.words_used_this_session);

        // Only prime during Rapport building or if deficit is high
        if deficit == 0 && phase != ConversationPhase::Rapport {
            return String::new();
        }

        // Generate prompt-based priming instruction
        format!(
            r#"
[LANGUAGE GUIDANCE]
Use warm, affirmative language. Incorporate words like: {}.
Current usage: {}/{} target. Increase usage naturally where appropriate.
"#,
            self.priming_words.join(", "),
            self.words_used_this_session,
            expected
        )
    }

    /// Count priming words in generated response (post-hoc tracking)
    ///
    /// Called after each response generation to update session statistics
    pub fn count_and_update(&mut self, response: &str) {
        let response_lower = response.to_lowercase();
        for word in &self.priming_words {
            self.words_used_this_session += response_lower.matches(word.as_str()).count();
        }
    }

    /// Validate response meets minimum priming threshold
    ///
    /// CONST-010 COMPLIANCE: Post-hoc validation since we cannot control
    /// token generation directly. Returns regeneration hint if density too low.
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    /// * `response` - Generated response text
    /// * `elapsed_secs` - Seconds elapsed in session
    ///
    /// # Returns
    /// Some(hint) if regeneration needed, None if validation passes
    pub fn validate_response(&self, response: &str, elapsed_secs: u64) -> Option<String> {
        if !self.enabled {
            return None;
        }

        let word_count = self.count_priming_words(response);
        let response_word_count = response.split_whitespace().count();
        let density = word_count as f32 / response_word_count.max(1) as f32;

        // Only enforce validation in first 120 seconds (rapport phase)
        if density < self.validation_threshold && elapsed_secs < 120 {
            Some("Rephrase with more affirmative language (certainly, happy to, easy).".into())
        } else {
            None
        }
    }

    /// Count priming words in text (internal helper)
    fn count_priming_words(&self, text: &str) -> usize {
        let lower = text.to_lowercase();
        self.priming_words
            .iter()
            .map(|w| lower.matches(w.as_str()).count())
            .sum()
    }

    /// Reset session tracking (call at session start)
    pub fn reset_session(&mut self) {
        self.words_used_this_session = 0;
    }
}
```

**REQ-GEN-001: Context Serialization for LLM with Dignity Protocol**

The Qwen 3 14B FP8 model processes **text only**. The `CognitiveState` and `NorthStar` vectors MUST be converted to a structured System Prompt Context String before generation.

**REQ-ARCH-003a: Semantic Telemetry (LLM HUD)**

The system MUST inject vector-derived gradients directly into the prompt to guide the LLM's linguistic shifts.

| Telemetry Component | Description |
|:--------------------|:------------|
| Current Position | User's VAK modality state and entropy level |
| Vector Correction | Formality and pace delta percentages |
| Semantic Pivot | Required intent transition path |
| Bridge Metaphor | Instruction for connecting current state to target |

**System Prompt Format with Teleology, Ghost Replay, Priming, and Semantic Telemetry:**

```
[CULTURAL LENS]
Locale: {locale}
Dignity Rule: {dignity_instruction}

[SYSTEM CONTEXT]
User ID: {user_id} (Verified: {identity_verified})
Archetype Profile: {primary_archetype_name} / {secondary_archetype_name}

[TELEOLOGY - CURRENT GOAL: {goal_name}]
Progress: {progress_percent:.0}%
Completed: {completed_milestones}
>> CURRENT MILESTONE: "{current_milestone_description}" (Mandatory: {current_mandatory})
Next: "{next_milestone_description}"

[PHYSICS TELEMETRY]
Current Position: User is in "{vak_modality}" state (Entropy: {entropy:.2}).
Vector Correction: Apply {formality_delta:+.0}% Formality, {pace_delta:+.0}% Pace.
Required Semantic Pivot: Move from "{current_intent}" -> "{target_intent}".
>>> INSTRUCTION: Use a "Bridge Metaphor" connecting [{vak_modality}] to [Solution Space].

[STRATEGY GUIDANCE]
North Star Strategy: {north_star_description}
EV: {prescience_ev:.2}

[LANGUAGE GUIDANCE]
Use warm, affirmative language. Incorporate words like: {priming_words}.
Current usage: {words_used}/{expected_words} target. Increase usage naturally where appropriate.

[PERFORMANCE CUES - GHOST REPLAY]
Target Tone: Match stored win profile (Similarity required: High)
Pacing: Speak at {holo_wpm:.0} WPM (Latency: {holo_latency:.0}ms)

[PHYSICS - UTL STATUS]
Learning Power (L): {l_value:.3} (Target: >0.6)
Total Loss (J): {j_loss:.3} (Target: <0.3)
Phase Alignment: {phase_cosine:.2} (1.0=Sync, -1.0=Clash)
Dyna-Lambdas: Task={lambda_task:.1}, Sem={lambda_semantic:.1}, Dyn={lambda_dyn:.1}
Goal: Minimize Loss (J) by synchronizing Phase (φ).
```

**Note:** The `[LANGUAGE GUIDANCE]` section is dynamically injected by the `PrimingController` when a priming word deficit exists. It is omitted when priming is disabled or the target density has been met.

```rust
/// Serialize CognitiveState to text prompt with Teleology, Semantic Telemetry, and UTL Physics
///
/// CRITICAL: Qwen 3 14B FP8 is a text-based LLM. It cannot process raw float vectors.
/// This function converts all vector-derived insights into natural language context
/// and injects:
/// - Cultural Lens dignity protocol
/// - Teleology block (goal progress and milestone checklist)
/// - Semantic Telemetry HUD
/// - UTL Physics status (Learning Power L, Total Loss J, Phase Alignment)
/// - Priming guidance (CONST-010: prompt injection for vocabulary steering)
/// - Ghost Replay performance cues
///
/// # Arguments
/// * `cognitive_state` - Current hexa-modal cognitive state
/// * `north_star` - Selected strategy from RuVector
/// * `hologram` - Optional Ghost Replay execution template
/// * `goal_status` - Teleological engine goal/milestone status
/// * `utl_result` - UTL Physics engine result (L, J, phase_cosine, components)
/// * `prescience_ev` - Expected value from MCTS simulation
/// * `archetype_registry` - Registry of archetype definitions
/// * `priming_instruction` - Priming injection string from PrimingController
pub fn serialize_context_for_llm(
    cognitive_state: &CognitiveState,
    north_star: &StrategyResult,
    hologram: Option<&HolographicExecution>,
    goal_status: &GoalStatus,
    utl_result: &UtlResult,
    prescience_ev: f32,
    archetype_registry: &HashMap<ArchetypeId, Archetype>,
    priming_instruction: &str,
) -> String {
    let primary = archetype_registry.get(&cognitive_state.primary_archetype)
        .map(|a| a.name)
        .unwrap_or("Unknown");
    let secondary = archetype_registry.get(&cognitive_state.secondary_archetype)
        .map(|a| a.name)
        .unwrap_or("Unknown");

    // Select Dignity Protocol based on Locale
    let dignity_instruction = get_dignity_instruction(&cognitive_state.locale);

    // Format Holographic Cues (Ghost Replay)
    let (holo_wpm, holo_latency, holo_valence, holo_arousal, holo_style) = match hologram {
        Some(h) => (h.wpm, h.latency_ms, h.valence, h.arousal, h.style_score),
        None => (0.0, 0.0, 0.5, 0.5, 0.5), // Defaults
    };

    // Calculate Vector Gradients for Telemetry
    let formality_delta = north_star.target_style - cognitive_state.style_score;
    let pace_delta = north_star.target_wpm - cognitive_state.chronemics[0];

    // Construct the Teleology Block (The Checklist)
    // This explicitly tells the LLM what milestones have been completed,
    // what the current goal is, and what the next milestone should be.
    let current_milestone = goal_status.current_milestone.as_ref();
    let next_milestone = goal_status.next_milestone.as_ref();

    let teleology_block = format!(
        r#"[TELEOLOGY - CURRENT GOAL: {}]
Progress: {:.0}%
Completed: {:?}
>> CURRENT MILESTONE: "{}" (Mandatory: {})
Next: "{}""#,
        goal_status.name,
        goal_status.progress_percent,
        goal_status.completed_milestones,
        current_milestone.map(|m| m.description.as_str()).unwrap_or("GOAL COMPLETE"),
        current_milestone.map(|m| m.mandatory).unwrap_or(false),
        next_milestone.map(|m| m.description.as_str()).unwrap_or("N/A"),
    );

    // Construct the Telemetry Block
    let telemetry_block = format!(
        r#"[PHYSICS TELEMETRY]
Current Position: User is in "{}" state (Entropy: {:.2}).
Vector Correction: Apply {:+.0}% Formality, {:+.0}% Pace.
Required Semantic Pivot: Move from "{}" -> "{}".
>>> INSTRUCTION: Use a "Bridge Metaphor" connecting [{}] to [Solution Space]."#,
        cognitive_state.vak_modality.description(),
        learning_signal.value,
        formality_delta * 100.0,
        pace_delta * 100.0,
        cognitive_state.intent_id,
        north_star.description,
        cognitive_state.vak_modality.description(),
    );

    // Build priming block only if instruction is non-empty
    let priming_block = if priming_instruction.is_empty() {
        String::new()
    } else {
        format!("\n{}", priming_instruction)
    };

    format!(
        r#"[CULTURAL LENS]
Locale: {}
Dignity Rule: {}

[SYSTEM CONTEXT]
User ID: {} (Verified: {})
Archetype Profile: {} / {}

{}

{}

[STRATEGY GUIDANCE]
North Star Strategy: {}
EV: {:.2}
{}
[PERFORMANCE CUES - GHOST REPLAY]
Target Tone: Match stored win profile (Similarity required: High)
Pacing: Speak at {:.0} WPM (Latency: {:.0}ms)
Emotion Target: Valence {:.2}, Arousal {:.2}
Formality: {:.2}

[PHYSICS - UTL STATUS]
Learning Power (L): {:.3} (Target: >0.6)
Total Loss (J): {:.3} (Target: <0.3)
Phase Alignment: {:.2} (1.0=Sync, -1.0=Clash)
Dyna-Lambdas: Task={:.1}, Sem={:.1}, Dyn={:.1}
Goal: Minimize Loss (J) by synchronizing Phase (φ)."#,
        cognitive_state.locale,
        dignity_instruction,
        cognitive_state.user_id,
        cognitive_state.identity_verified,
        primary,
        secondary,
        teleology_block,
        telemetry_block,
        north_star.description,
        prescience_ev,
        priming_block,
        holo_wpm, holo_latency, holo_valence, holo_arousal, holo_style,
        utl_result.l_value,
        utl_result.j_loss,
        utl_result.phase_cosine,
        utl_result.components[0], // Task
        utl_result.components[1], // Semantic
        utl_result.components[2], // Dynamic
    )
}

/// Get dignity instruction based on locale
///
/// These protocols ensure culturally-appropriate communication
fn get_dignity_instruction(locale: &str) -> &'static str {
    match locale {
        "ja-JP" => "PROTOCOL: High Context. Preserve 'Face'. Do not disagree directly. Use indirect suggestions.",
        "en-US" => "PROTOCOL: Low Context. Value Efficiency. Be direct and clear.",
        "de-DE" => "PROTOCOL: Precision. Value accuracy over harmony. Be technically precise.",
        "zh-CN" => "PROTOCOL: High Context. Respect hierarchy. Use respectful forms of address.",
        "br-PT" => "PROTOCOL: Relationship-focused. Build rapport before business. Be warm.",
        "fr-FR" => "PROTOCOL: Balanced. Moderate formality. Acknowledge expertise.",
        _ => "PROTOCOL: Universal. Be polite, clear, and respectful.",
    }
}

async fn process_turn(
    audio: AudioFrame,
    session: &mut SessionState,
    memory: &MemorySystem,
    models: &ModelRegistry,
    profiling: &ProfilingEngine,
    physics: &PhysicsEngine,
    analyzer: &CognitiveAnalyzer,
    teleology: &mut TeleologicalEngine,
) -> Result<TurnResponse, ProcessingError> {
    // PHASE 0: Parallel Stream Extraction (Grouped GEMM on Context B)
    // Launch single fused kernel for Streams A-E via cuBLAS Grouped GEMM
    let mut cognitive_state = analyzer.analyze(
        &audio.buffer,
        &audio.transcript,
        &audio.turn_timing,
        &session.locale,
    ).await?;

    // PHASE 1: Apply Cultural Lens Normalization
    // This MUST happen before Physics calculation
    physics.apply_cultural_lens(&mut cognitive_state);

    // PHASE 1.5: Teleological State Update
    // Check if user utterance semantically matches any pending milestones.
    // Returns ΔG (goal progress delta) for Physics Engine.
    let delta_goal = teleology.update_state(&mut cognitive_state);

    // PHASE 1.6: Hardship Protocol Check
    // Check transcript for crisis keywords (hospital, cancer, died, lost my job, etc.)
    // If detected, override physics weights for this turn to prioritize empathy.
    // This ensures we don't pressure someone who just said "I lost my job".
    if crate::core::defense::check_hardship_trigger(&audio.transcript) {
        // Override physics weights for this turn
        // Force Gamma 0.1, Force Empathetic TTS
        // Logic handled inside Physics Engine or via temporary session override
        session.trigger_hardship_mode();
    }

    // PHASE 2: Check Safety Stop
    if cognitive_state.safety_stop {
        return handle_safety_stop(&cognitive_state, session).await;
    }

    // PHASE 3: Profiling Logic & Fast-Track Identity Verification
    //
    // EXIT CONDITIONS for Safe Harbor:
    // A. Fast-Track Exit: Weighted Composite Confidence Score > 0.97 (Hexa-Modal Fusion)
    //    → Hydrate buffer from historical profile → Lock archetype immediately
    // B. Standard Exit: T >= 60s AND sufficient data accumulated
    //    → Calculate archetype from buffer → Lock
    //
    // Fast-Track enables returning users to be served with their personalized
    // archetype profile on the FIRST TURN of a new session.

    // Check if Identity was verified this turn (Fast-Track Path)
    if cognitive_state.identity_verified && !session.archetype_locked {
        // FAST-TRACK: Identity verified via Hexa-Modal Fusion
        // Hydrate buffer with historical profile data for immediate archetype calculation
        if let Some(ref history) = cognitive_state.historical_profile {
            session.safe_harbor_buffer.hydrate_from_history(history);
        }

        // Buffer now has sufficient data (from hydration), calculate immediately
        let classification = profiling.calculate_archetype(&session.safe_harbor_buffer)?;
        session.lock_archetype(classification);

        // Log Fast-Track event for metrics
        session.metrics.fast_track_exit = true;
        session.metrics.fast_track_turn = session.turn_count;
        session.metrics.identity_similarity = cognitive_state.identity_similarity;
    }

    // Determine Physics Weights based on current state
    let physics_weights = if session.archetype_locked {
        // ACTIVE MODE: Archetype locked (via Fast-Track or Standard exit)
        profiling.get_weights_for_archetype(&session.locked_archetype.primary)
    } else if session.elapsed_seconds() < 60 {
        // DISCOVERY MODE: Still in Safe Harbor, no identity match yet
        session.safe_harbor_buffer.accumulate(&cognitive_state);
        PhysicsWeights::safe_harbor()
    } else {
        // STANDARD EXIT: Time expired, force archetype calculation
        let classification = profiling.calculate_archetype(&session.safe_harbor_buffer)?;
        session.lock_archetype(classification);
        profiling.get_weights_for_archetype(&classification.primary)
    };

    // PHASE 4: UTL Physics Calculation
    // Calculate phase angle between Entropy and Coherence vectors
    let phase_angle = physics.calculate_phase_angle(
        &session.previous_semantic_embedding,
        &cognitive_state.semantic_embedding,
    );

    // Calculate task and meaning errors for UTL Loss function
    let task_error = 1.0 - cognitive_state.goal_progress_score;
    let meaning_error = 1.0 - cognitive_state.semantic_coherence;

    // Calculate UTL Physics (L and J)
    let utl_result = physics.calculate_utl_physics(
        session.delta_entropy,
        session.delta_coherence,
        phase_angle,
        task_error,
        meaning_error,
        &cognitive_state,
        &physics_weights,
    );

    // PHASE 4.5: Get Current Milestone for Goal-Directed Processing
    // The Teleological Engine provides the active milestone for:
    // 1. Prescience Engine simulation (Teleological Reward)
    // 2. Strategy retrieval prioritization (Goal-Directed Search)
    let goal_status = teleology.get_goal_status();
    let current_milestone = goal_status.current_milestone.as_ref();

    // PHASE 4.6: Prescience Engine (GPU Context C - 10,000+ parallel simulations)
    // Simulate 20 steps ahead using RuVector Graph + AgentDB Causal Links
    // Runs on Green Context C with cuBLAS batched operations
    // Simulations that achieve the current milestone receive massive EV bonus
    let (best_strategy_id, expected_value) = physics.prescience.predict_best_trajectory(
        &cognitive_state,
        memory.strategy.get_graph_access(),
        memory.reasoning.get_causal_access(),
        current_milestone,
    ).await;

    // PHASE 5: Strategy Lookup (RuVector) with Goal-Oriented Prioritization
    //
    // STRATEGY RETRIEVAL LOGIC:
    // A. Goal-Directed Search (Primary): If we have a Current Milestone, prioritize
    //    strategies specifically designed to advance that milestone.
    // B. Semantic Search (Fallback/Augment): Include context-relevant strategies
    //    based on user's semantic embedding for responsiveness to direct questions.
    // C. Merge and Deduplicate: Combine candidates with goal-directed strategies first.
    //
    // This ensures the system pursues business objectives (milestones) rather than
    // simply reacting to whatever the user happens to say.

    let mut north_star_candidates: Vec<StrategyResult> = Vec::new();

    // A. Goal-Directed Search (Primary)
    // If we have a current milestone, find strategies specifically designed to advance it
    if let Some(milestone) = current_milestone {
        let milestone_strategies = memory.strategy.find_strategies_for_milestone(
            &milestone.id,
            session.locked_archetype.primary,
            cognitive_state.vak_modality,
        ).await?;
        north_star_candidates.extend(milestone_strategies);
    }

    // B. Semantic Search (Fallback/Augment)
    // Include context-relevant strategies in case user asks a direct question
    // These are searched based on what the user said (semantic embedding)
    let semantic_strategies = memory.strategy.vector_search(
        &cognitive_state.semantic_embedding,
        5, // limit to top 5
        None,
    ).await?;

    // Add semantic strategies that aren't already in the list (deduplication by ID)
    let existing_ids: std::collections::HashSet<_> = north_star_candidates
        .iter()
        .map(|s| s.strategy_id.clone())
        .collect();

    for strategy in semantic_strategies {
        if !existing_ids.contains(&strategy.strategy_id) {
            north_star_candidates.push(strategy);
        }
    }

    // C. Select best strategy from merged candidates
    // Prefer goal-directed strategies (first in list) unless semantic match is significantly better
    let north_star = if let Some(first) = north_star_candidates.first() {
        first.clone()
    } else {
        // No strategies found - use exploratory fallback
        StrategyResult::exploratory_for_profile(
            session.locked_archetype.primary,
            cognitive_state.vak_modality,
        )
    };

    // PHASE 5.5: Retrieve Holographic Execution (Ghost Replay)
    let hologram = memory.identity.get_hologram_for_strategy(&best_strategy_id).await.ok();

    // PHASE 6: Priming & Context Serialization
    // Generate priming injection string based on session phase and word deficit
    // CONST-010 COMPLIANCE: Candle/GGUF does not support logit bias
    let elapsed_seconds = session.elapsed_seconds();
    let conversation_phase = session.get_phase();

    let priming_instruction = models.priming_controller.generate_prompt_injection(
        elapsed_seconds,
        conversation_phase,
    );

    // Serialize context with priming instruction and UTL physics
    let system_context = serialize_context_for_llm(
        &cognitive_state,
        &north_star,
        hologram.as_ref(),
        &goal_status,
        &utl_result,
        expected_value,
        &profiling.archetype_registry,
        &priming_instruction,
    );

    // PHASE 7: Response Generation (Qwen 3 FP8) with Priming Validation
    // Uses "Non-Thinking" (Instruct) mode for strict <50ms compliance.
    // CONST-010 COMPLIANCE: Candle/GGUF flow: Generate -> Validate -> (Optional) Regenerate
    //
    // The priming instruction is injected into the system prompt. After generation,
    // we validate the response density and regenerate with explicit hint if needed.

    // 7.1 Generate initial response with priming (Instruct mode for real-time)
    let mut response = models.brain_model.generate_with_priming(
        &system_context,
        &audio.transcript,
        &priming_instruction,
        256, // max tokens
        InferenceMode::Instruct, // FORCE non-thinking mode for speed
    ).await?;

    // 7.2 Validate Priming Density (Post-Hoc Check)
    // If validation fails (density too low in rapport phase), try one regeneration
    if let Some(refinement_hint) = models.priming_controller.validate_response(
        &response.text,
        elapsed_seconds,
    ) {
        // Regenerate with explicit refinement hint added to context
        log::info!(
            "PRIMING: Validation failed (density < threshold). Regenerating with hint: {}",
            refinement_hint
        );

        let refined_context = format!("{}\n[REFINEMENT]: {}", system_context, refinement_hint);
        response = models.brain_model.generate_with_priming(
            &refined_context,
            &audio.transcript,
            &priming_instruction,
            256,
            InferenceMode::Instruct, // FORCE non-thinking mode for speed
        ).await?;
    }

    // 7.3 Update Priming Stats (Session Tracking)
    // Count priming words in final response for next turn's deficit calculation
    models.priming_controller.count_and_update(&response.text);

    // PHASE 8: TTS & Trust Voice DSP
    let tts_style = physics_weights.tts_style;
    let mut audio_response = models.tts_model.synthesize(&response.text, tts_style).await?;

    // DETERMINE LFM TRIGGER (Leapable Frequency Modulation)
    // Trigger only during critical persuasion moments:
    // 1. Current milestone is mandatory and we are in a "Closing" or "Offer" strategy
    // 2. Or Physics Engine explicitly requested "Force Close"
    let trigger_lfm = if let Some(milestone) = current_milestone {
        // Check strategy description or metadata for offer/close intent
        north_star.description.to_lowercase().contains("close") ||
        north_star.description.to_lowercase().contains("offer") ||
        north_star.description.to_lowercase().contains("agreement") ||
        // Also trigger if resonance R(t) > 0.82 (High Receptivity)
        utl_result.trigger_close
    } else {
        false
    };

    // APPLY TRUST VOICE DSP (REQ-AUDIO-006)
    // Applies EQ + Compression + Saturation
    // Inject LFM (-18dB Gamma Glide) if trigger_lfm is true
    audio.trust_voice_processor.apply_trust_dsp(&mut audio_response, trigger_lfm);

    // APPLY VPCE PHASE-LOCKING (REQ-AUDIO-007)
    // Align TTS output phase with user's speech rhythm for unconscious rapport
    // Uses Stream B F0 contour and instantaneous phase from last user utterance
    let vpce_coherence = audio.vpce_processor.align_phase(
        &mut audio_response,
        &cognitive_state.f0_contour,
        cognitive_state.instantaneous_phase,
    );
    // Update CognitiveState with achieved phase coherence
    cognitive_state.phase_coherence = vpce_coherence;

    // PHASE 9: Learning & Storage
    //
    // This phase performs storage operations across all three databases:
    // 1. Identity (LanceDB): append_profile_snapshot for long-term tracking
    // 2. Reasoning (AgentDB): ReasoningBank, CausalMemory, and Reflexion storage
    // 3. Strategy (RuVector): Dual-write logic via createNode API
    //
    // IMPLEMENTATION MANDATE:
    // - Use AgentDB APIs for reasoning storage (NOT generic transition tables)
    // - Use RuVector createNode/createEdge APIs for strategy storage

    // 9.1 Identity Storage (LanceDB)
    // Store hexa-modal profile snapshot for long-term tracking
    memory.identity.append_profile_snapshot(
        &cognitive_state.user_id,
        &cognitive_state,
        session.turn_count,
    ).await?;

    // Check for any pending human vote override from previous Shadow Slot review
    let human_vote = memory.reasoning.get_pending_human_vote(
        &session.id,
        session.turn_count,
    ).await.ok().flatten();

    let reward = calculate_reward(
        session.delta_coherence,
        session.goal_progress_delta,
        cognitive_state.valence - session.previous_valence,
        human_vote,
    );

    // 9.2 Reasoning Storage (AgentDB)
    // Store experience in ReasoningBank if reward > 0.7 (successful strategy)
    // API: db.store({ id, vector, metadata }) - Core API accepts pre-computed vectors
    // OPTIMIZATION: Pass semantic_embedding from cognitive_state to bypass AgentDB's
    // internal embedding generation. This saves ~50ms latency by reusing the Nomic
    // vector already computed in Stream A. Metadata includes pattern_type: "reasoning_pattern"
    // for ReasoningBank query compatibility.
    if reward > 0.7 {
        memory.reasoning.record_experience(
            &session.id,
            &cognitive_state.transcript,        // User context (text for readability)
            &cognitive_state.semantic_embedding,// User context (768-dim Nomic vector from Stream A)
            &north_star.description,            // Strategy pattern
            "success",
            reward,
            &response.reasoning_trace,
        ).await?;
    }

    // Add causal link between strategy and goal progress
    // API: causal_add_edge({ cause, effect, uplift, confidence })
    // The uplift becomes the Impact Factor for Prescience Engine MCTS
    memory.reasoning.add_causal_link(
        &best_strategy_id,
        &goal_status.goal_id,
        learning_signal.goal_delta,  // Uplift = goal progress change
        reward.abs(),                // Confidence = reward magnitude
    ).await?;

    // Store near-miss episodes for Oneiric Engine replay
    // API: reflexion_store({ task, episode, outcome })
    if reward >= -0.2 && reward <= 0.2 {
        memory.reasoning.store_near_miss(
            &cognitive_state.intent_id,
            &cognitive_state,
            &best_strategy_id,
            reward,
        ).await?;
    }

    // 9.3 Strategy Storage (RuVector)
    // Dual-write logic via RuVector GraphDatabase createNode API
    if reward > 0.7 {
        // Store Win AND Holographic Execution (Dual-Write)
        // Uses RuVector createNode API (NOT raw Cypher)
        memory.strategy.store_win(
            &cognitive_state,
            &response.reasoning_trace,
            reward,
        ).await?;
    } else if reward < -0.3 {
        // Store Anti-Pattern via RuVector createNode API
        memory.strategy.store_fail(
            &cognitive_state.semantic_embedding,
            &cognitive_state.intent_id,
            &response.reasoning_trace,
        ).await?;
    }

    Ok(TurnResponse {
        audio: audio_response,
        response_text: response.text,
        learning_signal,
    })
}

/// Session end handler - runs pruning logic
async fn on_session_end(
    session: &SessionState,
    memory: &MemorySystem,
) -> Result<SessionEndReport, ProcessingError> {
    let prune_report = memory.strategy.prune_strategies_post_session().await?;

    Ok(SessionEndReport {
        session_id: session.id.clone(),
        total_turns: session.turn_count,
        prune_report,
    })
}
```

Contents:

## 12. Reward Calculation

**REQ-LEARN-001: Reward Function with Human-in-the-Loop Override and Resonance Reward**

The reward function calculates the learning signal for RL training. When a human operator provides feedback via the Shadow Slot review system, the human vote supersedes the calculated reward.

The reward function mathematically values "Calming the user down" (Arousal Drop) as highly as "Goal Progress" through the Resonance Reward component.

```rust
use crate::hitl::HumanVote;

/// Calculate reward for RL learning, accounting for Human Feedback and Resonance
///
/// If human_override is present, it supersedes calculated logic.
/// This enables the Human-in-the-Loop (HITL) system to correct or reinforce AI behavior.
///
/// Components (when no human override):
/// - delta_coherence: Movement toward alignment (30%)
/// - goal_progress: Task completion progress (30%)
/// - sentiment_delta: User emotional improvement (20%)
/// - resonance_reward: Arousal reduction reward (20%)
///
/// **Resonance Reward:**
/// If the user's arousal dropped (negative delta_arousal), the system is rewarded
/// for successfully calming them down. If arousal increased, the system is penalized.
/// This ensures the system values de-escalation as much as goal completion.
///
/// Human Override Values:
/// - Solidify: +1.0 (full positive reinforcement)
/// - Punish: -1.0 (full negative reinforcement, creates anti-pattern)
/// - Correct: +0.5 (neutral-positive calibration adjustment)
pub fn calculate_reward(
    delta_coherence: f32,
    goal_progress_delta: f32,
    user_sentiment_delta: f32,
    user_arousal_delta: f32,  // Change in arousal (Current - Previous)
    human_vote: Option<HumanVote>,
) -> f32 {
    // 1. Check for Human Override (God Mode)
    if let Some(vote) = human_vote {
        return match vote {
            HumanVote::Solidify => 1.0,
            HumanVote::Punish => -1.0,
            HumanVote::Correct => 0.5,
        };
    }

    // 2. Calculate Resonance Reward (Did we calm them down?)
    // If arousal dropped (negative delta), this is a positive reward.
    // Clamp to 0.0-0.5 range.
    let resonance_reward = if user_arousal_delta < 0.0 {
        user_arousal_delta.abs().clamp(0.0, 0.5)
    } else {
        // Penalty for increasing arousal (unless excitement, but context assumes debt)
        -0.2
    };

    // 3. Weighted Calculation
    // Coherence (Alignment): 30%
    // Goal (Money/Plan): 30%
    // Sentiment (Feeling Good): 20%
    // Resonance (Calming Down): 20%
    let raw = (delta_coherence * 0.3)
        + (goal_progress_delta * 0.3)
        + (user_sentiment_delta * 0.2)
        + (resonance_reward * 0.2);

    raw.clamp(-1.0, 1.0)
}
```

**REQ-LEARN-002: Integration with Shadow Slot**

The reward calculation integrates with the post-session Shadow Slot review system:

| Scenario | Reward Source | Value |
|:---------|:--------------|:------|
| **Real-time (no human review)** | Calculated from deltas | -1.0 to +1.0 |
| **Post-session: Solidify vote** | Human override | +1.0 |
| **Post-session: Punish vote** | Human override | -1.0 |
| **Post-session: Correct vote** | Human override | +0.5 |

When a human vote is applied via `ReasoningBrain::apply_human_vote()`, the system re-evaluates the affected transition with the overridden reward value.

## 13. Quality Assurance & Constraints

### 13.1 Mandatory Constraints

**CRITICAL CONSTRAINTS** (System will not function correctly if violated):

| Constraint ID | Description | Enforcement | Failure Mode |
|:--------------|:------------|:------------|:-------------|
| QA-001 | System MUST NOT mathematically sum vectors of differing dimensions | Parallel stream architecture | Math errors, invalid embeddings |
| QA-002 | System MUST use Gamma = 0.1 during Safe Harbor (T < 60s) | Hardcoded constant | Cold-start hallucinations |
| QA-003 | Weighted Composite Confidence Score < 0.97 MUST create new user | Threshold check in IdentityBrain | Identity false positives |
| QA-011 | Audio MUST be normalized to -3dB AND VAD-processed before WavLM | AudioPreprocessor pipeline | Composite score unreachable |
| QA-015 | w_e MUST be calculated from Valence/Arousal scalars, NOT 1024-dim embedding | EmotionalStream | Physics equation crash |
| QA-006 | Strategy pruning MUST occur post-session only | on_session_end handler | Database locking, data loss |
| QA-012 | Safe Harbor MUST last 60 seconds with Gamma=0.1 | SAFE_HARBOR_DURATION_SECONDS constant | Cold-start profile hallucinations |

**Standard Constraints**:

| Constraint ID | Description | Enforcement |
|:--------------|:------------|:------------|
| QA-004 | Safety Stop MUST trigger when Valence < 0.3 AND Arousal > 0.7 | Stream C logic |
| QA-005 | Duplicate failures MUST be deduplicated (similarity > 0.99) | RuVector store_fail |
| QA-007 | All models MUST load from specified paths | Path validation at startup |
| QA-008 | Latency MUST be < 50ms (Enforced via Green Context isolation) | Timeout enforcement |
| QA-009 | Nomic embeddings MUST use correct prefixes | query_prefix for input, document_prefix for storage |
| QA-010 | Archetype Reference Sets file MUST exist at startup | Panic if missing |
| QA-012 | LLM input MUST be serialized text, NOT raw vectors | serialize_context_for_llm function |
| QA-013 | Strategy retrieval MUST avoid anti-patterns (similarity > 0.90) | find_best_strategy logic |
| QA-014 | RuVector queries MUST use Cypher syntax via db.query() | All graph operations |
| QA-016 | Hexa-modal profile snapshots MUST be stored in LanceDB for drift tracking | append_profile_snapshot method |
| QA-017 | Minimum 3 vectors required per stream before archetype calculation | SafeHarborBuffer.has_sufficient_data |
| QA-018 | Post-VAD audio duration MUST be >= 1.0s for identity verification | AudioPreprocessor |

### 13.2 Hardware Utilization (CUDA 13.1 Green Context Partitioning)

| Context | SM Allocation | Assignment |
|:--------|:--------------|:-----------|
| **Context A** | 10% | Audio I/O, WavLM, Trust Voice DSP (Tile IR), cuFFT |
| **Context B** | 30% | Nomic, Wav2Vec2, RoBERTa, BERT (Grouped GEMM) |
| **Context C** | 60% | Qwen 3 14B (FP8), Prescience MCTS |
| **CPU** | N/A | WebSocket, Database Management, State Logic |

```rust
/// Initialize CUDA 13.1 Green Contexts at startup
/// Partitions the RTX 5090 into isolated "hardware lanes" with guaranteed QoS
pub fn initialize_green_contexts(config: &HardwareOptimizationConfig) -> GreenContexts {
    // Create Green Context A (Reflex Loop - 10% SMs)
    // Audio/DSP partition - never waits for other contexts
    let context_a = CudaContext::create_green(
        config.context_a_sm_percentage,
        GreenContextPriority::RealTime,
    ).expect("Failed to create Context A");

    // Create Green Context B (Semantic Loop - 30% SMs)
    // Grouped GEMM for parallel embedding extraction
    let context_b = CudaContext::create_green(
        config.context_b_sm_percentage,
        GreenContextPriority::High,
    ).expect("Failed to create Context B");

    // Create Green Context C (Deep Thought - 60% SMs)
    // FP8 LLM inference and Prescience MCTS
    let context_c = CudaContext::create_green(
        config.context_c_sm_percentage,
        GreenContextPriority::Normal,
    ).expect("Failed to create Context C");

    GreenContexts {
        context_a_reflex: context_a,
        context_b_semantic: context_b,
        context_c_deep: context_c,
    }
}
```

## 14. Workflow Summary

### 14.0 Critical Implementation Rules

Before implementing any component, ensure these rules are followed:

| Rule | Requirement | Violation Consequence |
|:-----|:------------|:----------------------|
| **Audio Preprocessing** | MUST normalize + VAD + validate 1.0s minimum BEFORE WavLM | 0.97 identity threshold unreachable |
| **Safe Harbor** | MUST use hardcoded Gamma=0.1 for T<60s | Cold-start hallucinations, incorrect archetypes |
| **Vector Separation** | MUST NOT concatenate vectors of different dimensions | Invalid vector space operations |
| **Emotion Routing** | w_e MUST use scalars, embedding goes to LanceDB | Physics equation crash |
| **Pruning Timing** | MUST prune ONLY post-session | Database locking, premature data loss |
| **Failure Deduplication** | MUST check similarity > 0.99 before storing failures | Database bloat |

### 14.1 Complete Processing Flow

```
1. INPUT: Audio Waveform arrives

2. PARALLEL STREAM EXTRACTION (6 concurrent streams):

   STREAM A (Semantic - 768-dim):
   ├── Prepend "search_query: " prefix to transcript
   ├── Nomic generates 768-dim vector
   ├── Scan for VAK keywords (visual/auditory/kinesthetic)
   ├── Query RuVector for nearest IntentNode
   └── Output: IntentID, SemanticCoherence, VakKeywords

   STREAM B (Tone/Identity - 512-dim):
   ├── MANDATORY: Normalize audio to -3dB
   ├── MANDATORY: Apply VAD to extract speech-only segments
   ├── MANDATORY: Validate post-VAD duration >= 1.0s
   ├── WavLM extracts 512-dim X-Vector from preprocessed audio
   ├── GenderClassifier classifies X-Vector → Gender (Male/Female)
   ├── Compare against LanceDB (threshold 0.97)
   ├── Compare against 49 North Star Reference Sets (Gender-Specific)
   └── Output: UserID, Archetypes, Gender, IdentitySimilarity, X-Vector → LanceDB

   STREAM C (Emotional - 1024-dim):
   ├── Wav2Vec2 extracts 1024-dim pooled embedding
   ├── Extract scalars: Arousal, Dominance, Valence
   ├── Calculate w_e (Emotional Weight) FROM SCALARS (NOT vector)
   ├── Store 1024-dim vector in LanceDB (baseline tracking)
   ├── Check Safety Stop: Valence < 0.3 AND Arousal > 0.7
   └── Output: EmotionEmbedding → LanceDB, Scalars, w_e, SafetyStop

   STREAM D (Style - scalar):
   ├── RoBERTa Formality classifier processes transcript
   └── Output: formality_score (0.0 = casual, 1.0 = formal)

   STREAM E (Action - 42-dim):
   ├── BERT Dialog Act classifier processes transcript
   ├── Softmax to get 42-class probabilities
   ├── Detect if directive (Command/Request/Instruct)
   └── Output: dialog_act_probabilities, top_act, is_directive

   STREAM F (Chronemic - 4-dim):
   ├── Calculate WPM from word timestamps
   ├── Calculate response latency
   ├── Calculate jitter (pace variation)
   ├── Calculate overlap ratio
   └── Output: [wpm, latency_ms, jitter, overlap_ratio]

3. BUILD COGNITIVE STATE:
   - Combine all stream outputs into CognitiveState struct
   - NO vector addition - parallel outputs only
   - Derive VAK modality from Stream A keywords + Stream F pace

4. SAFETY CHECK:
   - IF SafetyStop == true: Trigger rapport rebuild, return early

5. CULTURAL LENS NORMALIZATION:
   - Load cultural norms for user's locale from config
   - Calculate normalized_pace (deviation from baseline)
   - Calculate silence_entropy (latency vs. tolerance)
   - Calculate aggression_score (directive + directness_bias)
   - Store in CognitiveState for LLM context

6. PROFILING LOGIC:
   - IF T < 60s: Accumulate all 6 streams + Gender votes, use Gamma = 0.1
   - IF T >= 60s AND not locked:
     - **Determine Consensus Gender** via Majority Vote of gender_votes buffer
     - **Calculate User Position Vectors** (Average of buffers for each of the 5 embedding spaces)
     - NOTE: The User does NOT have a single centroid - each space is independent
     - Calculate Cumulative Distance between User's 5 vectors and the 49 **Gender-Specific North Star Reference Sets**
     - Reference vector selection: Use tone_male/emotion_male OR tone_female/emotion_female based on Consensus Gender
     - Distance = (Sem*0.20) + (Tone*0.20) + (Style*0.15) + (Action*0.15) + (Chron*0.15) + (Emo*0.15)
     - Lock Primary + Secondary Archetype
     - Behavior = (Primary_Complement * 0.7) + (Secondary_Complement * 0.3)
   - IF locked: Use archetype-matched physics

7. PROSODIC ANTICIPATION GRAPH (PAG):
   - Input: Tonal Drift (Stream B), IBI (Stream B/Bio), Lexical Entropy (Stream A), Rate Variance (Stream F)
   - Process: GNN Message Passing on 500ms temporal nodes
   - Output: PagPrediction (State at t+5s)
   - Logic:
     - IF AngerRising: Set override strategy to "Pre-emptive Empathy", lower Gamma
     - IF Disengaging: Set override strategy to "Attention Hook"
     - IF PeakReceptive: Flag for Resonance Trigger

8. PHYSICS CALCULATION:
   - L = f((ΔS × ΔC) × w_e)
   - w_e from Valence/Arousal scalars
   - Apply gamma from archetype weights

9. COGNITIVE RESONANCE MAPPING (CRM) & TEMPORAL ARCHETYPE DRIFT (TAD):
   - Retrieve Previous Turn North Star Distances from IdentityBrain (get_previous_distances)
   - Calculate Current Turn North Star Distances (from profiling)
   - CALCULATE TAD:
     - Drift_Velocity = Σ(w_i × (Prev_Dist - Curr_Dist)) for Trust/Passion archetypes
     - Formula: (Dist_Prev_Trust - Dist_Curr_Trust) * weight_trust + (Dist_Prev_Passion - Dist_Curr_Passion) * weight_passion
   - Determine is_receptivity_window: Velocity > velocity_threshold (default 0.05)
   - Get current milestone embedding for S(t) calculation
   - Calculate P(t): Prosodic Alignment via F0 cross-correlation (Stream B + previous Operator F0)
   - Calculate S(t): Semantic Coherence via cosine similarity (Stream A + Milestone embedding)
   - Calculate C(t): Chrono-Rhythmic Sync via jitter inverse (Stream F)
   - Calculate σ(t): Noise from biometric dissonance (Stream B extension)
   - Compute R(t) = (P × S × C) / σ
   - Update CognitiveState with CRM telemetry (resonance_score, p_t, s_t, c_t, sigma_t)
   - Update CognitiveState with TAD telemetry (drift_velocity, is_receptivity_window)
   - Update CognitiveState with PAG telemetry (pag_prediction from Step 7)
   - Determine force_close_mode:
       (R(t) > 0.82 AND all component thresholds exceeded)
       OR
       (is_receptivity_window == true) ← TAD Override
       OR
       (pag_prediction.predicted_state == PeakReceptive) ← PAG Override

10. STRATEGY LOOKUP & PRESCIENCE:
   - Query semantic embedding for candidate North Stars
   - PRESCIENCE ENGINE: Run 10,000+ MCTS simulations on GPU (Green Context C)
   - **IF force_close_mode == true**: Filter strategies to "CLOSING" type only
   - Calculate Expected Value (EV) for top candidates using AgentDB Causal Links
   - Check against nearest anti-pattern (similarity > 0.90 = reject)
   - Select strategy with highest EV that avoids Anti-Patterns

11. CONTEXT SERIALIZATION:
   - Retrieve Holographic Execution (Ghost Replay) from LanceDB for selected strategy
   - Convert CognitiveState to text System Prompt
   - Include [CULTURAL LENS] section with locale and dignity protocol
   - Include [PAG PREDICTION] section with predicted emotional state
   - Inject [PERFORMANCE CUES] (Tone, Pace, Emotion targets from Hologram)
   - NO raw vectors sent to LLM

12. GENERATION (Qwen 3 14B FP8):
    - Input: Serialized text context + User transcript
    - Mode: InferenceMode::Instruct (Non-Thinking for <50ms latency)
    - Output: Response text + reasoning trace

13. TTS & TRUST VOICE DSP (CUDA Tile IR on Context A):
    - Select style based on archetype weights
    - **PAG Style Override**: IF AngerRising, force "empathetic_calm" TTS style
    - Synthesize audio response
    - DETERMINE LFM TRIGGER:
      - Enable if Strategy Type is "CLOSING", "OFFER", or "MICRO_YES"
      - **DISABLE if PAG predicts AngerRising** (LFM contraindicated for angry users)
    - APPLY TRUST VOICE DSP via GPU Tile Kernel:
      - HPF @ 85Hz (Biquad Tile)
      - Boost @ 140Hz +3dB (Biquad Tile)
      - Cut @ 3kHz -3dB (Biquad Tile)
      - Compress 3:1 (Tile)
      - Saturate 5% (Tile)
      - [CONDITIONAL] Inject LFM (17-21Hz Glide @ -18dB) if Triggered
    - Stream output directly from GPU memory (zero PCIe latency)

14. STORAGE & LEARNING:
    - LanceDB: Append ProfileSnapshot for drift tracking
    - AgentDB: Record transition for Q-learning
    - **PAG Learning**: Store PAGNode with current window features in RuVector
    - RuVector & LanceDB (Dual-Write):
      - IF reward > 0.7: Store Logic in RuVector AND Hologram in LanceDB
      - IF reward < -0.3: Store as FAIL (deduplicated at 0.99)
    - NO DELETION during active session

15. POST-SESSION (on_session_end):
    - Run strategy pruning: Keep Top 1 per IntentID
    - Deduplicate failures (similarity > 0.99)
    - **Train PAG GNN**: Update edge weights using session trajectory outcomes
    - This is the ONLY time deletion occurs
```

### 14.2 Storage Clarification

| Storage | Contents | Model Source |
|:--------|:---------|:-------------|
| **RuVector** | North Stars (strategy logic), Intent Nodes, Anti-Patterns | Nomic (768-dim) |
| **LanceDB** | Voice Fingerprints, Profile Snapshots, Execution Holograms (Ghost Replay) | WavLM (512-dim), All 6 streams |
| **AgentDB** | Causal impact factors, Session state, Q-learning transitions | N/A |

## 15. Error Handling

**REQ-ERROR-001: Error Types**

The system defines a comprehensive error type hierarchy to handle all failure modes. Each error type maps to a specific constraint violation.

| Error Type | Constraint Violated | Recovery Action |
|:-----------|:--------------------|:----------------|
| `IdentityBelowThreshold` | REQ-CONST-003 (0.97 composite threshold) | Treat as NewUser, no Fast-Track exit |
| `SafeHarborViolation` | REQ-PROFILE-001 (T < 60s) | Reject archetype lock, continue accumulating |
| `InsufficientData` | REQ-PROFILE-001b (minimum vectors) | Wait for more data |
| `NoSpeechDetected` | REQ-AUDIO-001 (VAD) | Skip turn for identity, use text only |
| `AudioDurationBelowMinimum` | REQ-AUDIO-002 (1.0s minimum) | Skip identity verification for this turn |
| `LatencyViolation` | REQ-CONST-001 (200ms) | Log warning, continue with partial results |
| `PruningDuringSession` | REQ-DATA-003 (post-session only) | Reject operation, mark for review instead |

```rust
#[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]
pub enum CognitiveError {
    // === Model & System Errors ===
    #[error("Model not found at path: {0}")]
    ModelNotFound(String),

    #[error("Archetype reference sets file not found at: {0}")]
    ReferenceSetsNotFound(String),

    // === Identity Verification Errors (REQ-CONST-003 - Hexa-Modal Fusion) ===
    #[error("Identity verification failed: Weighted Composite Confidence Score {0} below threshold 0.97")]
    IdentityBelowThreshold(f32),

    // === Safe Harbor Errors (REQ-PROFILE-001) ===
    #[error("Safe Harbor violation: attempted archetype lock at T={0}s (minimum 60s)")]
    SafeHarborViolation(u64),

    #[error("Insufficient data for archetype calculation: {0} vectors (minimum 3 per stream)")]
    InsufficientData(usize),

    // === Safety Errors ===
    #[error("Safety stop triggered: Valence={valence}, Arousal={arousal}")]
    SafetyStopTriggered { valence: f32, arousal: f32 },

    // === Dimension & Type Errors ===
    #[error("Dimension mismatch: expected {expected}, got {actual}")]
    DimensionMismatch { expected: usize, actual: usize },

    #[error("Vector type mismatch: cannot use {0}-dim vector in physics equation (requires scalar)")]
    VectorInPhysicsEquation(usize),

    // === Latency Errors (REQ-CONST-001) ===
    #[error("Latency exceeded 200ms: {0}ms")]
    LatencyViolation(u64),

    // === Audio Preprocessing Errors (REQ-AUDIO-001, REQ-AUDIO-002) ===
    #[error("No speech detected in audio buffer after VAD")]
    NoSpeechDetected,

    #[error("Silent audio - cannot normalize to -3dB")]
    SilentAudio,

    #[error("Audio duration below minimum: {actual}s (required: {required}s)")]
    AudioDurationBelowMinimum { actual: f32, required: f32 },

    #[error("Audio preprocessing failed: {0}")]
    AudioPreprocessingFailed(String),

    // === Strategy Pruning Errors (REQ-DATA-003) ===
    #[error("Pruning attempted during active session - pruning is post-session only")]
    PruningDuringSession,

    #[error("Strategy deduplication failed: could not check similarity")]
    DeduplicationFailed,

    // === Database Errors ===
    #[error("RuVector error: {0}")]
    RuVector(#[from] RuVectorError),

    #[error("LanceDB error: {0}")]
    LanceDb(#[from] LanceDbError),

    #[error("AgentDB error: {0}")]
    AgentDb(#[from] AgentDbError),
}

impl CognitiveError {
    /// Check if error is recoverable (can continue processing)
    pub fn is_recoverable(&self) -> bool {
        matches!(
            self,
            CognitiveError::NoSpeechDetected
                | CognitiveError::AudioDurationBelowMinimum { .. }
                | CognitiveError::LatencyViolation(_)
                | CognitiveError::IdentityBelowThreshold(_)
        )
    }

    /// Check if error requires safety stop
    pub fn requires_safety_stop(&self) -> bool {
        matches!(self, CognitiveError::SafetyStopTriggered { .. })
    }
}
```

## 16. Testing Requirements

**REQ-TEST-001: Test Coverage**

| Test Category | Requirement | Validation |
|:--------------|:------------|:-----------|
| Dimension Enforcement | Semantic=768, Emotion=1024, Identity=512, Action=42, Chronemic=4 | Compile-time checks |
| Gender Bifurcation | Male Audio MUST match Male North Star Vectors closer than Female Vectors | Unit test |
| Gender Persistence | Profile Snapshot MUST retain gender tag across sessions | Integration test |
| Gender Voting | Mixed buffer (60% Male, 40% Female frames) MUST result in Male Consensus | Unit test |
| Reference Set Integrity | NorthStarReferenceSet file MUST contain non-zero vectors for both tone_male and tone_female | Unit test |
| Identity Threshold | Composite similarity=0.96 MUST create new user (no Fast-Track) | Unit test |
| Identity Threshold | Composite similarity=0.97 MUST verify existing user (triggers Fast-Track) | Unit test |
| Fast Track ID | Identity Verification > 0.97 MUST exit Safe Harbor at T < 60s | Integration test |
| Fast Track ID | Verified identity MUST hydrate buffer from historical_profile | Integration test |
| Multimodal Fusion | Weak Voice (0.90) + Strong Behavior (0.99) MUST Verify if composite > 0.97 | Unit test |
| Multimodal Fusion | All 6 stream weights MUST sum to 1.0 | Unit test |
| Multimodal Fusion | Voice weight MUST be 0.60 (primary biometric) | Unit test |
| Safe Harbor | T=30s MUST use Gamma=0.1 | Integration test |
| Archetype Lock | T=65s MUST calculate and lock archetype | Integration test |
| Safety Stop | Valence=0.2, Arousal=0.8 MUST trigger | Unit test |
| Strategy Pruning Timing | Pruning MUST only occur post-session | Integration test |
| Strategy Pruning | 3 strategies for same intent → keep 1 | Unit test |
| Failure Dedup | Two failures with sim=0.995 → increment counter | Unit test |
| Behavioral Blend | Primary * 0.7 + Secondary * 0.3 | Unit test |
| Model Paths | All 5 model paths must exist | Startup validation |
| Latency | 95th percentile < 200ms | Load test |
| Nomic Prefix | Query uses "search_query: " prefix | Unit test |
| Nomic Prefix | Document uses "search_document: " prefix | Unit test |
| Reference Sets Load | Missing reference sets file panics at startup | Unit test |
| Audio Normalization | Audio normalized to -3dB before WavLM | Unit test |
| VAD Applied | Silence removed before WavLM extraction | Unit test |
| Minimum Duration | Post-VAD audio < 1.0s discarded for identity | Unit test |
| LLM Serialization | Context serialized to text, not vectors | Unit test |
| Priming Injection | System MUST inject priming words into System Prompt when deficit exists | Unit test |
| Priming Density | Response validation MUST trigger regeneration if density < 0.03 during first 120s | Unit test |
| Priming Word Tracking | Session MUST track cumulative priming word usage across turns | Unit test |
| Priming Configuration | [priming] TOML section MUST load with words, target_density, validation_threshold | Unit test |
| Anti-Pattern Avoidance | Strategy with >0.90 similarity to failure rejected | Unit test |
| w_e from Scalars | w_e calculated from Valence/Arousal, not 1024-dim | Unit test |
| Emotion Storage | 1024-dim stored in LanceDB, scalars used for physics | Unit test |
| Cultural Silence Normalization | 3s silence → high entropy for en-US, low for ja-JP | Unit test |
| Style Formality Range | RoBERTa output is 0.0-1.0 | Unit test |
| Directive Detection | Request/Instruct/Suggest → is_directive = true | Unit test |
| Cultural Aggression | Directive + low directness_bias → high aggression | Unit test |
| Dignity Protocol | ja-JP locale → "Preserve Face" instruction | Unit test |
| Trust Voice EQ | Output spectrum MUST show boost at ~140Hz and cut at ~3kHz | Unit test (FFT analysis) |
| Trust Voice Dynamics | Output RMS MUST show reduced dynamic range (compression active) | Unit test |
| Trust Voice Saturation | Output THD (Total Harmonic Distortion) MUST increase slightly (>0%) | Unit test |
| Hybrid Distance Normalization | Identical reference sets → distance ~0.0, max distance ≤ 1.0 | Unit test |
| Chronemic Z-Score | Raw chronemics normalized to [-2.0, 2.0] range | Unit test |
| Cosine Distance Bounds | Cosine distance (1 - sim) bounded [0.0, 1.0] | Unit test |
| VPCE Phase Extraction | Hilbert transform MUST extract valid phase angle from F0 | Unit test (cuFFT) |
| VPCE Latency | Phase adjustment calculation MUST complete < 10ms | Benchmark |
| VPCE Limits | Micro-timing shift MUST NOT exceed ±50ms | Unit test |
| VPCE Degradation | If Φ < 0.6, system MUST output standard TTS timing | Integration test |

```rust
#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn test_dimensions_are_correct() {
        assert_eq!(dimensions::SEMANTIC_DIM, 768);
        assert_eq!(dimensions::EMOTION_DIM, 1024);
        assert_eq!(dimensions::IDENTITY_DIM, 512);
        assert_eq!(dimensions::STYLE_DIM, 1);
        assert_eq!(dimensions::ACTION_DIM, 42);
        assert_eq!(dimensions::CHRONEMIC_DIM, 4);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_composite_identity_threshold_rejection() {
        let threshold = COMPOSITE_IDENTITY_THRESHOLD;
        assert_eq!(threshold, 0.97);

        // 0.96 composite MUST NOT verify (no Fast-Track)
        let similarity = 0.96;
        assert!(similarity < threshold);

        // 0.97 composite MUST verify (triggers Fast-Track)
        let similarity = 0.97;
        assert!(similarity >= threshold);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_hexa_modal_weights_sum_to_one() {
        // Weights from config/cognitive_physics.toml [identity] section
        let weight_voice = 0.60;
        let weight_semantic = 0.10;
        let weight_emotion = 0.10;
        let weight_style = 0.10;
        let weight_action = 0.05;
        let weight_chronemic = 0.05;

        let sum = weight_voice + weight_semantic + weight_emotion
            + weight_style + weight_action + weight_chronemic;

        assert!((sum - 1.0).abs() < 0.001, "Weights must sum to 1.0, got {}", sum);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_voice_is_primary_biometric() {
        // Voice weight MUST be 0.60 (highest weight = primary biometric)
        let weight_voice = 0.60;
        let weight_semantic = 0.10;
        let weight_emotion = 0.10;
        let weight_style = 0.10;
        let weight_action = 0.05;
        let weight_chronemic = 0.05;

        assert!(weight_voice > weight_semantic);
        assert!(weight_voice > weight_emotion);
        assert!(weight_voice > weight_style);
        assert!(weight_voice > weight_action);
        assert!(weight_voice > weight_chronemic);
        assert_eq!(weight_voice, 0.60);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_weak_voice_strong_behavior_can_verify() {
        // Scenario: Voice similarity is weak (0.90) but all behavioral signals are very strong (0.99)
        // This tests that Hexa-Modal Fusion can still verify if composite > 0.97
        let voice_sim = 0.90;      // Weak voice match
        let sem_sim = 0.99;        // Strong semantic match
        let emo_sim = 0.99;        // Strong emotion match
        let style_sim = 0.99;      // Strong style match
        let action_sim = 0.99;     // Strong action match
        let chron_sim = 0.99;      // Strong chronemic match

        // Weighted composite calculation
        let composite = (voice_sim * 0.60)
            + (sem_sim * 0.10)
            + (emo_sim * 0.10)
            + (style_sim * 0.10)
            + (action_sim * 0.05)
            + (chron_sim * 0.05);

        // Weighted Composite Confidence Score = 0.54 + 0.099 + 0.099 + 0.099 + 0.0495 + 0.0495 = 0.936
        // This is BELOW 0.97 Composite threshold, so verification should FAIL
        assert!(composite < COMPOSITE_IDENTITY_THRESHOLD,
            "Weak voice (0.90) should not be saved by behavior alone, composite = {}", composite);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_strong_voice_enables_verification() {
        // Scenario: Voice similarity is strong enough to carry verification
        let voice_sim = 0.99;      // Strong voice match
        let sem_sim = 0.90;        // Moderate semantic match
        let emo_sim = 0.90;        // Moderate emotion match
        let style_sim = 0.90;      // Moderate style match
        let action_sim = 0.90;     // Moderate action match
        let chron_sim = 0.90;      // Moderate chronemic match

        // Weighted composite calculation
        let composite = (voice_sim * 0.60)
            + (sem_sim * 0.10)
            + (emo_sim * 0.10)
            + (style_sim * 0.10)
            + (action_sim * 0.05)
            + (chron_sim * 0.05);

        // Weighted Composite Confidence Score = 0.594 + 0.09 + 0.09 + 0.09 + 0.045 + 0.045 = 0.954
        // This is still below 0.97 Composite threshold
        assert!(composite < COMPOSITE_IDENTITY_THRESHOLD,
            "Need very strong signals across modalities, composite = {}", composite);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_perfect_match_verifies() {
        // Scenario: All signals are perfect matches
        let voice_sim = 1.0;
        let sem_sim = 1.0;
        let emo_sim = 1.0;
        let style_sim = 1.0;
        let action_sim = 1.0;
        let chron_sim = 1.0;

        let composite = (voice_sim * 0.60)
            + (sem_sim * 0.10)
            + (emo_sim * 0.10)
            + (style_sim * 0.10)
            + (action_sim * 0.05)
            + (chron_sim * 0.05);

        assert_eq!(composite, 1.0);
        assert!(composite > COMPOSITE_IDENTITY_THRESHOLD);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_fast_track_buffer_hydration() {
        // Test that hydration properly populates the buffer
        let mut buffer = SafeHarborBuffer::new();
        let historical = ProfileSnapshot::default();

        // Before hydration - buffer is empty
        assert!(!buffer.has_sufficient_data());

        // Hydrate from historical profile
        buffer.hydrate_from_history(&historical);

        // After hydration - buffer has sufficient data
        assert!(buffer.has_sufficient_data());
        assert_eq!(buffer.semantic_vectors.len(), 3);
        assert_eq!(buffer.tone_vectors.len(), 3);
        assert_eq!(buffer.emotion_vectors.len(), 3);
        assert_eq!(buffer.style_scalars.len(), 3);
        assert_eq!(buffer.action_logits.len(), 3);
        assert_eq!(buffer.chronemic_vectors.len(), 3);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_fast_track_bypasses_time_check() {
        // Test that Fast-Track exit works before T=60s
        let mut session = SessionState::new();
        session.start_time = Instant::now(); // Just started

        // Simulate identity verification at T=5s
        let identity_verified = true;
        let elapsed = 5; // seconds

        // Without Fast-Track: would need to wait until T=60s
        assert!(elapsed < SAFE_HARBOR_DURATION_SECONDS);

        // With Fast-Track: can lock immediately if identity_verified
        let can_lock = identity_verified || elapsed >= SAFE_HARBOR_DURATION_SECONDS;
        assert!(can_lock, "Fast-Track should allow immediate lock");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_safety_stop_trigger() {
        let valence = 0.2;  // < 0.3
        let arousal = 0.8;  // > 0.7

        let should_trigger = valence < EmotionalStream::NEGATIVE_VALENCE_THRESHOLD
            && arousal > EmotionalStream::HIGH_AROUSAL_THRESHOLD;

        assert!(should_trigger);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_behavioral_blend() {
        let primary = ArchetypeBehavior {
            assertiveness: 0.8,
            warmth: 0.4,
            pace: 0.9,
            formality: 0.7,
        };
        let secondary = ArchetypeBehavior {
            assertiveness: 0.3,
            warmth: 0.8,
            pace: 0.5,
            formality: 0.3,
        };

        let blend = calculate_behavioral_blend(&primary, &secondary);

        // 0.8 * 0.7 + 0.3 * 0.3 = 0.56 + 0.09 = 0.65
        assert!((blend.assertiveness - 0.65).abs() < 0.001);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_vad_filtering_rejects_short_audio() {
        let preprocessor = AudioPreprocessor::new();

        // Create audio buffer with only 0.5s of speech (below 1.0s threshold)
        let short_audio = AudioBuffer {
            samples: vec![0.5; 8000], // 0.5s at 16kHz
            sample_rate: 16000,
        };

        let result = preprocessor.preprocess_for_identity(&short_audio);

        // Should fail with InsufficientDuration
        assert!(matches!(result, Err(AudioError::InsufficientDuration { .. })));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_w_e_calculated_from_scalars_not_vector() {
        let stream = EmotionalStream::new();

        let valence = 0.3;
        let arousal = 0.8;

        let w_e = stream.calculate_emotional_weight(valence, arousal);

        // For low valence + high arousal, w_e should be low
        assert!(w_e < 0.5);

        // Positive valence should give full weight
        let w_e_positive = stream.calculate_emotional_weight(0.7, 0.5);
        assert_eq!(w_e_positive, 1.0);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_cultural_silence_normalization_en_us() {
        let norms = CulturalBaseline {
            baseline_pace_wpm: 150.0,
            silence_tolerance_sec: 1.5,
            directness_bias: 0.8,
            formality_floor: 0.3,
        };

        // 3 second silence in en-US (tolerance = 1.5s)
        let latency_sec = 3.0;
        let silence_entropy = if latency_sec > norms.silence_tolerance_sec {
            ((latency_sec - norms.silence_tolerance_sec) * 0.5).clamp(0.0, 1.0)
        } else {
            0.0
        };

        // 3.0 - 1.5 = 1.5 * 0.5 = 0.75 (high entropy)
        assert!((silence_entropy - 0.75).abs() < 0.01);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_cultural_silence_normalization_ja_jp() {
        let norms = CulturalBaseline {
            baseline_pace_wpm: 110.0,
            silence_tolerance_sec: 4.0,
            directness_bias: 0.2,
            formality_floor: 0.8,
        };

        // 3 second silence in ja-JP (tolerance = 4.0s)
        let latency_sec = 3.0;
        let silence_entropy = if latency_sec > norms.silence_tolerance_sec {
            ((latency_sec - norms.silence_tolerance_sec) * 0.5).clamp(0.0, 1.0)
        } else {
            0.0
        };

        // 3.0 < 4.0, so entropy = 0.0 (silence is normal in ja-JP)
        assert_eq!(silence_entropy, 0.0);
    }

    #[test]

    }

    #[test]
    fn test_directive_detection() {
        let directive_acts = [
            DialogActType::Request,
            DialogActType::Instruct,
            DialogActType::Suggest,
        ];

        for act in directive_acts {
            assert!(ActionStream::DIRECTIVE_ACTS.contains(&act));
        }

        // Non-directive acts should not be in the list
        assert!(!ActionStream::DIRECTIVE_ACTS.contains(&DialogActType::Question));
        assert!(!ActionStream::DIRECTIVE_ACTS.contains(&DialogActType::Inform));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_cultural_aggression_indirect_culture() {
        let norms = CulturalBaseline {
            baseline_pace_wpm: 110.0,
            silence_tolerance_sec: 4.0,
            directness_bias: 0.2, // Indirect culture
            formality_floor: 0.8,
        };

        let is_directive = true;

        let aggression_score = if is_directive && norms.directness_bias < 0.3 {
            0.9 // High aggression - commands in indirect culture
        } else if is_directive && norms.directness_bias >= 0.7 {
            0.1 // Normal - commands in direct culture
        } else {
            0.2
        };

        // Directive in indirect culture = high aggression
        assert_eq!(aggression_score, 0.9);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_cultural_aggression_direct_culture() {
        let norms = CulturalBaseline {
            baseline_pace_wpm: 150.0,
            silence_tolerance_sec: 1.5,
            directness_bias: 0.8, // Direct culture
            formality_floor: 0.3,
        };

        let is_directive = true;

        let aggression_score = if is_directive && norms.directness_bias < 0.3 {
            0.9
        } else if is_directive && norms.directness_bias >= 0.7 {
            0.1 // Normal - commands in direct culture
        } else {
            0.2
        };

        // Directive in direct culture = low aggression (normal)
        assert_eq!(aggression_score, 0.1);
    }
```
