    #[test]
    fn test_weighted_distance_formula() {
        // Verify weights sum to 1.0
        let weights = [0.20, 0.20, 0.15, 0.15, 0.15, 0.15];
        let sum: f32 = weights.iter().sum();
        assert!((sum - 1.0).abs() < 0.001);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_hybrid_distance_normalization() {
        let profiler = ProfilingEngine::default();

        // Mock User Position (Identical to North Star Reference Set)
        let user_perfect = UserPosition {
            semantic: [0.1; 768],
            tone: [0.1; 512],
            emotion: [0.1; 1024],
            style: 0.5,
            action: [0.1; 42],
            chronemic: [0.0; 4], // Normalized to mean (z-score = 0)
        };

        let north_star = NorthStarReferenceSet {
            archetype_id: ArchetypeId(1),
            semantic: [0.1; 768],
            tone: [0.1; 512],
            emotion: [0.1; 1024],
            style: 0.5,
            action: [0.1; 42],
            chronemic: [0.0; 4],
        };

        // Distance should be 0.0 for identical reference sets
        let dist = profiler.calculate_weighted_distance(&user_perfect, &north_star);
        assert!(dist < 0.0001, "Identical reference sets should have ~0 distance, got {}", dist);

        // Mock User Position (Maximum Distance)
        // Flip vectors to be orthogonal/opposite where possible
        let user_worst = UserPosition {
            semantic: [-0.1; 768],  // Opposite direction
            tone: [-0.1; 512],      // Opposite direction
            emotion: [-0.1; 1024],  // Opposite direction
            style: 1.0,             // North star is 0.5, max dist is 0.5
            action: [-0.1; 42],     // Opposite direction
            chronemic: [2.0; 4],    // 2 sigma away (maximum clamped value)
        };

        let dist_worst = profiler.calculate_weighted_distance(&user_worst, &north_star);

        // Ensure result is strictly bounded 0.0 to 1.0
        // Our logic clamps sub-distances to 1.0, so max weighted sum is 1.0
        assert!(dist_worst <= 1.0, "Distance should be bounded to 1.0, got {}", dist_worst);
        assert!(dist_worst > 0.5, "Max-distance position should have high distance, got {}", dist_worst);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_chronemic_zscore_normalization() {
        // Test that chronemic vectors are properly Z-score normalized
        let mut state = create_mock_cognitive_state();
        state.locale = "en-US".to_string();

        // Set raw chronemic values with vastly different scales
        state.chronemics = [
            150.0,    // WPM (typical: 150)
            1500.0,   // Latency ms (typical: 1500)
            100.0,    // Jitter ms (typical: 100)
            0.1,      // Overlap ratio (typical: 0.1)
        ];

        let engine = PhysicsEngine::default();
        engine.apply_cultural_lens(&mut state);

        // After normalization, all values should be in similar range (-2.0 to 2.0)
        for i in 0..4 {
            assert!(state.chronemics[i] >= -2.0 && state.chronemics[i] <= 2.0,
                "Normalized chronemic[{}] should be in [-2, 2], got {}",
                i, state.chronemics[i]);
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_cosine_distance_bounds() {
        // Verify cosine distance (1 - similarity) is bounded [0.0, 1.0] for normalized vectors
        let vec_a: [f32; 768] = [0.1; 768];
        let vec_b: [f32; 768] = [-0.1; 768]; // Opposite direction

        let similarity = cosine_similarity_768(&vec_a, &vec_b);
        let distance = (1.0 - similarity).clamp(0.0, 1.0);

        assert!(distance >= 0.0 && distance <= 1.0,
            "Cosine distance should be bounded [0, 1], got {}", distance);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_priming_injection_generates_when_deficit_exists() {
        let config = PrimingConfig {
            enabled: true,
            words: vec!["certainly".into(), "happy".into(), "easy".into()],
            target_density_per_minute: 5.0,
            validation_threshold: 0.03,
        };
        let controller = PrimingController::new(&config);

        // At T=60s with 0 words used, expect 5 word deficit
        let injection = controller.generate_prompt_injection(60, ConversationPhase::Rapport);

        // Injection should contain guidance
        assert!(!injection.is_empty());
        assert!(injection.contains("certainly"));
        assert!(injection.contains("happy"));
        assert!(injection.contains("LANGUAGE GUIDANCE"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_priming_injection_empty_when_no_deficit() {
        let config = PrimingConfig {
            enabled: true,
            words: vec!["certainly".into()],
            target_density_per_minute: 5.0,
            validation_threshold: 0.03,
        };
        let mut controller = PrimingController::new(&config);

        // Simulate having met the target
        controller.words_used_this_session = 10; // Exceeded 5/minute at T=60s

        let injection = controller.generate_prompt_injection(60, ConversationPhase::Action);

        // Injection should be empty when no deficit and not in Rapport phase
        assert!(injection.is_empty());
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_priming_validation_triggers_regeneration() {
        let config = PrimingConfig {
            enabled: true,
            words: vec!["certainly".into(), "happy".into()],
            target_density_per_minute: 5.0,
            validation_threshold: 0.03,
        };
        let controller = PrimingController::new(&config);

        // Response with 0 priming words and 100 total words = 0% density
        let low_density_response = "This is a response without any of the target words at all. ".repeat(10);

        let hint = controller.validate_response(&low_density_response, 30); // T=30s (within 120s)

        // Should return regeneration hint
        assert!(hint.is_some());
        assert!(hint.unwrap().contains("affirmative"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_priming_validation_passes_with_sufficient_density() {
        let config = PrimingConfig {
            enabled: true,
            words: vec!["certainly".into(), "happy".into()],
            target_density_per_minute: 5.0,
            validation_threshold: 0.03,
        };
        let controller = PrimingController::new(&config);

        // Response with priming words (3 occurrences in ~30 words = 10% density)
        let good_response = "I'm certainly happy to help you. This is certainly easy.";

        let hint = controller.validate_response(good_response, 30);

        // Should pass validation (no regeneration needed)
        assert!(hint.is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_priming_word_tracking_across_turns() {
        let config = PrimingConfig {
            enabled: true,
            words: vec!["certainly".into(), "happy".into()],
            target_density_per_minute: 5.0,
            validation_threshold: 0.03,
        };
        let mut controller = PrimingController::new(&config);

        assert_eq!(controller.words_used_this_session, 0);

        // Simulate first response
        controller.count_and_update("I'm certainly happy to assist.");
        assert_eq!(controller.words_used_this_session, 2); // "certainly" + "happy"

        // Simulate second response
        controller.count_and_update("This is certainly straightforward.");
        assert_eq!(controller.words_used_this_session, 3); // +1 "certainly"
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_priming_config_loads_from_toml() {
        // Validate the expected TOML structure
        let toml_content = r#"
            [priming]
            enabled = true
            words = ["certainly", "absolutely", "happy"]
            target_density_per_minute = 5.0
            validation_threshold = 0.03
        "#;

        let config: toml::Value = toml::from_str(toml_content).unwrap();
        let priming = config.get("priming").unwrap();

        assert_eq!(priming.get("enabled").unwrap().as_bool().unwrap(), true);
        assert_eq!(priming.get("target_density_per_minute").unwrap().as_float().unwrap(), 5.0);
        assert_eq!(priming.get("validation_threshold").unwrap().as_float().unwrap(), 0.03);

        let words = priming.get("words").unwrap().as_array().unwrap();
        assert_eq!(words.len(), 3);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_priming_disabled_skips_injection() {
        let config = PrimingConfig {
            enabled: false, // Disabled
            words: vec!["certainly".into()],
            target_density_per_minute: 5.0,
            validation_threshold: 0.03,
        };
        let controller = PrimingController::new(&config);

        // Should return empty even with deficit
        let injection = controller.generate_prompt_injection(60, ConversationPhase::Rapport);
        assert!(injection.is_empty());

        // Validation should also pass (no enforcement)
        let hint = controller.validate_response("no priming words here", 30);
        assert!(hint.is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_priming_validation_skipped_after_120s() {
        let config = PrimingConfig {
            enabled: true,
            words: vec!["certainly".into()],
            target_density_per_minute: 5.0,
            validation_threshold: 0.03,
        };
        let controller = PrimingController::new(&config);

        // Response with 0 priming words
        let low_density_response = "This response has no target words at all.";

        // At T=150s (beyond 120s threshold), validation should pass
        let hint = controller.validate_response(low_density_response, 150);
        assert!(hint.is_none(), "Validation should be skipped after 120s");
    }

    // GENDER BIFURCATION TESTS
    // =========================================================================

    #[test]
    fn test_gender_bifurcation_male_matches_male_vectors() {
        let profiler = ProfilingEngine::default();

        // Mock male user voice embedding
        let male_user_tone = [0.5f32; 512];

        // North Star with gender-specific vectors
        let north_star = NorthStarReferenceSet {
            archetype_id: ArchetypeId(1),
            semantic: [0.1; 768],
            tone_male: [0.5; 512],     // Close to male user
            tone_female: [-0.5; 512],  // Far from male user
            emotion: [0.1; 1024],
            emotion_male: [0.2; 1024],
            emotion_female: [-0.2; 1024],
            style: 0.5,
            action: [0.1; 42],
            chronemic: [0.0; 4],
        };

        // Calculate distances for male and female
        let male_dist = 1.0 - cosine_similarity_512(&male_user_tone, &north_star.tone_male);
        let female_dist = 1.0 - cosine_similarity_512(&male_user_tone, &north_star.tone_female);

        assert!(male_dist < female_dist,
            "Male user MUST be closer to male reference vectors, male_dist={}, female_dist={}",
            male_dist, female_dist);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_gender_persistence_in_profile_snapshot() {
        let snapshot = ProfileSnapshot {
            semantic_vector: [0.0; 768],
            tone_vector: [0.0; 512],
            emotion_vector: [0.0; 1024],
            style_score: 0.5,
            action_logits: [0.0; 42],
            chronemics: [0.0; 4],
            archetype: ArchetypeId(1),
            vak_modality: VakType::Visual,
            gender: Gender::Female,
            turn_number: 5,
            timestamp: chrono::Utc::now(),
        };

        // Gender should be retained in snapshot
        assert_eq!(snapshot.gender, Gender::Female);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_gender_majority_voting_60_40_split() {
        let profiler = ProfilingEngine::default();

        // 60% male, 40% female votes
        let gender_votes = vec![
            Gender::Male, Gender::Male, Gender::Male,
            Gender::Male, Gender::Male, Gender::Male,  // 6 male
            Gender::Female, Gender::Female, Gender::Female, Gender::Female,  // 4 female
        ];

        let consensus = profiler.calculate_consensus_gender(&gender_votes);

        assert_eq!(consensus, Gender::Male,
            "60% Male votes MUST result in Male consensus");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_gender_majority_voting_tie_defaults_to_male() {
        let profiler = ProfilingEngine::default();

        // 50% male, 50% female votes (tie)
        let gender_votes = vec![
            Gender::Male, Gender::Male, Gender::Male,
            Gender::Female, Gender::Female, Gender::Female,
        ];

        let consensus = profiler.calculate_consensus_gender(&gender_votes);

        assert_eq!(consensus, Gender::Male,
            "Tie MUST default to Male consensus");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_reference_set_has_nonzero_gender_vectors() {
        // Load reference sets file
        let reference_sets = load_north_star_reference_sets();

        for (id, north_star) in reference_sets.iter() {
            // Verify tone_male is non-zero
            let tone_male_sum: f32 = north_star.tone_male.iter().map(|x| x.abs()).sum();
            assert!(tone_male_sum > 0.0,
                "Archetype {} has zero tone_male vector", id);

            // Verify tone_female is non-zero
            let tone_female_sum: f32 = north_star.tone_female.iter().map(|x| x.abs()).sum();
            assert!(tone_female_sum > 0.0,
                "Archetype {} has zero tone_female vector", id);

            // Verify emotion_male is non-zero
            let emo_male_sum: f32 = north_star.emotion_male.iter().map(|x| x.abs()).sum();
            assert!(emo_male_sum > 0.0,
                "Archetype {} has zero emotion_male vector", id);

            // Verify emotion_female is non-zero
            let emo_female_sum: f32 = north_star.emotion_female.iter().map(|x| x.abs()).sum();
            assert!(emo_female_sum > 0.0,
                "Archetype {} has zero emotion_female vector", id);
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_safe_harbor_buffer_accumulates_gender_votes() {
        let mut buffer = SafeHarborBuffer::new();

        let state1 = CognitiveState {
            detected_gender: Gender::Male,
            ..CognitiveState::default()
        };
        let state2 = CognitiveState {
            detected_gender: Gender::Female,
            ..CognitiveState::default()
        };
        let state3 = CognitiveState {
            detected_gender: Gender::Male,
            ..CognitiveState::default()
        };

        buffer.accumulate(&state1);
        buffer.accumulate(&state2);
        buffer.accumulate(&state3);

        assert_eq!(buffer.gender_votes.len(), 3);
        assert_eq!(buffer.gender_votes[0], Gender::Male);
        assert_eq!(buffer.gender_votes[1], Gender::Female);
        assert_eq!(buffer.gender_votes[2], Gender::Male);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_hydrate_from_history_populates_gender_votes() {
        let mut buffer = SafeHarborBuffer::new();

        let historical = ProfileSnapshot {
            semantic_vector: [0.0; 768],
            tone_vector: [0.0; 512],
            emotion_vector: [0.0; 1024],
            style_score: 0.5,
            action_logits: [0.0; 42],
            chronemics: [0.0; 4],
            archetype: ArchetypeId(1),
            vak_modality: VakType::Visual,
            gender: Gender::Female,
            turn_number: 10,
            timestamp: chrono::Utc::now(),
        };

        buffer.hydrate_from_history(&historical);

        // Should have 3 gender votes (all Female from historical)
        assert_eq!(buffer.gender_votes.len(), 3);
        assert!(buffer.gender_votes.iter().all(|&g| g == Gender::Female));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_no_vector_addition() {
        // This test ensures we're using parallel streams, not vector fusion
        let semantic: [f32; 768] = [0.0; 768];
        let emotion: [f32; 1024] = [0.0; 1024];
        let identity: [f32; 512] = [0.0; 512];
        let style: f32 = 0.5;
        let action: [f32; 42] = [0.0; 42];
        let chronemic: [f32; 4] = [0.0; 4];

        // These CANNOT be added - they are different types/dimensions
        // Compiler enforces this - vectors remain separate in CognitiveState
        let _state = CognitiveState {
            semantic_embedding: semantic,
            emotion_embedding: emotion,
            x_vector: identity,
            style_score: style,
            dialog_acts: action,
            chronemics: chronemic,
            // ... other fields
            intent_id: String::new(),
            semantic_coherence: 0.0,
            vak_keywords: VakKeywordCounts::default(),
            user_id: String::new(),
            identity_verified: false,
            identity_similarity: 0.0,
            primary_archetype: ArchetypeId(0),
            secondary_archetype: ArchetypeId(1),
            arousal: 0.0,
            dominance: 0.0,
            valence: 0.0,
            w_e: 1.0,
            safety_stop: false,
            top_dialog_act: DialogActType::Inform,
            is_directive: false,
            normalized_pace: 0.0,
            silence_entropy: 0.0,
            aggression_score: 0.0,
            vak_modality: VakType::Visual,
            timestamp_ms: 0,
            locale: "en-US".to_string(),
        };
    }
}

## 17. Glossary

| Term | Definition |
|:-----|:-----------|
| AgentDB | Short-term reasoning and RL transition storage |
| Anti-Pattern | Failed strategy stored in RuVector with is_antipattern=true |
| Archetype | One of 49 Hogshead personality profiles |
| **5-Vector Combination** | The array of 5 independent vectors (Semantic, Tone, Emotion, Style, Action) used to define a user's position or an Archetype's reference point. No centroid is calculated. |
| **North Star Reference Set** | The collection of 5 reference vectors that define a specific Archetype across the 5 independent embedding spaces (hogshead_reference_vectors.bin) |
| CognitiveState | Unified struct from parallel hexa-modal analysis |
| Coherence | Measure of alignment between AI and user |
| Context Serialization | Converting CognitiveState to text for LLM input |
| Cypher | Graph query language used by RuVector via db.query() |
| Discovery Phase | First 60 seconds with Gamma = 0.1 |
| Entropy | Measure of confusion or novelty in communication |
| Identity Lock | Voice fingerprint verified at > 0.97 similarity |
| LanceDB | Voice identity and profile history storage (hexa-modal profile snapshots, append-only) |
| Mean Voice Vector | Average of accumulated WavLM X-Vectors over 60s, used for archetype classification |
| Nomic Prefix | Required prefix for embedding quality (search_query: or search_document:) |
| North Star Reference Vector | The specific vector within a Reference Set that applies to a single embedding space. E.g., The "Power Archetype Semantic Reference Vector" is the ruler for the Semantic space only. |
| Parallel Streams | Six concurrent extraction pipelines (A, B, C, D, E, F) |
| Post-Session Pruning | Strategy cleanup that occurs ONLY after session ends |
| RuVector | GNN-enabled strategy graph storage with Cypher queries (768-dim semantic) |
| Safe Harbor | Discovery phase with hardcoded Gamma = 0.1 |
| Safety Stop | Triggered when Valence < 0.3 AND Arousal > 0.7 |
| Tone | Archetype Signal - behavioral fingerprint derived from Mean Voice Vector |
| Hexa-Modal | Six input modalities processed in parallel (Semantic, Tone, Emotion, Style, Action, Chronemic) |
| VAD | Voice Activity Detection for speech-only extraction (MANDATORY for 0.97 Composite Score) |
| w_e | Emotional weight for physics equation, calculated from Valence/Arousal scalars (NOT 1024-dim vector) |
| X-Vector | 512-dim identity embedding from WavLM |
| Holographic Execution | A "Full-Sense" recording (Hexa-modal) of a successful turn stored in LanceDB |
| Ghost Replay | The process of using a Holographic Execution to instruct the AI to mimic a past winning performance |
| Prescience Engine | GPU-based MCTS simulation (Green Context C) that predicts conversation trajectories in vector space using 10,000+ parallel simulations |
| Expected Value (EV) | The calculated probability of success for a strategy based on Prescience simulation |
| Dual-Write | Storage operation that writes both Logic (RuVector) and Hologram (LanceDB) atomically |
| MCTS | Monte Carlo Tree Search - algorithm used by Prescience Engine on GPU Green Context C to simulate future states |
| **Green Contexts** | CUDA 13.1 feature allowing spatial partitioning of the RTX 5090 into isolated "hardware lanes" with guaranteed QoS. Context A (10% SMs) handles Audio/DSP, Context B (30% SMs) handles Embedding inference via Grouped GEMM, Context C (60% SMs) handles LLM and Prescience. |
| **CUDA Tile** | Programming model for authoring tile-based kernels (Tile IR) that abstract away thread management for DSP operations. Used by Trust Voice Processor for zero-latency audio processing directly in GPU SRAM. |
| **Grouped GEMM** | cuBLAS feature allowing multiple matrix multiplications of different shapes/weights to be fused into a single kernel launch. Used to batch Streams A-E inference for 4x throughput increase. |
| **FP8** | 8-bit Floating Point precision natively supported by Blackwell Tensor Cores for 2x throughput compared to FP16. Used for Qwen 3 14B inference. |
| **cuFFT DX** | CUDA FFT Device Extensions optimized for small power-of-2 sizes. Used for 4096-point FFTs enabling medical-grade micro-tremor detection in real-time on Green Context A. |
| Priming | The technique of influencing LLM vocabulary selection via System Prompt Injection to increase the density of specific persuasive words (e.g., "certainly", "agreed"). Implemented via `PrimingController` which generates prompt injection strings and validates response density. |
| Priming Density | The ratio of priming words to total words in a generated response. Validation threshold is 0.03 (3%) during first 120 seconds of conversation. |
| Prompt Injection | The mechanism by which priming guidance is inserted into the System Prompt before LLM generation. |
| **Instruct Mode** | A Qwen 3 inference mode that outputs standard instruction-following responses without internal reasoning tokens. Used during the Real-Time Loop to minimize latency and ensure strict <50ms response compliance. |
| **Thinking Mode** | A Qwen 3 inference mode that outputs internal reasoning tokens (Chain-of-Thought) before the final response. Used during offline Oneiric Engine dreaming simulations for deep reasoning and generating high-quality synthetic strategies ("Vaccine Nodes"). |
| **Qwen 3 14B FP8** | The primary LLM used for response generation. Supports dual-mode inference (Instruct/Thinking) and is optimized for RTX 5090 Blackwell FP8 Tensor Cores with ~15GB VRAM footprint. |
| **Cognitive Resonance (CRM)** | The calculated synchronization state R(t) between Operator and Counterpart based on Prosody, Semantics, and Rhythm. Used to trigger the Close Window. |
| **Resonance Equation** | R(t) = (P(t) × S(t) × C(t)) / σ(t). Defines the mathematical condition for maximum receptivity. |
| **P(t)** | Prosodic Alignment score derived from Stream B. Cross-correlation of F0 contours between Operator and Counterpart. |
| **S(t)** | Semantic Coherence to Goal score derived from Stream A. Cosine similarity between Counterpart utterance and current Milestone embedding. |
| **C(t)** | Chrono-Rhythmic Sync score derived from Stream F. Phase alignment of syllable timing calculated as inverse of jitter. |
| **Close Window** | The timeframe where R(t) > 0.82 and all component thresholds are exceeded, triggering a forceful attempt to resolve the conversation goal via strategy override to CLOSING type. |
| **σ(t)** | Noise/Uncertainty factor in the Resonance Equation. Derived from biometric dissonance (Stream B extension). Higher values reduce R(t). |
| **Temporal Archetype Drift (TAD)** | A metric tracking the rate of change in a user's psychological position. Specifically monitors the velocity of movement toward "Receptive" archetypes (Trust, Passion). |
| **Drift Velocity** | The calculated speed of psychological shift. Formula: Σ(w_i × (Distance_t-1 - Distance_t)). Positive values indicate warming rapport (user moving closer to Trust/Passion); negative values indicate cooling/withdrawal. |
| **Receptivity Window** | A specific timeframe where Drift Velocity exceeds the configured threshold (default > 0.05), indicating the user is rapidly becoming receptive. Acts as a force-override to trigger the "Close Window" strategy, independent of static CRM thresholds. |
| **LFM** | Leapable Frequency Modulation. A DSP technique injecting 17-21Hz harmonic glides at -18dB to stimulate parasympathetic calm during closing. |
| **VPCE** | Voice Phase Coherence Engine. Maintains phase-locking between synthetic voice and user speech to create unconscious rapport. |
| **Phase Coherence ($\Phi$)** | Coefficient $|⟨e^{i\theta_{AI}} \times e^{-i\theta_{recipient}}⟩|$ measuring the alignment of speech envelopes. |
| **Micro-timing Adjustment** | A latency shift of $\pm 50ms$ applied to TTS output onset to align with the user's rhythmic phase. |
| **PLL** | Phase-Locked Loop. A control system implemented in CUDA Tile IR to synchronize the frequency/phase of the TTS generator with the user's input signal. |

## 19. Required Data Files

The following files MUST exist before system startup:

| File Path | Description | Action if Missing |
|:----------|:------------|:------------------|
| `./data/profiles/hogshead_reference_vectors.bin` | 49 pre-computed Reference Sets (arrays of vectors, one per embedding space) | PANIC at startup |
| `./data/profiles/base_psychology.toml` | L0 psychology configuration | PANIC at startup |
| `./config/cognitive_physics.toml` | System configuration including cultural norms | PANIC at startup |
| `./data/strategy/ruvector.db` | RuVector database (created if missing) | Initialize empty |
| `./data/identity/voice_identities.lance` | LanceDB identity storage (created if missing) | Initialize empty |
| `./data/memory/agent.db` | AgentDB reasoning storage (created if missing) | Initialize empty |
| `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/nomic-embed-text-v1` | Nomic Embed Text v1 (768-dim) | PANIC at startup |
| `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/wavlm-base-plus-sv` | WavLM Base Plus SV (512-dim) | PANIC at startup |
| `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/wav2vec2-emotion` | Wav2Vec2 Emotion (1024-dim) | PANIC at startup |
| `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/roberta-formality` | RoBERTa Formality Classifier | PANIC at startup |
| `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/bert-dialog-act` | BERT Dialog Act Classifier (42 classes) | PANIC at startup |
| `/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/qwen3-14b-fp8-instruct.safetensors` | Qwen 3 14B FP8 | PANIC at startup |

**REQ-FILES-001: Startup Validation**

```rust
use std::path::Path;

/// Validate all required files exist at startup
///
/// CRITICAL: Panics if any required file is missing
/// This is intentional - system cannot function without these files
pub fn validate_required_files() {
    let required_panic_files = [
        // Configuration and reference sets
        "./data/profiles/hogshead_reference_vectors.bin",
        "./data/profiles/base_psychology.toml",
        "./config/cognitive_physics.toml",

        // Models
        "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/nomic-embed-text-v1",
        "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/wavlm-base-plus-sv",
        "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/wav2vec2-emotion",
        "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/roberta-formality",
        "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/bert-dialog-act",
        "/home/cabdru/leapable/src/models/qwen3-14b-fp8-instruct.safetensors",
    ];

    for path in required_panic_files {
        if !Path::new(path).exists() {
            panic!("FATAL: Required file not found: {}", path);
        }
    }

    // Optional files - initialize if missing
    let optional_initialize_files = [
        ("./data/strategy/ruvector.db", "RuVector"),
        ("./data/identity/voice_identities.lance", "LanceDB"),
        ("./data/memory/agent.db", "AgentDB"),
    ];

    for (path, name) in optional_initialize_files {
        if !Path::new(path).exists() {
            println!("INFO: {} database not found at {}. Will initialize empty.", name, path);
        }
    }
}
```

### 19.1 System Bootstrap Sequence

**REQ-BOOT-001: Application Startup Order**

The main binary MUST execute the following bootstrap sequence in order. Each step depends on the previous step completing successfully.

| Order | Step | Component | Failure Behavior |
|:------|:-----|:----------|:-----------------|
| 1 | Validate Files | `validate_required_files()` | PANIC if missing |
| 2 | Load Config | `Config::load()` | PANIC if invalid |
| 3 | Initialize Models | `ModelRegistry::new()` | PANIC if model load fails |
| 4 | Initialize Memory | `MemorySystem::new()` | PANIC if database init fails |
| 5 | **Ingest Teleology** | `ingest_teleology_config()` | PANIC if ingestion fails |
| 6 | Initialize Physics | `PhysicsEngine::new()` | PANIC if init fails |
| 7 | Initialize Profiling | `ProfilingEngine::new()` | PANIC if reference sets missing |
| 8 | Start API Server | `ApiServer::start()` | PANIC if port unavailable |

**REQ-BOOT-002: Teleology Ingestion at Startup**

The system MUST ingest the Teleology configuration into RuVector before accepting any session connections. This ensures the decision graph contains all GoalNodes and MilestoneNodes required for goal-directed behavior.

```rust
use config::Config;
use memory::MemorySystem;
use models::ModelRegistry;
use physics::PhysicsEngine;
use profiling::ProfilingEngine;
use api::ApiServer;
use audio::AudioEngine;
use analyzer::CognitiveAnalyzer;

/// Main application entry point
///
/// Executes the bootstrap sequence and starts the cognitive radar system.
/// CRITICAL: All initialization steps must complete before accepting connections.
#[tokio::main]
async fn main() -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {
    // STEP 1: Validate required files exist
    println!("BOOT: Validating required files...");
    validate_required_files();

    // STEP 2: Load configuration from TOML
    println!("BOOT: Loading configuration...");
    let config = Config::load("./config/cognitive_physics.toml")?;

    // STEP 3: Initialize ML models
    // This loads Nomic, WavLM, Wav2Vec2, RoBERTa, BERT, and Qwen 3 14B FP8
    println!("BOOT: Initializing ML models...");
    let models = ModelRegistry::new(&config.models).await?;

    // STEP 4: Initialize Memory System (RuVector, LanceDB, AgentDB)
    println!("BOOT: Initializing memory system...");
    let memory = MemorySystem::new().await?;

    // STEP 5: CRITICAL - Ingest Teleology Configuration into RuVector
    // This ensures the decision graph matches the business rules defined in TOML
    // Must happen BEFORE any session processing begins
    println!("BOOT: Ingesting Teleology configuration into RuVector...");
    memory.strategy.ingest_teleology_config(
        &config.teleology,
        &models.nomic,
    ).await?;
    println!("BOOT: Teleology ingestion complete. Goal: '{}' with {} milestones.",
        config.teleology.active_goal.name,
        config.teleology.active_goal.milestones.len()
    );

    // STEP 6: Initialize Physics Engine (includes Prescience Engine)
    println!("BOOT: Initializing physics engine...");
    let physics = PhysicsEngine::new(&config.physics, &config.cultural_norms)?;

    // STEP 7: Initialize Profiling Engine (loads North Star Reference Sets)
    println!("BOOT: Initializing profiling engine...");
    let profiling = ProfilingEngine::new(
        "./data/profiles/hogshead_reference_vectors.bin",
        "./data/profiles/base_psychology.toml",
    )?;

    // STEP 8: Initialize Cognitive Analyzer (parallel stream processing)
    println!("BOOT: Initializing cognitive analyzer...");
    let analyzer = CognitiveAnalyzer::new(&models)?;

    // STEP 9: Initialize Audio Engine
    println!("BOOT: Initializing audio engine...");
    let audio = AudioEngine::new(&config.audio)?;

    // STEP 10: Start API Server
    println!("BOOT: Starting API server on {}:{}...", config.api.host, config.api.port);
    let server = ApiServer::new(
        memory,
        models,
        physics,
        profiling,
        analyzer,
        audio,
        config,
    );

    println!("BOOT: System ready. Accepting connections.");
    server.start().await?;

    Ok(())
}
```

**REQ-BOOT-003: Graceful Shutdown**

On SIGTERM or SIGINT, the system MUST:

1. Stop accepting new connections
2. Complete in-progress turns (max 5 second timeout)
3. Run post-session cleanup for active sessions
4. Flush memory buffers to disk
5. Exit cleanly

```rust
impl ApiServer {
    /// Handle graceful shutdown
    ///
    /// Called on SIGTERM/SIGINT to ensure clean termination.
    pub async fn shutdown(&self) -> Result<(), ShutdownError> {
        println!("SHUTDOWN: Signal received, initiating graceful shutdown...");

        // 1. Stop accepting new connections
        self.stop_accepting().await;

        // 2. Wait for in-progress turns (max 5 seconds)
        let active_sessions = self.get_active_sessions().await;
        println!("SHUTDOWN: Waiting for {} active sessions...", active_sessions.len());

        tokio::time::timeout(
            std::time::Duration::from_secs(5),
            self.wait_for_sessions(&active_sessions),
        ).await.ok();

        // 3. Run post-session cleanup
        for session in &active_sessions {
            if let Err(e) = on_session_end(session, &self.memory).await {
                eprintln!("SHUTDOWN: Error cleaning up session {}: {}", session.id, e);
            }
        }

        // 4. Flush memory buffers
        println!("SHUTDOWN: Flushing memory buffers...");
        self.memory.flush().await?;

        println!("SHUTDOWN: Clean shutdown complete.");
        Ok(())
    }
}
```

## 20. Frontend & Human-in-the-Loop Specifications

This section defines the requirements for the Cognitive Command Center (Frontend UI) and the Human-in-the-Loop (HITL) workflows that enable operator oversight and RL learning correction.

### 20.1 The Cognitive Command Center (UI)

The Frontend acts as the control plane for the Cognitive Radar. It visualizes system state and issues overrides. The Frontend does NOT process heavy physics logic—all computation occurs on the backend.

**REQ-UI-001: The Hexa-Modal Cockpit (Real-Time Dashboard)**

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Theme** | Dark mode, high-contrast data-ink visualization |
| **Framework** | React with Tauri for native desktop deployment |
| **Data Source** | WebSocket connection to `cognitive-bridge` crate |
| **Refresh Rate** | 60Hz for stream telemetry, 1Hz for trajectory updates |

**HUD Components:**

| Component ID | Name | Description |
|:-------------|:-----|:------------|
| **HUD-001** | **Identity Ring** | Visual indicator of voice identity verification status |
| **HUD-002** | **Safety Gauge** | Bi-axial chart (Valence vs Arousal) with danger zone highlighting |
| **HUD-003** | **Manual Takeover** | Emergency intervention button ("Big Red Button") |
| **HUD-004** | **Stream Monitor** | 6 vertical bars indicating health of each analysis stream |
| **HUD-005** | **Johari Scope** | 2D Scatter Plot of Entropy (X) vs Coherence (Y). Visualizes the "Learning Zone" trajectory. |
| **HUD-006** | **Phase Meter** | Radial gauge showing cos φ (Phase Alignment). Green=Sync (1.0), Red=Desync (-1.0). |
| **HUD-007** | **Resonance & Drift Monitor** | Real-time graph of R(t). Overlay: Drift Velocity trend line. Flashes **GOLD** when R(t) > 0.82 (standard CRM trigger). Flashes **PLATINUM** when `is_receptivity_window` is TRUE (TAD Trigger), indicating rapid psychological warming independent of static thresholds. Shows P, S, C sub-bars below the main score. |

**Identity Ring States:**

| State | Color | Condition |
|:------|:------|:----------|
| **Verified** | Green | Identity similarity > 0.97 |
| **Uncertain** | Yellow | Identity similarity < 0.97 but > 0.85 |
| **Mismatch** | Red | Identity similarity < 0.85 or voice fingerprint changed mid-session |

**Safety Gauge Quadrants:**

| Quadrant | Valence | Arousal | Interpretation |
|:---------|:--------|:--------|:---------------|
| **Top-Right** | Positive | High | Excited/Happy (Safe) |
| **Top-Left** | Negative | High | Angry/Frustrated (DANGER ZONE) |
| **Bottom-Right** | Positive | Low | Calm/Content (Safe) |
| **Bottom-Left** | Negative | Low | Sad/Disengaged (Monitor) |

**Manual Takeover Behavior:**

| Step | Action |
|:-----|:-------|
| **1** | Send `StopGeneration` signal to backend via WebSocket |
| **2** | Enable Operator Microphone for live intervention |
| **3** | Tag timestamp in AgentDB as `CRITICAL_FAILURE` |
| **4** | Log event for post-session analysis |

**Stream Monitor States:**

| State | Visual | Meaning |
|:------|:-------|:--------|
| **Active** | Green bar | Stream processing normally |
| **Degraded** | Yellow bar | Stream latency > 100ms |
| **Failed** | Grey bar | Stream sensor failed (e.g., VAD silence, model timeout) |

---

**REQ-UI-002: The Cognitive Universe (3D Visualization)**

Interactive 3D visualization of the embedding space showing user trajectory relative to North Star strategies.

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Method** | Client-side UMAP or t-SNE projection of 768-dim vectors into 3D space |
| **Library** | Three.js or React Three Fiber |
| **Update Rate** | 1Hz for trajectory updates |

**Visual Elements:**

| Element | Appearance | Description |
|:--------|:-----------|:------------|
| **Static Galaxy** | Faint white points | Pre-computed North Star strategy positions |
| **User Comet** | Glowing trail with color gradient | User's semantic trajectory history (last 30 turns) |
| **AI Magnet** | Pulsing beacon | Currently selected Strategy target position |
| **Anti-Pattern Zones** | Red fog regions | Areas near known anti-patterns (avoidance regions) |

**View Filters:**

| Filter ID | Name | Shows |
|:----------|:-----|:------|
| **VIEW-001** | Semantic Space | Nomic 768-dim embeddings (intent/topic) |
| **VIEW-002** | Tone Space | WavLM 512-dim embeddings (voice characteristics) |
| **VIEW-003** | Emotion Space | Wav2Vec2 1024-dim embeddings (emotional state) |

---

**REQ-UI-003: The North Star Architect (Strategy Graph Editor)**

Node-based visual editor for viewing and creating conversation strategies.

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Interface Style** | Node-based editor (similar to Unreal Blueprint or Node-RED) |
| **Library** | React Flow or similar node graph library |
| **Access Control** | L0 psychology nodes are read-only unless "Admin Unlock" is toggled |

**Functionality:**

| Feature | Description |
|:--------|:------------|
| **Visual Graph** | Display IntentNode → Strategy → Outcome relationships from RuVector |
| **Drag-and-Drop Linking** | Manually link Strategies to IntentNodes |
| **Natural Language Injection** | Text input field where operator types a strategy description |
| **Anti-Pattern Markers** | Visual indicator (red border) for strategies marked as `is_antipattern=true` |

**Natural Language Injection Workflow:**

| Step | Action | Backend Effect |
|:-----|:-------|:---------------|
| **1** | Operator types strategy text (e.g., "Use humor to diffuse tension") | — |
| **2** | Click "Create Strategy" button | Send text to backend |
| **3** | Backend embeds via Nomic (768-dim) | `nomic_embedding` generated |
| **4** | Backend creates Strategy node with `origin: HUMAN_INJECTED` | Node stored in RuVector |
| **5** | UI updates to show new node in graph | Real-time sync via WebSocket |

---

### 20.2 Frontend Communication Layer

**REQ-ARCH-004: Frontend Real-Time Bridge**

The system exposes a WebSocket server via the `cognitive-bridge` crate to power the Hexa-Modal Cockpit.

| Data Type | Direction | Frequency | Payload Description |
|:----------|:----------|:----------|:--------------------|
| **Stream Telemetry** | Server → Client | 60Hz | Hexa-modal output (Valence, Arousal, Entropy, Identity similarity) |
| **Trajectory Update** | Server → Client | 1Hz | Reduced dimension coordinates for UMAP visualization |
| **Critical Alerts** | Server → Client | Event-Driven | Safety Stop triggers, Identity Mismatch warnings |
| **Manual Takeover** | Client → Server | Event-Driven | Stop TTS, enable operator microphone |
| **Archetype Override** | Client → Server | Event-Driven | Operator manually selects correct archetype |
| **Strategy Injection** | Client → Server | Event-Driven | New strategy text for embedding and storage |

**WebSocket Message Schema:**

```rust
/// Messages sent from Backend to Frontend
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub enum BackendMessage {
    /// 60Hz telemetry update with UTL Physics data AND Cognitive Resonance Mapping
    Telemetry {
        valence: f32,
        arousal: f32,
        entropy: f32,              // Delta S (Change in novelty/uncertainty)
        coherence: f32,            // Delta C (Change in integration/sense-making)
        phase_cosine: f32,         // cos φ (Phase alignment: 1.0=Sync, -1.0=Desync)
        learning_power: f32,       // L (UTL Learning Power: 0.0 to 1.0)
        utl_loss: f32,             // J (UTL Total Loss - optimization target)

        // Cognitive Resonance Mapping (CRM) Fields
        resonance_score: f32,      // R(t) - Combined resonance score
        prosodic_alignment: f32,   // P(t) - Prosodic alignment component
        semantic_goal_coherence: f32, // S(t) - Semantic goal coherence component
        chrono_sync: f32,          // C(t) - Chrono-rhythmic sync component
        resonance_trigger: bool,   // Is Close Window Open? (R(t) > 0.82 + thresholds OR TAD)

        // Temporal Archetype Drift (TAD) Fields
        drift_velocity: f32,       // Rate of psychological shift toward Trust/Passion
                                   // Positive = warming up; Negative = cooling off
        is_receptivity_window: bool, // Is the user in a TAD-triggered Receptivity Window?
                                     // True when drift_velocity > threshold (default 0.05)

        identity_similarity: f32,
        stream_health: [StreamHealth; 6],
    },
    /// 1Hz trajectory update for 3D visualization
    Trajectory {
        user_position: [f32; 3],
        strategy_position: [f32; 3],
        trail_points: Vec<[f32; 3]>,
    },
    /// Event-driven critical alert
    Alert {
        alert_type: AlertType,
        message: String,
        timestamp: chrono::DateTime<chrono::Utc>,
    },
}

/// Messages sent from Frontend to Backend
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub enum FrontendMessage {
    /// Emergency stop
    ManualTakeover { operator_id: String },
    /// Override detected archetype
    ArchetypeOverride { archetype: ArchetypeId },
    /// Inject new strategy via North Star Architect
    InjectStrategy { text: String, target_archetype: ArchetypeId, vak_modality: VakType },
    /// Apply HITL vote to past transition
    ApplyHumanVote { session_id: String, turn: u32, vote: HumanVote },
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub enum StreamHealth {
    Active,
    Degraded,
    Failed,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub enum AlertType {
    SafetyStop,
    IdentityMismatch,
    HighArousalWarning,
    StreamFailure { stream_index: u8 },
}
```

---

### 20.3 Human-in-the-Loop (HITL) Workflows

**REQ-HITL-001: The Shadow Slot (Post-Session Review)**

Post-session review mechanism for human operators to reinforce or correct AI learning.

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Trigger** | Session End event |
| **Selection Criteria** | Turns where \|reward\| > 0.7 (high-impact moments) |
| **Interface** | "Replay Reel" showing turn transcript, AI action, and calculated reward |

**Operator Voting Options:**

| Vote | Label | Effect on RuVector | Reward Override |
|:-----|:------|:-------------------|:----------------|
| **Solidify** | Thumbs Up | Increases edge weight for the strategy | +1.0 |
| **Punish** | Thumbs Down | Marks StrategyNode as `is_antipattern=true` for this Intent context | -1.0 |
| **Correct** | Calibrate | AI outcome was acceptable, but internal reasoning weights were wrong | +0.5 |

**Shadow Slot UI Components:**

| Component | Description |
|:----------|:------------|
| **Turn Card** | Displays turn number, user transcript, AI response, calculated reward |
| **Reasoning Trace** | Shows AI's reasoning for the action taken |
| **Vote Buttons** | Three buttons: Solidify (green), Punish (red), Correct (yellow) |
| **Skip Button** | Skip this turn without voting |
| **Progress Bar** | Shows progress through all candidate turns |

---

**REQ-HITL-002: Live Archetype Calibration**

Real-time correction of archetype misclassification during active session.

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Trigger** | Operator observes AI misclassifying user archetype |
| **Interface** | Dropdown selector in Cockpit HUD |
| **Immediate Effect** | Overwrites `CognitiveState.primary_archetype` for active session |

**Backend Effects:**

| Step | Action |
|:-----|:-------|
| **1** | Receive `ArchetypeOverride` message via WebSocket |
| **2** | Update `session.locked_archetype` to operator-selected value |
| **3** | Update LanceDB profile snapshot at T=60s with manually corrected label |
| **4** | Log event: `HITL_ARCHETYPE_OVERRIDE` with old and new archetype IDs |

**Archetype Selector Options:**

The dropdown displays all 49 Hogshead archetypes grouped by primary advantage:
- Power (7 variants)
- Passion (7 variants)
- Mystique (7 variants)
- Prestige (7 variants)
- Trust (7 variants)
- Innovation (7 variants)
- Alert (7 variants)

---

**REQ-HITL-003: Semantic Drift Patching**

Mechanism to teach the system new vocabulary when it fails to match user terminology to known intents.

| Attribute | Specification |
|:----------|:--------------|
| **Trigger** | User uses slang/terminology AI fails to match to an Intent |
| **Interface** | Right-click context menu on transcript text |
| **Action** | Operator highlights phrase → selects "Link to Intent" → chooses Intent from list |

**Backend Effects:**

| Step | Action |
|:-----|:-------|
| **1** | Receive highlighted phrase and selected IntentNode ID |
| **2** | Embed phrase via Nomic (768-dim) |
| **3** | Create new `EntryNode` in RuVector pointing to selected Intent |
| **4** | Store with metadata: `source: HUMAN_PATCHED`, `original_phrase: "[text]"` |

**Entry Node Schema:**

```rust
/// A vocabulary entry that maps user language to an Intent
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub struct EntryNode {
    /// Unique identifier
    pub id: String,
    /// Original phrase from user transcript
    pub phrase: String,
    /// Nomic embedding of the phrase
    pub embedding: [f32; 768],
    /// Target IntentNode ID
    pub target_intent: String,
    /// How this entry was created
    pub source: EntrySource,
    /// Timestamp
    pub created_at: chrono::DateTime<chrono::Utc>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
pub enum EntrySource {
    /// Learned automatically from successful conversations
    Learned,
    /// Manually created by operator via Semantic Drift Patching
    HumanPatched,
}
```

---

### 20.4 UI Technology Stack

| Layer | Technology | Purpose |
|:------|:-----------|:--------|
| **Framework** | React 18+ with TypeScript | Component-based UI development |
| **Desktop Wrapper** | Tauri 2.0 | Native desktop application with Rust backend integration |
| **State Management** | Zustand or Jotai | Lightweight reactive state |
| **3D Visualization** | React Three Fiber + Three.js | Cognitive Universe rendering |
| **Node Graph** | React Flow | North Star Architect strategy editor |
| **Charts** | Recharts or Victory | Safety Gauge and Stream Monitor |
| **WebSocket** | Native WebSocket API | Real-time communication with cognitive-bridge |
| **Styling** | Tailwind CSS | Dark mode, high-contrast design system |
